function getLoadedSystemNodeCount(){
  const seen=new Set();
  const append=(items)=>{
    if(!Array.isArray(items)){return;}
    items.forEach((node)=>{
      if(node?.id){seen.add(node.id);}
    });
  };
  append(S.modelNodes);
  if(S.canvases&&typeof S.canvases==='object'){
    Object.values(S.canvases).forEach((canvas)=>append(canvas?.nodes));
  }
  return seen.size;
}

function canOpenFaultInjectionEntry(){
  return Boolean(S.sysLoaded&&getLoadedSystemNodeCount()>0);
}

// ─── UI 更新 ───
function updateUI(){
  [1,2,3].forEach(i=>{
    const el=document.getElementById('s'+i);
    const nm=document.getElementById('sn'+i);
    el.classList.remove('active','done');
    if(i<S.step){el.classList.add('done');nm.textContent='✓';}
    else if(i===S.step){el.classList.add('active');nm.textContent=i;}
    else nm.textContent=i;
  });

  const impFlt=document.getElementById('btn-imp-flt');
  const savSys=document.getElementById('btn-save-sys');
  const savRes=document.getElementById('btn-save-res');
  const setTopButtonReady=(button,ready)=>{
    if(!button){return;}
    button.classList.toggle('tbtn-disabled',!ready);
    button.classList.toggle('ready',!!ready);
    button.disabled=!ready;
    button.setAttribute('aria-disabled',ready?'false':'true');
  };

  setTopButtonReady(savSys,Boolean(S.sysLoaded));
  setTopButtonReady(impFlt,canOpenFaultInjectionEntry());
  setTopButtonReady(savRes,Boolean(S.simDone));

  let statusText='就绪 · 等待导入系统模型';
  if(S.sysLoaded && S.step===1){
    if(!S.modelNodes.length){
      statusText='系统建模中 · 请拖拽组件到画布';
    }else if(canInitializeSimulation()){
      statusText='系统建模中 · 当前链路已可运行，可直接初始化仿真';
    }else{
      statusText='系统建模中 · 单击模块后可在右侧保存设置';
    }
  }else if(S.step===2){
    statusText=hasSimulationFaults()
      ?'系统模型已保存 · 当前包含故障注入，可继续仿真分析'
      :'系统模型已保存 · 故障注入为可选，可直接初始化仿真';
  }else if(S.step===3){
    statusText=hasSimulationFaults()
      ?'故障配置完成 · 仿真分析'
      :'仿真分析阶段 · 当前为无故障基线仿真';
  }
  if(typeof SIM!=='undefined'){
    if(SIM.running&&!SIM.paused){
      statusText=`仿真运行中 · t = ${SIM.time.toFixed(2)}s / ${SIM.duration.toFixed(2)}s`;
    }else if(SIM.paused){
      statusText=`仿真已暂停 · t = ${SIM.time.toFixed(2)}s / ${SIM.duration.toFixed(2)}s`;
    }else if(SIM.hasSamples&&S.step===3){
      statusText=`仿真结果就绪 · ${SIM.datasetName} · 已采样 ${SIM.stepIndex} 步`;
    }
  }
  document.getElementById('stxt').textContent=statusText;
  const sd=document.getElementById('sdot');
  sd.className='sdot'+['','sdot-b','sdot-r','sdot-g'][S.step];
  document.getElementById('sblk').textContent=`组件: ${S.modelNodes.length} · 连线: ${S.modelEdges.length}`;
  document.getElementById('sflt').textContent=`故障模型: ${S.faultModels}`;
  updateSimbarEnabled();
}
// --- 基础工具 ---
function clamp(value,min,max){return Math.min(Math.max(value,min),max);}

function cloneDefaults(value){
  return JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(value));
}

function createEmptyCanvasRecord(id,name,parentSubsystemNodeId=null){
  return {
    id,
    name,
    parentSubsystemNodeId,
    viewport:{scale:1,offsetX:0,offsetY:0},
    nodes:[],
    edges:[]
  };
}

function ensureWorkbenchCanvasState(){
  if(!S.canvases||typeof S.canvases!=='object'){
    S.canvases={};
  }
  if(!S.canvases[S.rootCanvasId]){
    S.canvases[S.rootCanvasId]=createEmptyCanvasRecord(S.rootCanvasId,'顶层',null);
  }
  if(!S.activeCanvasId||!S.canvases[S.activeCanvasId]){
    S.activeCanvasId=S.rootCanvasId;
  }
  if(!Array.isArray(S.canvasTrail)||S.canvasTrail.length===0){
    S.canvasTrail=[S.rootCanvasId];
  }
  if(S.canvasTrail[0]!==S.rootCanvasId){
    S.canvasTrail=[S.rootCanvasId,...S.canvasTrail.filter(Boolean).filter(canvasId=>canvasId!==S.rootCanvasId)];
  }
  if(S.canvasTrail[S.canvasTrail.length-1]!==S.activeCanvasId){
    S.canvasTrail=[...S.canvasTrail.filter(Boolean),S.activeCanvasId];
  }
  if(!S.canvases[S.activeCanvasId]){
    S.canvases[S.activeCanvasId]=createEmptyCanvasRecord(
      S.activeCanvasId,
      S.activeCanvasId===S.rootCanvasId?'顶层':'未命名画布',
      null
    );
  }
}

function getCanvasRecord(canvasId=S.activeCanvasId){
  ensureWorkbenchCanvasState();
  return S.canvases[canvasId]||null;
}

function getActiveCanvasRecord(){
  return getCanvasRecord(S.activeCanvasId);
}

function syncActiveCanvasViewportFromState(){
  ensureWorkbenchCanvasState();
  const canvas=getActiveCanvasRecord();
  if(!canvas){return;}
  canvas.viewport={
    scale:S.canvasScale,
    offsetX:S.canvasOffsetX,
    offsetY:S.canvasOffsetY
  };
}

function restoreActiveCanvasViewport(canvasId=S.activeCanvasId){
  ensureWorkbenchCanvasState();
  const viewport=getCanvasRecord(canvasId)?.viewport||{};
  S.canvasScale=Number.isFinite(viewport.scale)?viewport.scale:1;
  S.canvasOffsetX=Number.isFinite(viewport.offsetX)?viewport.offsetX:0;
  S.canvasOffsetY=Number.isFinite(viewport.offsetY)?viewport.offsetY:0;
}

function setActiveCanvasRecord(canvasId,trail=null){
  ensureWorkbenchCanvasState();
  if(!S.canvases[canvasId]){
    return false;
  }
  syncActiveCanvasViewportFromState();
  S.activeCanvasId=canvasId;
  if(Array.isArray(trail)&&trail.length){
    const normalizedTrail=trail.filter(Boolean);
    if(normalizedTrail[0]!==S.rootCanvasId){
      normalizedTrail.unshift(S.rootCanvasId);
    }
    S.canvasTrail=normalizedTrail;
  }else{
    S.canvasTrail=canvasId===S.rootCanvasId?[S.rootCanvasId]:[S.rootCanvasId,canvasId];
  }
  restoreActiveCanvasViewport(canvasId);
  return true;
}

function getSubsystemCanvasId(nodeId){
  return `canvas-${nodeId}`;
}

function createSubsystemCanvas(node){
  const canvasId=getSubsystemCanvasId(node.id);
  if(!S.canvases[canvasId]){
    S.canvases[canvasId]=createEmptyCanvasRecord(canvasId,node.props?.name||'子系统',node.id);
  }
  node.targetCanvasId=canvasId;
  return S.canvases[canvasId];
}

function openCanvasRecord(canvasId,trail=null){
  if(!setActiveCanvasRecord(canvasId,trail)){
    return false;
  }
  S.selBlk=null;
  S.selEdge=null;
  clearPendingConnection();
  renderModelNodes();
  clampCanvasOffset();
  applyCanvasTransform();
  renderPropertyPanel(null);
  syncConfigTargets('');
  updateUI();
  return true;
}

function openSubsystemCanvas(nodeId){
  const node=getNode(nodeId);
  if(!node||node.type!=='subsystem_block'||!node.targetCanvasId){
    return false;
  }
  const trail=S.activeCanvasId===S.rootCanvasId
    ?[S.rootCanvasId,node.targetCanvasId]
    :[...S.canvasTrail.filter(Boolean),node.targetCanvasId];
  return openCanvasRecord(node.targetCanvasId,trail);
}

function goToRootCanvas(){
  return openCanvasRecord(S.rootCanvasId,[S.rootCanvasId]);
}

function navigateToCanvas(canvasId){
  const trailIndex=S.canvasTrail.indexOf(canvasId);
  if(trailIndex===-1){
    return false;
  }
  return openCanvasRecord(canvasId,S.canvasTrail.slice(0,trailIndex+1));
}

function renderCanvasBreadcrumbs(){
  const host=document.getElementById('canvas-breadcrumbs');
  if(!host){return;}
  ensureWorkbenchCanvasState();
  const trail=S.canvasTrail.filter(Boolean);
  host.innerHTML=trail.map((canvasId,index)=>{
    const canvas=getCanvasRecord(canvasId);
    const label=canvasId===S.rootCanvasId?'顶层':(canvas?.name||canvasId);
    const isLast=index===trail.length-1;
    return `
      <button type="button" class="canvas-breadcrumbs__item${isLast?' is-active':''}" data-canvas-id="${canvasId}" ${canvasId===S.rootCanvasId?'data-breadcrumb-root="true"':''} ${isLast?'aria-current="page"':''}>
        ${escapeHtml(label)}
      </button>
      ${!isLast?'<span class="canvas-breadcrumbs__sep">/</span>':''}`;
  }).join('');
  host.querySelectorAll('[data-canvas-id]').forEach(btn=>{
    btn.addEventListener('click',()=>{
      const canvasId=btn.dataset.canvasId||S.rootCanvasId;
      if(canvasId===S.activeCanvasId){return;}
      navigateToCanvas(canvasId);
    });
  });
}

function ensureSubsystemCanvasNode(node){
  if(!node||node.type!=='subsystem_block'){
    return null;
  }
  const canvas=createSubsystemCanvas(node);
  if(canvas&&canvas.parentSubsystemNodeId!==node.id){
    canvas.parentSubsystemNodeId=node.id;
  }
  return canvas;
}

Object.defineProperty(S,'modelNodes',{
  configurable:true,
  enumerable:true,
  get(){
    return getActiveCanvasRecord()?.nodes||[];
  },
  set(value){
    const canvas=getActiveCanvasRecord();
    if(canvas){
      canvas.nodes=Array.isArray(value)?value:[];
    }
  }
});

Object.defineProperty(S,'modelEdges',{
  configurable:true,
  enumerable:true,
  get(){
    return getActiveCanvasRecord()?.edges||[];
  },
  set(value){
    const canvas=getActiveCanvasRecord();
    if(canvas){
      canvas.edges=Array.isArray(value)?value:[];
    }
  }
});

ensureWorkbenchCanvasState();

const WORKBENCH_STORAGE_KEY='gz-workbench-system-model';

function getRuntimeListenerStore(){
  if(!window.__GZ_RUNTIME_LISTENERS__){
    window.__GZ_RUNTIME_LISTENERS__={};
  }
  return window.__GZ_RUNTIME_LISTENERS__;
}

function getWorkbenchSnapshotApi(){
  return window.__GZ_WORKBENCH_SNAPSHOT__||null;
}

function createSystemModelSnapshot(){
  const api=getWorkbenchSnapshotApi();
  return api?.createWorkbenchSnapshot?api.createWorkbenchSnapshot(S):cloneDefaults({
    version:1,
    modelNodes:S.modelNodes,
    modelEdges:S.modelEdges,
    nodeSeq:S.nodeSeq,
    edgeSeq:S.edgeSeq,
    rootCanvasId:S.rootCanvasId,
    activeCanvasId:S.activeCanvasId,
    canvasTrail:S.canvasTrail,
    canvases:S.canvases,
    activeLineType:S.activeLineType,
    faultedBlks:S.faultedBlks,
    importedFaultModels:S.importedFaultModels
  });
}

function restoreSystemModelSnapshot(snapshot){
  const api=getWorkbenchSnapshotApi();
  const restored=api?.restoreWorkbenchSnapshot?api.restoreWorkbenchSnapshot(snapshot):cloneDefaults(snapshot);
  S.canvases=restored.canvases||{};
  S.rootCanvasId=restored.rootCanvasId||'canvas-root';
  S.activeCanvasId=restored.activeCanvasId||S.rootCanvasId;
  S.canvasTrail=Array.isArray(restored.canvasTrail)&&restored.canvasTrail.length
    ?restored.canvasTrail
    :[S.rootCanvasId];
  ensureWorkbenchCanvasState();
  S.modelNodes=restored.modelNodes||[];
  S.modelEdges=restored.modelEdges||[];
  S.nodeSeq=restored.nodeSeq||0;
  S.edgeSeq=restored.edgeSeq||0;
  S.activeLineType=restored.activeLineType||'normal';
  S.workspaceSource=typeof restored.workspaceSource==='string'?restored.workspaceSource:(S.workspaceSource||'');
  S.faultedBlks=restored.faultedBlks||[];
  S.importedFaultModels=restored.importedFaultModels||[];
  S.faultModels=S.importedFaultModels.length;
  S.selBlk=null;
  S.selEdge=null;
  restoreActiveCanvasViewport(S.activeCanvasId);
  applyCanvasTransform();
  clearPendingConnection();
  renderCanvasBreadcrumbs();
  syncAllPythonInputConnectionState();
  renderModelNodes();
  renderPropertyPanel(null);
  setConnectionTool(S.activeLineType);
  syncConfigTargets('');
}

function escapeHtml(value){
  return String(value ?? '')
    .replace(/&/g,'&amp;')
    .replace(/</g,'&lt;')
    .replace(/>/g,'&gt;')
    .replace(/"/g,'&quot;')
    .replace(/'/g,'&#39;');
}

function clampInterfaceCount(value,[min,max]){
  const parsed=Number.parseInt(value,10);
  if(!Number.isFinite(parsed)){return min;}
  return clamp(parsed,min,max);
}

function normalizeSimulationInterfaceList(items,prefix,fallbackType,minCount=0){
  const base=Array.isArray(items)?items:[];
  const normalized=base
    .map((item,index)=>({
      name:String(item?.name||`${prefix} ${index+1}`).trim()||`${prefix} ${index+1}`,
      type:PORT_FORMATS.includes(item?.type)?item.type:(fallbackType||'标量')
    }))
    .filter(Boolean);
  while(normalized.length<minCount){
    normalized.push({
      name:`${prefix} ${normalized.length+1}`,
      type:fallbackType||'标量'
    });
  }
  return normalized;
}

function normalizeSimulationInterfaces(props){
  const inputFallback=PORT_FORMATS.includes(props?.inputFormat)?props.inputFormat:'标量';
  const outputFallback=PORT_FORMATS.includes(props?.outputFormat)?props.outputFormat:'标量';
  props.inputs=normalizeSimulationInterfaceList(props?.inputs,'输入',inputFallback,1);
  props.outputs=normalizeSimulationInterfaceList(props?.outputs,'输出',outputFallback,1);
  props.middleVars=normalizeSimulationInterfaceList(props?.middleVars,'中间量',outputFallback,0);
  if(!props.middleVars.length&&props?.inputFormat){
    props.middleVars=[{name:'中间量 1',type:outputFallback}];
  }
  if(!props.ffunctionNote){
    props.ffunctionNote='当前预留 Python 函数接口，可在后续导入函数定义。';
  }
  delete props.inputFormat;
  delete props.outputFormat;
  return props;
}

function getSimulationPortSets(props){
  normalizeSimulationInterfaces(props);
  return {
    inputs:props.inputs,
    outputs:props.outputs,
    middleVars:props.middleVars
  };
}

function getSimulationNodeSize(props){
  const groups=getSimulationPortSets(props);
  const leftCount=Math.max(groups.inputs.length,1);
  const rightCount=Math.max(groups.outputs.length,1);
  const topCount=groups.middleVars.length;
  const verticalDominant=Math.max(leftCount,rightCount);
  return {
    width:clamp(196+Math.max(0,topCount-2)*28,196,336),
    height:clamp(116+Math.max(0,verticalDominant-2)*22+(topCount?18:0),116,312)
  };
}

function applyNodeGeometry(node){
  if(!node){return;}
  if(node.type==='flow_block'&&isPythonBoundFlowBlock(node)){
    const size=getPythonBindingNodeSize(node);
    node.w=size.width;
    node.h=size.height;
  }else if(node.type==='simulation_block'){
    normalizeSimulationInterfaces(node.props);
    const size=getSimulationNodeSize(node.props);
    node.w=size.width;
    node.h=size.height;
  }else{
    const meta=COMPONENT_LIBRARY[node.type];
    if(meta){
      node.w=meta.width;
      node.h=meta.height;
    }
  }
  node.x=clamp(node.x,CANVAS_STAGE.nodePadding,CANVAS_STAGE.width-node.w-CANVAS_STAGE.nodePadding);
  node.y=clamp(node.y,CANVAS_STAGE.nodeMinY,CANVAS_STAGE.height-node.h-CANVAS_STAGE.nodePadding);
}

function pruneInvalidEdgesForNode(node){
  const ports=getNodePorts(node);
  const outputCount=ports.outputs.length;
  const inputCount=ports.inputs.length;
  const removed=S.modelEdges.filter(edge=>{
    if(edge.sourceNodeId===node.id&&(edge.sourcePortIndex||0)>=outputCount){return true;}
    if(edge.targetNodeId===node.id&&(edge.targetPortIndex||0)>=inputCount){return true;}
    return false;
  });
  if(!removed.length){return 0;}
  const removedIds=new Set(removed.map(edge=>edge.id));
  S.modelEdges=S.modelEdges.filter(edge=>!removedIds.has(edge.id));
  syncAllPythonInputConnectionState();
  if(S.selEdge&&removedIds.has(S.selEdge)){S.selEdge=null;}
  if(S.protocolInjectTargetId&&removedIds.has(S.protocolInjectTargetId)){
    S.protocolInjectTargetId='';
    S.protocolInjectSelectionMode='';
    S.protocolInjectSelectionId='';
  }
  return removed.length;
}

function getSimulationFlatOutputs(props){
  const groups=getSimulationPortSets(props);
  return [
    ...groups.outputs.map((item,index)=>({kind:'output',name:item.name,type:item.type,index,side:'right'})),
    ...groups.middleVars.map((item,index)=>({kind:'middle',name:item.name,type:item.type,index,side:'top'}))
  ];
}

function buildSimulationInterfaceRows(items,prefix){
  return items.map((item,index)=>`
    <div class="sim-intf-row" data-role="${prefix}" data-index="${index}">
      <div class="props-field">
        <label>${prefix}名称 ${index+1}</label>
        <input data-sim-field="name" value="${escapeHtml(item.name)}">
      </div>
      <div class="props-field">
        <label>${prefix}类型</label>
        <select data-sim-field="type">${buildSelectOptions(PORT_FORMATS,item.type)}</select>
      </div>
    </div>`).join('');
}

function buildSimulationBlockFields(node){
  normalizeSimulationInterfaces(node.props);
  return `
    <div class="pgroup">
      <div class="pglbl">仿真接口</div>
      <div class="props-field"><label>模块名称</label><input id="prop-name" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.name)}"></div>
      <div class="props-field"><label>模块类型</label><select id="prop-moduleType">${buildSelectOptions(SIM_MODULE_TYPES,node.props.moduleType)}</select></div>
      <div class="sim-intf-toolbar">
        <div class="sim-intf-counts">
          <div class="props-field"><label>输入数量</label><input id="sim-input-count" type="number" min="${SIM_INTERFACE_LIMITS.inputs[0]}" max="${SIM_INTERFACE_LIMITS.inputs[1]}" value="${node.props.inputs.length}"></div>
          <div class="props-field"><label>输出数量</label><input id="sim-output-count" type="number" min="${SIM_INTERFACE_LIMITS.outputs[0]}" max="${SIM_INTERFACE_LIMITS.outputs[1]}" value="${node.props.outputs.length}"></div>
          <div class="props-field"><label>中间变量数量</label><input id="sim-middle-count" type="number" min="${SIM_INTERFACE_LIMITS.middleVars[0]}" max="${SIM_INTERFACE_LIMITS.middleVars[1]}" value="${node.props.middleVars.length}"></div>
        </div>
        <button class="props-secondary" type="button" onclick="syncSimulationInterfaceCounts()">同步接口数量</button>
        <div class="sim-intf-note">中间变量当前位于模块上方，作为辅助观测端口使用；输入仍在左侧，主输出仍在右侧。</div>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div class="sim-intf-group">
      <div class="sim-intf-head">
        <div class="sim-intf-title">输入端口</div>
        <div class="sim-intf-meta">${node.props.inputs.length} 个左侧端口</div>
      </div>
      <div class="sim-intf-list">${buildSimulationInterfaceRows(node.props.inputs,'输入')}</div>
    </div>
    <div class="sim-intf-group">
      <div class="sim-intf-head">
        <div class="sim-intf-title">输出端口</div>
        <div class="sim-intf-meta">${node.props.outputs.length} 个右侧主输出</div>
      </div>
      <div class="sim-intf-list">${buildSimulationInterfaceRows(node.props.outputs,'输出')}</div>
    </div>
    <div class="sim-intf-group">
      <div class="sim-intf-head">
        <div class="sim-intf-title">中间变量</div>
        <div class="sim-intf-meta">${node.props.middleVars.length} 个顶部观测端口</div>
      </div>
      <div class="sim-intf-list">${node.props.middleVars.length?buildSimulationInterfaceRows(node.props.middleVars,'中间量'):'<div class="sim-intf-note">当前没有暴露的中间变量端口，可先调整数量后再同步。</div>'}</div>
    </div>
    <div class="props-field"><label>函数说明</label><textarea id="prop-ffunctionNote">${escapeHtml(node.props.ffunctionNote)}</textarea></div>
    <div class="props-help">后续这里会接入 Python 函数导入能力。当前版本先支持接口编排、端口连线和基础模块运行时。</div>`;
}

function readSimulationInterfaceRows(role){
  return [...document.querySelectorAll(`.sim-intf-row[data-role="${role}"]`)].map((row,index)=>({
    name:(row.querySelector('[data-sim-field="name"]')?.value||`${role} ${index+1}`).trim()||`${role} ${index+1}`,
    type:row.querySelector('[data-sim-field="type"]')?.value||'标量'
  }));
}

function syncSimulationInterfaceCounts(){
  const node=getNode(S.selBlk);
  if(!node||node.type!=='simulation_block'){return;}
  const nextProps=cloneDefaults(node.props);
  nextProps.inputs=readSimulationInterfaceRows('输入');
  nextProps.outputs=readSimulationInterfaceRows('输出');
  nextProps.middleVars=readSimulationInterfaceRows('中间量');
  normalizeSimulationInterfaces(nextProps);
  const inputCount=clampInterfaceCount(document.getElementById('sim-input-count')?.value,SIM_INTERFACE_LIMITS.inputs);
  const outputCount=clampInterfaceCount(document.getElementById('sim-output-count')?.value,SIM_INTERFACE_LIMITS.outputs);
  const middleCount=clampInterfaceCount(document.getElementById('sim-middle-count')?.value,SIM_INTERFACE_LIMITS.middleVars);
  nextProps.inputs=normalizeSimulationInterfaceList(nextProps.inputs.slice(0,inputCount),'输入',nextProps.inputs[0]?.type||'标量',inputCount);
  nextProps.outputs=normalizeSimulationInterfaceList(nextProps.outputs.slice(0,outputCount),'输出',nextProps.outputs[0]?.type||'标量',outputCount);
  nextProps.middleVars=normalizeSimulationInterfaceList(nextProps.middleVars.slice(0,middleCount),'中间量',nextProps.middleVars[0]?.type||'标量',middleCount);
  const preview={...node,props:nextProps};
  renderPropertyPanel(preview);
}

function isSubsystemBoundaryNodeType(type){
  return type==='subsystem_in_port'||type==='subsystem_out_port';
}

function normalizeSubsystemInterfaceList(items,prefix,minCount=0){
  const base=Array.isArray(items)?items:[];
  const normalized=base
    .map((item,index)=>({
      id:String(item?.id||`${prefix.toLowerCase()}-${index+1}`).trim()||`${prefix.toLowerCase()}-${index+1}`,
      name:String(item?.name||`${prefix} ${index+1}`).trim()||`${prefix} ${index+1}`,
      type:PORT_FORMATS.includes(item?.type)?item.type:'标量',
      order:Number.isFinite(Number(item?.order))?Number(item.order):index
    }))
    .filter(Boolean);
  while(normalized.length<minCount){
    normalized.push({
      id:`${prefix.toLowerCase()}-${normalized.length+1}`,
      name:`${prefix} ${normalized.length+1}`,
      type:'标量',
      order:normalized.length
    });
  }
  return normalized.map((item,index)=>({
    ...item,
    order:index
  }));
}

function ensureSubsystemInterface(nodeOrProps){
  const props=nodeOrProps?.props||nodeOrProps||{};
  if(!props.interface||typeof props.interface!=='object'){
    props.interface={};
  }
  props.interface.inputs=normalizeSubsystemInterfaceList(props.interface.inputs,'输入',0);
  props.interface.outputs=normalizeSubsystemInterfaceList(props.interface.outputs,'输出',0);
  return props.interface;
}

function buildSubsystemInterfaceRows(items,role){
  return items.map((item,index)=>`
    <div class="sim-intf-row subsystem-intf-row" data-subsystem-role="${role}" data-index="${index}" data-port-id="${escapeHtml(item.id)}">
      <div class="props-field">
        <label>${role==='input'?'输入':'输出'}名称 ${index+1}</label>
        <input data-subsystem-field="name" value="${escapeHtml(item.name)}">
      </div>
      <div class="props-field">
        <label>${role==='input'?'输入':'输出'}类型</label>
        <select data-subsystem-field="type">${buildSelectOptions(PORT_FORMATS,item.type)}</select>
      </div>
    </div>`).join('');
}

function buildSubsystemBlockFields(node){
  const canvas=ensureSubsystemCanvasNode(node);
  const intf=ensureSubsystemInterface(node);
  return `
    <div class="pgroup">
      <div class="pglbl">子系统设置</div>
      <div class="props-field"><label>模块名称</label><input id="prop-name" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.name)}"></div>
      <div class="props-field"><label>模块说明</label><textarea id="prop-description" rows="3" placeholder="可填写子系统职责、输入输出说明">${escapeHtml(node.props.description||'')}</textarea></div>
      <div class="prow"><span class="pk">子画布 ID</span><span class="pv">${escapeHtml(node.targetCanvasId||canvas?.id||'--')}<</span></div>
    </div>
    <div class="sim-intf-toolbar">
      <div class="sim-intf-counts">
        <div class="props-field"><label>输入数量</label><input id="subsystem-input-count" type="number" min="${SUBSYSTEM_INTERFACE_LIMITS.inputs[0]}" max="${SUBSYSTEM_INTERFACE_LIMITS.inputs[1]}" value="${intf.inputs.length}"></div>
        <div class="props-field"><label>输出数量</label><input id="subsystem-output-count" type="number" min="${SUBSYSTEM_INTERFACE_LIMITS.outputs[0]}" max="${SUBSYSTEM_INTERFACE_LIMITS.outputs[1]}" value="${intf.outputs.length}"></div>
      </div>
      <button class="props-secondary" type="button" onclick="syncSubsystemInterfaceCounts()">同步接口数量</button>
      <div class="sim-intf-note">父层子系统块显示这些稳定端口；进入子系统后会自动同步为内部边界输入/输出节点。</div>
    </div>
    <div class="sim-intf-group">
      <div class="sim-intf-head">
        <div class="sim-intf-title">输入接口</div>
        <div class="sim-intf-meta">${intf.inputs.length} 个父层输入</div>
      </div>
      <div class="sim-intf-list">${intf.inputs.length?buildSubsystemInterfaceRows(intf.inputs,'input'):'<div class="sim-intf-note">当前没有输入接口。</div>'}</div>
    </div>
    <div class="sim-intf-group">
      <div class="sim-intf-head">
        <div class="sim-intf-title">输出接口</div>
        <div class="sim-intf-meta">${intf.outputs.length} 个父层输出</div>
      </div>
      <div class="sim-intf-list">${intf.outputs.length?buildSubsystemInterfaceRows(intf.outputs,'output'):'<div class="sim-intf-note">当前没有输出接口。</div>'}</div>
    </div>`;
}

function readSubsystemInterfaceRows(role){
  return [...document.querySelectorAll(`.subsystem-intf-row[data-subsystem-role="${role}"]`)].map((row,index)=>({
    id:row.dataset.portId||`${role}-${index+1}`,
    name:(row.querySelector('[data-subsystem-field="name"]')?.value||`${role==='input'?'输入':'输出'} ${index+1}`).trim()||`${role==='input'?'输入':'输出'} ${index+1}`,
    type:row.querySelector('[data-subsystem-field="type"]')?.value||'标量',
    order:index
  }));
}

function getSubsystemBoundaryNodeId(subsystemNodeId,role,portId){
  return `node-${subsystemNodeId}-${role}-${portId}`;
}

function createSubsystemBoundaryNode(subsystemNode,role,item,index,existingNode=null){
  const type=role==='input'?'subsystem_in_port':'subsystem_out_port';
  const meta=COMPONENT_LIBRARY[type];
  const defaultX=role==='input'?64:(CANVAS_STAGE.width-meta.width-64);
  const defaultY=160+(index*92);
  return {
    id:existingNode?.id||getSubsystemBoundaryNodeId(subsystemNode.id,role,item.id),
    type,
    x:existingNode?.x ?? defaultX,
    y:existingNode?.y ?? defaultY,
    w:meta.width,
    h:meta.height,
    props:{
      ...(existingNode?.props||{}),
      name:item.name,
      interfacePortId:item.id,
      interfaceRole:role,
      portType:item.type,
      order:item.order
    },
    pythonBinding:null
  };
}

function syncSubsystemBoundaryNodes(node){
  if(!node||node.type!=='subsystem_block'){return null;}
  const canvas=ensureSubsystemCanvasNode(node);
  const intf=ensureSubsystemInterface(node);
  canvas.name=node.props.name;
  const existingBoundaryByKey=new Map(
    (canvas.nodes||[])
      .filter(item=>isSubsystemBoundaryNodeType(item.type))
      .map(item=>[`${item.props?.interfaceRole||'input'}:${item.props?.interfacePortId||item.id}`,item])
  );
  const nextBoundaryNodes=[
    ...intf.inputs.map((item,index)=>createSubsystemBoundaryNode(node,'input',item,index,existingBoundaryByKey.get(`input:${item.id}`))),
    ...intf.outputs.map((item,index)=>createSubsystemBoundaryNode(node,'output',item,index,existingBoundaryByKey.get(`output:${item.id}`)))
  ];
  const nextBoundaryIds=new Set(nextBoundaryNodes.map(item=>item.id));
  const removedBoundaryIds=(canvas.nodes||[])
    .filter(item=>isSubsystemBoundaryNodeType(item.type)&&!nextBoundaryIds.has(item.id))
    .map(item=>item.id);

  canvas.nodes=[
    ...nextBoundaryNodes,
    ...(canvas.nodes||[]).filter(item=>!isSubsystemBoundaryNodeType(item.type))
  ];
  if(removedBoundaryIds.length){
    canvas.edges=(canvas.edges||[]).filter(edge=>!removedBoundaryIds.includes(edge.sourceNodeId)&&!removedBoundaryIds.includes(edge.targetNodeId));
  }
  return canvas;
}

function syncSubsystemInterfaceCounts(){
  const node=getNode(S.selBlk);
  if(!node||node.type!=='subsystem_block'){return;}
  const nextProps=cloneDefaults(node.props);
  ensureSubsystemInterface(nextProps);
  nextProps.interface.inputs=readSubsystemInterfaceRows('input');
  nextProps.interface.outputs=readSubsystemInterfaceRows('output');
  const inputCount=clampInterfaceCount(document.getElementById('subsystem-input-count')?.value,SUBSYSTEM_INTERFACE_LIMITS.inputs);
  const outputCount=clampInterfaceCount(document.getElementById('subsystem-output-count')?.value,SUBSYSTEM_INTERFACE_LIMITS.outputs);
  nextProps.interface.inputs=normalizeSubsystemInterfaceList(nextProps.interface.inputs.slice(0,inputCount),'输入',inputCount);
  nextProps.interface.outputs=normalizeSubsystemInterfaceList(nextProps.interface.outputs.slice(0,outputCount),'输出',outputCount);
  const preview={...node,props:nextProps};
  renderPropertyPanel(preview);
}

function getNode(id){
  return S.modelNodes.find(node=>node.id===id);
}

function getEdge(id){
  return S.modelEdges.find(edge=>edge.id===id);
}

function getLayerLabel(layer){
  return LAYER_LABELS[layer]||layer||'未分类';
}

function isPhysicalFaultNodeType(type){
  return type==='fault_bias'||type==='fault_noise';
}

function isElectricalInjectableType(type){
  return type==='flow_block'||type==='simulation_block';
}

function isProtocolInjectableEdge(edge){
  return !!edge&&edge.lineType==='can';
}

function isFaultNodeType(type){
  return isPhysicalFaultNodeType(type);
}

function hasActiveRuntimeFault(target){
  if(!target){return false;}
  const api=window.__GZ_FAULT_INJECTION_RUNTIME__;
  if(api?.hasActiveFaultBinding?.(target)){return true;}
  return Array.isArray(target.faultBindings)&&target.faultBindings.some(binding=>binding&&binding.active!==false);
}

function isFaultNode(node){
  return !!node&&(isFaultNodeType(node.type)||Boolean(node.injectedFault)||hasActiveRuntimeFault(node));
}

function getMutationScopeForType(type){
  return isFaultNodeType(type)?'fault':'system';
}

function getMutationScopeForEdge(edge){
  const sourceNode=getNode(edge?.sourceNodeId);
  const targetNode=getNode(edge?.targetNodeId);
  return (sourceNode&&isFaultNodeType(sourceNode.type))||(targetNode&&isFaultNodeType(targetNode.type))?'fault':'system';
}

function syncFaultModelCount(){
  S.faultModels=S.importedFaultModels.length;
  S.faultLoaded=S.faultModels>0;
}

function initializeFaultCatalog(){
  S.availableFaultModels=cloneDefaults(FAULT_CATALOG_SEED);
  S.importedFaultModels=[];
  syncFaultModelCount();
  S.selectedFaultCatalogId=S.availableFaultModels[0]?.id||'';
}

function buildFaultCatalogMeta(model){
  return `${model.tags?.[0]||'Fault'} · ${getLayerLabel(model.layer)} · ${model.createdAt||'未记录'}`;
}

function getFaultCatalogModel(id){
  return S.availableFaultModels.find(model=>model.id===id);
}

function getImportedFaultModel(id){
  return S.importedFaultModels.find(model=>model.id===id);
}

function ensureImportedFaultModel(model){
  if(!model){return null;}
  const existed=S.importedFaultModels.find(item=>item.id===model.id);
  if(existed){
    syncFaultModelCount();
    return existed;
  }
  const copy=cloneDefaults(model);
  S.importedFaultModels.unshift(copy);
  syncFaultModelCount();
  return copy;
}

function upsertAvailableFaultModel(model){
  if(!model){return null;}
  const existed=S.availableFaultModels.find(item=>item.id===model.id||(item.name===model.name&&item.layer===model.layer));
  if(existed){
    Object.assign(existed,model);
    return existed;
  }
  S.availableFaultModels.unshift(cloneDefaults(model));
  return S.availableFaultModels[0];
}

function renderFaultCatalogList(){
  const container=document.getElementById('ifm-list-container');
  if(!container){return;}
  if(!S.selectedFaultCatalogId&&S.availableFaultModels.length){
    S.selectedFaultCatalogId=S.availableFaultModels[0].id;
  }
  container.innerHTML='';
  if(S.availableFaultModels.length===0){
    container.innerHTML='<div class="ifm-empty">当前没有可导入的故障模型，请先从模板库新建。</div>';
  }else{
    S.availableFaultModels.forEach(model=>{
      const item=document.createElement('div');
      const imported=S.importedFaultModels.some(entry=>entry.id===model.id);
      item.className=`ifm-item${S.selectedFaultCatalogId===model.id?' on':''}${imported?' is-imported':''}`;
      item.dataset.faultId=model.id;
      item.innerHTML=`
        <div class="ifm-icon">${model.layer==='electrical'?'电':model.layer==='physical'?'物':'协'}</div>
        <div style="min-width:0;flex:1">
          <div class="ifm-name">${escapeHtml(model.name)}</div>
          <div class="ifm-meta">${escapeHtml(buildFaultCatalogMeta(model))}</div>
        </div>
        ${imported?'<span class="ifm-state">已导入</span>':''}`;
      item.addEventListener('click',()=>selectFaultCatalogModel(model.id));
      container.appendChild(item);
    });
  }
  const selected=getFaultCatalogModel(S.selectedFaultCatalogId);
  document.getElementById('ifm-sel-hint').textContent=selected
    ?`已选：${selected.name} · ${getLayerLabel(selected.layer)}`
    :'已选：未选择故障模型';
}

function selectFaultCatalogModel(id){
  S.selectedFaultCatalogId=id;
  renderFaultCatalogList();
}

function getElectricalInjectableNodes(){
  return S.modelNodes.filter(node=>isElectricalInjectableType(node.type));
}

function clearCanvasSelection(){
  S.selBlk=null;
  S.selEdge=null;
  renderModelNodes();
  renderPropertyPanel(null);
}

function findNearestEdgeIdByClientPoint(clientX,clientY,threshold=14){
  const paths=[...document.querySelectorAll('.edge-path[data-edge-id]')];
  if(paths.length===0){return '';}
  const point=clientToStagePoint(clientX,clientY);
  const stageThreshold=threshold/Math.max(S.canvasScale,0.001);
  let nearestId='';
  let nearestDistance=Infinity;

  paths.forEach(path=>{
    const total=path.getTotalLength();
    const sampleStep=Math.max(8,total/18);
    for(let cursor=0;cursor<=total;cursor+=sampleStep){
      const pos=path.getPointAtLength(Math.min(cursor,total));
      const distance=Math.hypot(pos.x-point.x,pos.y-point.y);
      if(distance<nearestDistance){
        nearestDistance=distance;
        nearestId=path.dataset.edgeId||'';
      }
    }
    const last=path.getPointAtLength(total);
    const lastDistance=Math.hypot(last.x-point.x,last.y-point.y);
    if(lastDistance<nearestDistance){
      nearestDistance=lastDistance;
      nearestId=path.dataset.edgeId||'';
    }
  });

  return nearestDistance<=stageThreshold?nearestId:'';
}

function getConfigurableNodes(){
  return S.modelNodes.filter(node=>node.type==='flow_block'||node.type==='simulation_block');
}

function getNodeTypeCount(type){
  return S.modelNodes.filter(node=>node.type===type).length+1;
}

function getCanvasViewport(){
  return document.getElementById('canvas-viewport');
}

function getCanvasStage(){
  return document.getElementById('canvas-stage');
}

function getEdgeLabel(edge){
  if(edge.lineType==='can'&&edge.injectedFault?.faultKind){
    return `CAN · ${edge.injectedFault.faultKind}`;
  }
  return edge.lineType==='can'?'CAN':'LINK';
}

function createDefaultPythonBinding(){
  return {
    bound:false,
    fileName:null,
    moduleName:null,
    description:'',
    entryFunction:null,
    parsedInterface:null,
    rawSource:'',
    executionMode:'mock',
    executionConfig:{endpoint:'/api/python-flow/execute',timeoutMs:3000},
    portMapping:{inputs:[],outputs:[],middleVars:[]}
  };
}

function ensureFlowNodePythonBinding(node){
  if(!node||node.type!=='simulation_block'){return createDefaultPythonBinding();}
  if(!node.pythonBinding){
    node.pythonBinding=createDefaultPythonBinding();
  }
  if(!node.pythonBinding.portMapping){
    node.pythonBinding.portMapping={inputs:[],outputs:[],middleVars:[]};
  }
  return node.pythonBinding;
}

function isPythonBoundFlowBlock(node){
  return !!node&&node.type==='simulation_block'&&ensureFlowNodePythonBinding(node).bound;
}

function getPythonBindingNodeSize(node){
  const binding=ensureFlowNodePythonBinding(node);
  const inputCount=Math.max(binding.portMapping.inputs.length,1);
  const outputCount=Math.max(binding.portMapping.outputs.length,1);
  const middleCount=binding.portMapping.middleVars.length;
  const verticalDominant=Math.max(inputCount,outputCount);
  return {
    width:clamp(210+Math.max(0,middleCount-1)*34,210,360),
    height:clamp(102+Math.max(0,verticalDominant-2)*24+(middleCount?22:0),102,320)
  };
}

function getPythonBindingSummary(node){
  const binding=ensureFlowNodePythonBinding(node);
  return `${binding.portMapping.inputs.length} 输入 / ${binding.portMapping.outputs.length} 输出 / ${binding.portMapping.middleVars.length} 中间变量`;
}

function buildPythonPortTooltip(meta,kind='input'){
  if(!meta){return '';}
  const parts=[meta.displayName||meta.varName||'端口'];
  if(meta.type){parts.push(`类型: ${meta.type}`);}
  if(kind==='input'&&meta.default!==null&&meta.default!==undefined&&meta.default!==''){
    parts.push(`默认值: ${meta.default}`);
  }
  if(meta.comment){parts.push(meta.comment);}
  return parts.join('\\n');
}

function buildEdgePortMeta(port){
  return {
    kind:port.kind||'output',
    varName:port.meta?.varName||null,
    displayName:port.meta?.displayName||port.label||'',
    type:port.meta?.type||'any',
    default:port.meta?.default??null
  };
}

function normalizePortType(type){
  if(!type){return 'any';}
  return String(type).trim().toLowerCase();
}

function arePortTypesCompatible(sourceMeta,targetMeta){
  const sourceType=normalizePortType(sourceMeta?.type);
  const targetType=normalizePortType(targetMeta?.type);
  if(sourceType==='any'||targetType==='any'){return true;}
  if(sourceType===targetType){return true;}
  if(sourceType==='int'&&targetType==='float'){return true;}
  return false;
}

function getPortDisplayName(port){
  if(port?.meta?.displayName){return port.meta.displayName;}
  if(port?.meta?.varName){return port.meta.varName;}
  return '';
}

function getPortTooltip(port,direction='input'){
  if(port?.meta){
    return buildPythonPortTooltip(port.meta,direction==='input'?'input':(port.kind||'output'));
  }
  return port?.label||'';
}

function isPortConnected(nodeId,direction,index){
  if(direction==='input'){
    return S.modelEdges.some(edge=>edge.targetNodeId===nodeId&&(edge.targetPortIndex||0)===index);
  }
  return S.modelEdges.some(edge=>edge.sourceNodeId===nodeId&&(edge.sourcePortIndex||0)===index);
}

function getPortTone(node,port,direction){
  if(direction==='input'){
    return port?.meta?.connected?'#1d6fbf':'#6f8fb8';
  }
  if(port?.kind==='middle'){
    return '#27808f';
  }
  if(node.type==='signal_source'){
    return '#4f86e7';
  }
  return '#6da0ff';
}

function appendPortLabel(portEl,port){
  const label=getPortDisplayName(port);
  if(!label){return;}
  const labelEl=document.createElement('span');
  labelEl.className='node-port__label';
  labelEl.textContent=label;
  portEl.appendChild(labelEl);
}

function syncPythonInputConnectionState(nodeId){
  const node=getNode(nodeId);
  if(!isPythonBoundFlowBlock(node)){return;}
  node.pythonBinding.portMapping.inputs.forEach((port,index)=>{
    port.connected=S.modelEdges.some(edge=>edge.targetNodeId===nodeId&&(edge.targetPortIndex||0)===index);
  });
}

function syncAllPythonInputConnectionState(){
  S.modelNodes.forEach(node=>{
    if(isPythonBoundFlowBlock(node)){
      syncPythonInputConnectionState(node.id);
    }
  });
}

function openPythonBindingDialog(nodeId=''){
  const target=getNode(nodeId||S.selBlk);
  if(!target||target.type!=='simulation_block'){
    toast('请先选中一个仿真块以绑定 Python 文件','w');
    return;
  }
  const binding=ensureFlowNodePythonBinding(target);
  window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('gz:open-python-binding',{
    detail:{
      targetNode:{id:target.id,label:target.props.name,props:cloneDefaults(target.props)},
      parsedInterface:binding.bound?cloneDefaults(binding.parsedInterface):null,
      boundSnapshot:binding.bound?cloneDefaults(binding):null
    }
  }));
}

function applyPythonBindingToNode(nodeId,binding){
  const node=getNode(nodeId);
  if(!node||node.type!=='simulation_block'){return;}
  node.pythonBinding=cloneDefaults(binding);
  applyNodeGeometry(node);
  const removedEdges=pruneInvalidEdgesForNode(node);
  syncAllPythonInputConnectionState();
  markTopologyDirty('system');
  renderModelNodes();
  selectNode(node.id);
  syncConfigTargets(node.id);
  updateUI();
  toast(`已为 ${node.props.name} 绑定 ${binding.fileName}${removedEdges?`，并移除 ${removedEdges} 条无效连线`:''}`,'s');
}

function unbindPythonBinding(nodeId=''){
  const node=getNode(nodeId||S.selBlk);
  if(!node||node.type!=='simulation_block'){return;}
  const binding=ensureFlowNodePythonBinding(node);
  if(!binding.bound){
    toast('当前仿真块尚未绑定 Python 文件','w');
    return;
  }
  node.pythonBinding=createDefaultPythonBinding();
  applyNodeGeometry(node);
  const removedEdges=pruneInvalidEdgesForNode(node);
  syncAllPythonInputConnectionState();
  markTopologyDirty('system');
  renderModelNodes();
  selectNode(node.id);
  syncConfigTargets(node.id);
  updateUI();
  toast(`已解除 ${node.props.name} 的 Python 绑定${removedEdges?`，并移除 ${removedEdges} 条无效连线`:''}`,'s');
}

function getNodePorts(node){
  if(!node){return {inputs:[],outputs:[]};}
  if(node.type==='flow_block'&&isPythonBoundFlowBlock(node)){
    const binding=ensureFlowNodePythonBinding(node);
    return {
      inputs:binding.portMapping.inputs.map((item,index)=>({
        key:`input-${index}`,
        label:item.displayName||item.varName||`input_${index}`,
        kind:'input',
        side:'left',
        meta:item
      })),
      outputs:[
        ...binding.portMapping.outputs.map((item,index)=>({
          key:`output-${index}`,
          label:item.displayName||item.varName||`output_${index}`,
          kind:'output',
          side:'right',
          meta:item
        })),
        ...binding.portMapping.middleVars.map((item,index)=>({
          key:`middle-${index}`,
          label:item.displayName||item.varName||`middle_${index}`,
          kind:'middle',
          side:'top',
          meta:item
        }))
      ]
    };
  }
  if(node.type==='signal_source'){
    return {
      inputs:[],
      outputs:[{key:'signal',label:node.props.outputFormat||'输出'}]
    };
  }
  if(node.type==='flow_block'){
    return {
      inputs:[{key:'input',label:node.props.inputName||'输入'}],
      outputs:[{key:'output',label:node.props.outputName||'输出'}]
    };
  }
  if(node.type==='simulation_block'){
    const groups=getSimulationPortSets(node.props);
    return {
      inputs:groups.inputs.map((item,index)=>({
        key:`input-${index}`,
        label:`输入 ${index+1} · ${item.name} / ${item.type}`,
        kind:'input',
        side:'left'
      })),
      outputs:getSimulationFlatOutputs(node.props).map((item,index)=>({
        key:`${item.kind}-${item.index}`,
        label:`${item.kind==='middle'?'中间量':'输出'} ${item.index+1} · ${item.name} / ${item.type}`,
        kind:item.kind,
        side:item.side,
        portIndex:index
      }))
    };
  }
  if(node.type.startsWith('fault_')){
    return {
      inputs:[{key:'input',label:'故障输入'}],
      outputs:[{key:'output',label:'故障输出'}]
    };
  }
  if(node.type.startsWith('instrument_')){
    return {
      inputs:[{key:'input',label:'观测输入'}],
      outputs:[]
    };
  }
  return {inputs:[],outputs:[]};
}

function canvasNumber(value,fallback=0){
  const numeric=Number(value);
  return Number.isFinite(numeric)?numeric:fallback;
}

function isFiniteCanvasPoint(point){
  return Boolean(point)&&Number.isFinite(point.x)&&Number.isFinite(point.y);
}

function getPortInfo(node,direction,index=0){
  const ports=getNodePorts(node)[direction==='input'?'inputs':'outputs'];
  const port=ports[index];
  if(!port){return null;}
  const side=port.side||(direction==='input'?'left':'right');
  const meta=COMPONENT_LIBRARY[node.type]||{};
  const nodeW=canvasNumber(node.w,canvasNumber(meta.width,120));
  const nodeH=canvasNumber(node.h,canvasNumber(meta.height,70));
  const nodeX=canvasNumber(node.x,0);
  const nodeY=canvasNumber(node.y,0);
  let localX=direction==='input'?0:nodeW;
  let localY=Math.round(nodeH/2);
  if(side==='top'){
    const topPorts=ports.filter(item=>(item.side||'right')==='top');
    const topIndex=topPorts.findIndex(item=>item.key===port.key);
    const topGap=nodeW/(Math.max(topPorts.length,1)+1);
    localX=Math.round(topGap*(topIndex+1));
    localY=0;
  }else{
    const sidePorts=ports.filter(item=>(item.side||(direction==='input'?'left':'right'))===side);
    const sideIndex=sidePorts.findIndex(item=>item.key===port.key);
    const gap=nodeH/(Math.max(sidePorts.length,1)+1);
    localY=Math.round(gap*(sideIndex+1));
    localX=side==='left'?0:nodeW;
  }
  return {
    ...port,
    direction,
    side,
    index,
    localX,
    localY,
    x:nodeX+localX,
    y:nodeY+localY
  };
}

function buildEdgePath(start,end){
  if(!isFiniteCanvasPoint(start)||!isFiniteCanvasPoint(end)){
    return 'M 0 0 C 0 0, 0 0, 0 0';
  }
  const deltaX=Math.max(64,Math.abs(end.x-start.x)*0.42);
  const deltaY=Math.max(48,Math.abs(end.y-start.y)*0.38);
  const cp1={
    x:start.side==='right'?start.x+deltaX:(start.side==='left'?start.x-deltaX:start.x),
    y:start.side==='top'?start.y-deltaY:start.y
  };
  const cp2={
    x:end.side==='right'?end.x+deltaX:(end.side==='left'?end.x-deltaX:end.x),
    y:end.side==='top'?end.y-deltaY:end.y
  };
  return `M ${start.x} ${start.y} C ${cp1.x} ${cp1.y}, ${cp2.x} ${cp2.y}, ${end.x} ${end.y}`;
}

function clientToStagePoint(clientX,clientY){
  const viewport=getCanvasViewport();
  const rect=viewport.getBoundingClientRect();
  return {
    x:(clientX-rect.left-S.canvasOffsetX)/S.canvasScale,
    y:(clientY-rect.top-S.canvasOffsetY)/S.canvasScale
  };
}

function movedBeyondPointerThreshold(startX,startY,currentX,currentY,threshold=POINTER_DRAG_THRESHOLD){
  return Math.hypot((currentX||0)-(startX||0),(currentY||0)-(startY||0))>=threshold;
}

function clampCanvasOffset(){
  const viewport=getCanvasViewport();
  if(!viewport){return;}
  const scaledWidth=CANVAS_STAGE.width*S.canvasScale;
  const scaledHeight=CANVAS_STAGE.height*S.canvasScale;
  const width=viewport.clientWidth;
  const height=viewport.clientHeight;
  const edgeGap=72;

  if(scaledWidth<=width-edgeGap*2){
    S.canvasOffsetX=Math.round((width-scaledWidth)/2);
  }else{
    S.canvasOffsetX=clamp(S.canvasOffsetX,width-scaledWidth-edgeGap,edgeGap);
  }

  if(scaledHeight<=height-edgeGap*2){
    S.canvasOffsetY=Math.round((height-scaledHeight)/2);
  }else{
    S.canvasOffsetY=clamp(S.canvasOffsetY,height-scaledHeight-edgeGap,edgeGap);
  }
}

function applyCanvasTransform(){
  const stage=getCanvasStage();
  if(stage){
    stage.style.transform=`translate(${S.canvasOffsetX}px,${S.canvasOffsetY}px) scale(${S.canvasScale})`;
  }
  const fill=document.getElementById('canvas-zoom-fill');
  const reset=document.getElementById('canvas-zoom-reset');
  const percent=Math.round(S.canvasScale*100);
  if(fill){
    const ratio=clamp((S.canvasScale-CANVAS_STAGE.minScale)/(CANVAS_STAGE.maxScale-CANVAS_STAGE.minScale),0,1);
    fill.style.width=`${Math.round(28+ratio*72)}%`;
  }
  if(reset){
    reset.textContent=`${percent}%`;
  }
  syncActiveCanvasViewportFromState();
}

function setCanvasZoom(nextScale,pivotClientX,pivotClientY){
  const viewport=getCanvasViewport();
  if(!viewport){return;}
  const rect=viewport.getBoundingClientRect();
  const oldScale=S.canvasScale;
  const clampedScale=clamp(nextScale,CANVAS_STAGE.minScale,CANVAS_STAGE.maxScale);
  const pivotX=(pivotClientX ?? (rect.left+rect.width/2))-rect.left;
  const pivotY=(pivotClientY ?? (rect.top+rect.height/2))-rect.top;
  const stageX=(pivotX-S.canvasOffsetX)/oldScale;
  const stageY=(pivotY-S.canvasOffsetY)/oldScale;
  S.canvasScale=clampedScale;
  S.canvasOffsetX=pivotX-stageX*S.canvasScale;
  S.canvasOffsetY=pivotY-stageY*S.canvasScale;
  clampCanvasOffset();
  applyCanvasTransform();
}

function handleCanvasZoomIn(){
  setCanvasZoom(S.canvasScale+0.1);
}

function handleCanvasZoomOut(){
  setCanvasZoom(S.canvasScale-0.1);
}

function handleCanvasZoomReset(){
  S.canvasScale=1;
  S.canvasOffsetX=0;
  S.canvasOffsetY=0;
  clampCanvasOffset();
  applyCanvasTransform();
}

function setConnectionTool(type){
  S.activeLineType=type==='can'?'can':'normal';
  document.querySelectorAll('.citem-line-tool').forEach(item=>{
    item.classList.toggle('active',item.dataset.lineType===S.activeLineType);
  });
  const chip=document.getElementById('line-mode-chip');
  if(chip){
    chip.textContent=S.activeLineType==='can'?'CAN 总线':'普通连接线';
    chip.classList.toggle('can',S.activeLineType==='can');
  }
  if(S.pendingConnection){
    S.pendingConnection.lineType=S.activeLineType;
    renderEdges();
  }
}

function clearPendingConnection(){
  S.pendingConnection=null;
  renderEdges();
}

function markTopologyDirty(scope='system'){
  if(scope==='system'){
    S.systemSaved=false;
  }
  S.simDone=false;
  if(typeof SIM!=='undefined'){
    if(typeof clearSimLoop==='function'){clearSimLoop();}
    SIM.inited=false;
    SIM.running=false;
    SIM.paused=false;
    SIM.hasSamples=false;
    SIM.time=0;
    SIM.stepIndex=0;
  }
  if(scope==='system'){
    if(S.step!==1){S.step=1;}
    return;
  }
  if(S.systemSaved){
    S.step=2;
  }
}

function buildSelectOptions(options,selected){
  return options.map(option=>`<option value="${escapeHtml(option)}"${option===selected?' selected':''}>${escapeHtml(option)}</option>`).join('');
}

function buildNodeSubtitle(node){
  const props=node.props;
  const faultNote=node.injectedFault?' · 电气故障':''; 
  switch(node.type){
    case 'signal_source':
      return `${props.waveType} · 幅值${props.amplitude} · ${props.outputFormat}`;
    case 'flow_block':
      return `${props.inputName} / ${props.inputFormat} → ${props.outputName} / ${props.outputFormat}${faultNote}`;
    case 'simulation_block':
      normalizeSimulationInterfaces(props);
      return `${props.inputs.length}输入 · ${props.outputs.length}输出 · ${props.middleVars.length}中间量 · ${props.moduleType}${faultNote}`;
    case 'fault_bias':
    case 'fault_noise':
    case 'fault_stuck':
    case 'fault_drift':
      return `${props.faultType} · ${props.layer}`;
    case 'instrument_scope':
      return `${props.instrumentType} · 双击查看波形`;
    case 'instrument_spectrum':
    case 'instrument_logger':
      return `${props.instrumentType} · ${props.sampleRate}`;
    case 'link_normal':
    case 'link_can':
      return `${props.sourcePort} → ${props.targetPort}`;
    default:
      return '';
  }
}

function renderEdges(){
  const edgeGroup=document.getElementById('edge-group');
  const preview=document.getElementById('edge-preview');
  if(!edgeGroup||!preview){return;}
  edgeGroup.innerHTML='';

  S.modelEdges.forEach(edge=>{
    const sourceNode=getNode(edge.sourceNodeId);
    const targetNode=getNode(edge.targetNodeId);
    if(!sourceNode||!targetNode){return;}
    const sourcePort=getPortInfo(sourceNode,'output',edge.sourcePortIndex||0);
    const targetPort=getPortInfo(targetNode,'input',edge.targetPortIndex||0);
    if(!sourcePort||!targetPort||!isFiniteCanvasPoint(sourcePort)||!isFiniteCanvasPoint(targetPort)){return;}
    const selected=S.selEdge===edge.id;
    const faulted=Boolean(edge.injectedFault);
    const edgePath=buildEdgePath(sourcePort,targetPort);

    const hit=document.createElementNS('http://www.w3.org/2000/svg','path');
    hit.setAttribute('d',edgePath);
    hit.setAttribute('class','edge-hit');
    hit.dataset.edgeId=edge.id;
    hit.addEventListener('click',event=>{
      event.stopPropagation();
      selectEdge(edge.id);
    });
    edgeGroup.appendChild(hit);

    const path=document.createElementNS('http://www.w3.org/2000/svg','path');
    path.setAttribute('d',edgePath);
    path.setAttribute('class',`edge-path edge-path--${edge.lineType}${selected?' is-selected':''}${faulted?' is-faulted':''}`);
    path.setAttribute('marker-end',faulted?'url(#edge-arrow-fault)':`url(#edge-arrow-${edge.lineType})`);
    path.dataset.edgeId=edge.id;
    path.addEventListener('click',event=>{
      event.stopPropagation();
      selectEdge(edge.id);
    });
    edgeGroup.appendChild(path);

    const label=document.createElementNS('http://www.w3.org/2000/svg','text');
    label.setAttribute('class',`edge-label${selected?' is-selected':''}${faulted?' is-faulted':''}`);
    label.setAttribute('x',String(Math.round((sourcePort.x+targetPort.x)/2)));
    label.setAttribute('y',String(Math.round((sourcePort.y+targetPort.y)/2)-10));
    label.setAttribute('text-anchor','middle');
    label.dataset.edgeId=edge.id;
    label.textContent=getEdgeLabel(edge);
    label.addEventListener('click',event=>{
      event.stopPropagation();
      selectEdge(edge.id);
    });
    edgeGroup.appendChild(label);
  });

  if(S.pendingConnection){
    const sourceNode=getNode(S.pendingConnection.sourceNodeId);
    const sourcePort=sourceNode?getPortInfo(sourceNode,'output',S.pendingConnection.sourcePortIndex||0):null;
    if(sourcePort){
      preview.style.display='block';
      preview.setAttribute('d',buildEdgePath(sourcePort,{
        x:S.pendingConnection.x,
        y:S.pendingConnection.y
      }));
      preview.setAttribute('stroke',S.pendingConnection.lineType==='can'?'#8c7cf6':'#7ab7ff');
      preview.setAttribute('stroke-width',S.pendingConnection.lineType==='can'?'2.8':'2');
    }else{
      preview.style.display='none';
      preview.setAttribute('d','');
    }
  }else{
    preview.style.display='none';
    preview.setAttribute('d','');
  }
}

function updateNodePositionDOM(node){
  const element=document.getElementById(`b-${node.id}`);
  if(!element){return;}
  element.style.left=`${node.x}px`;
  element.style.top=`${node.y}px`;
}

function beginNodeDrag(event,nodeId){
  if(event.button!==0||event.target.closest('.node-port')){return;}
  const node=getNode(nodeId);
  if(!node){return;}
  selectNode(nodeId);
  NODE_DRAG.active=true;
  NODE_DRAG.engaged=false;
  NODE_DRAG.pointerId=event.pointerId;
  NODE_DRAG.nodeId=nodeId;
  NODE_DRAG.startX=event.clientX;
  NODE_DRAG.startY=event.clientY;
  NODE_DRAG.originX=node.x;
  NODE_DRAG.originY=node.y;
}

function handlePortClick(event,nodeId,direction,index){
  event.stopPropagation();
  const node=getNode(nodeId);
  if(!node){return;}
  const port=getPortInfo(node,direction,index);
  if(!port){return;}

  if(direction==='output'){
    S.pendingConnection={
      sourceNodeId:nodeId,
      sourcePortIndex:index,
      lineType:S.activeLineType,
      x:port.x,
      y:port.y
    };
    renderEdges();
    return;
  }

  if(!S.pendingConnection){
    toast('请先从输出端口开始连线','w');
    return;
  }

  if(S.pendingConnection.sourceNodeId===nodeId){
    toast('请连接到其他模块的输入端口','w');
    clearPendingConnection();
    return;
  }

  const sourceNode=getNode(S.pendingConnection.sourceNodeId);
  const sourcePort=getPortInfo(sourceNode,'output',S.pendingConnection.sourcePortIndex||0);
  const sourceMeta=buildEdgePortMeta(sourcePort);
  const targetMeta=buildEdgePortMeta(port);
  if(!arePortTypesCompatible(sourceMeta,targetMeta)){
    toast(`端口类型不兼容：${sourceMeta.type||'any'} -> ${targetMeta.type||'any'}`,'w');
    clearPendingConnection();
    return;
  }

  const duplicate=S.modelEdges.some(edge=>
    edge.sourceNodeId===S.pendingConnection.sourceNodeId &&
    edge.targetNodeId===nodeId &&
    (edge.sourcePortIndex||0)===(S.pendingConnection.sourcePortIndex||0) &&
    (edge.targetPortIndex||0)===index
  );
  if(duplicate){
    toast('该连线已存在','w');
    clearPendingConnection();
    return;
  }

  const occupiedTarget=S.modelEdges.some(edge=>
    edge.targetNodeId===nodeId &&
    (edge.targetPortIndex||0)===index
  );
  if(occupiedTarget){
    toast('该输入端口已有连线，请先删除原连线，避免信号耦合','w');
    clearPendingConnection();
    return;
  }

  const newEdge={
    id:`edge-${++S.edgeSeq}`,
    lineType:S.pendingConnection.lineType,
    sourceNodeId:S.pendingConnection.sourceNodeId,
    targetNodeId:nodeId,
    sourcePortIndex:S.pendingConnection.sourcePortIndex||0,
    targetPortIndex:index,
    sourcePort:{
      index:S.pendingConnection.sourcePortIndex||0,
      varName:sourceMeta.varName,
      displayName:sourceMeta.displayName,
      type:sourceMeta.type
    },
    targetPort:{
      index,
      varName:targetMeta.varName,
      displayName:targetMeta.displayName,
      type:targetMeta.type
    },
    sourcePortMeta:sourceMeta,
    targetPortMeta:targetMeta
  };
  S.modelEdges.push(newEdge);
  syncAllPythonInputConnectionState();
  markTopologyDirty(getMutationScopeForEdge(newEdge));
  S.selEdge=newEdge.id;
  S.selBlk=null;
  clearPendingConnection();
  renderPropertyPanel(newEdge);
  updateUI();
  toast('连线已创建','s');
}

function renderModelNodes(){
  const layer=document.getElementById('node-layer');
  if(!layer){return;}
  layer.innerHTML='';
  S.modelNodes.forEach(node=>{
    applyNodeGeometry(node);
    const meta=COMPONENT_LIBRARY[node.type];
    const faulted=S.faultedBlks.includes(node.id)||Boolean(node.injectedFault);
    const pythonBound=isPythonBoundFlowBlock(node);
    const el=document.createElement('div');
    el.id=`b-${node.id}`;
    el.className=`blk ${meta.className}${S.selBlk===node.id?' sel':''}${faulted?' faulted':''}${pythonBound?' python-bound':''}`;
    el.style.left=`${node.x}px`;
    el.style.top=`${node.y}px`;
    el.style.width=`${node.w}px`;
    el.style.height=`${node.h}px`;
    if(node.type==='simulation_block'||pythonBound){
      const topPortCount=node.type==='simulation_block'
        ?(node.props.middleVars?.length||0)
        :(node.pythonBinding?.portMapping?.middleVars?.length||0);
      el.style.paddingTop=`${topPortCount?18:10}px`;
      el.style.paddingBottom='10px';
    }else{
      el.style.paddingTop='';
      el.style.paddingBottom='';
    }
    const nodeTitle=pythonBound?(node.pythonBinding?.fileName||node.props.name):node.props.name;
    const nodeSubtitle=pythonBound?`流程块 · ${getPythonBindingSummary(node)}`:buildNodeSubtitle(node);
    el.innerHTML=`
      <div class="fbadge">F</div>
      ${pythonBound?'<div class="node-card__python-chip">Py</div>':''}
      <div class="blk-kicker">${pythonBound?'已绑定 Python':(faulted&&!isFaultNodeType(node.type)?`${meta.badge} 故障` : meta.badge)}</div>
      <div class="blk-lbl">${escapeHtml(nodeTitle)}</div>
      <div class="blk-sub">${escapeHtml(nodeSubtitle)}</div>`;
    el.addEventListener('pointerdown',event=>beginNodeDrag(event,node.id));
    el.addEventListener('click',event=>{
      if(event.target.closest('.node-port')){return;}
      selectNode(node.id);
      if(node.type==='instrument_scope'||node.type==='instrument_logger'||node.type==='instrument_spectrum'||node.type==='flow_block'){
        const now=Date.now();
        if(NODE_DOUBLE_CLICK.nodeId===node.id&&(now-NODE_DOUBLE_CLICK.timestamp)<320){
          NODE_DOUBLE_CLICK.nodeId='';
          NODE_DOUBLE_CLICK.timestamp=0;
          if(node.type==='instrument_scope'){
            openScope(node.id);
          }else if(node.type==='flow_block'){
            openPythonBindingDialog(node.id);
          }else{
            renderPropertyPanel(node);
          }
          return;
        }
        NODE_DOUBLE_CLICK.nodeId=node.id;
        NODE_DOUBLE_CLICK.timestamp=now;
      }
    });
    if(node.type==='instrument_scope'){
      el.title='双击查看示波器';
      el.addEventListener('dblclick',event=>{
        event.stopPropagation();
        openScope(node.id);
      });
    }

    if(node.type==='instrument_logger'||node.type==='instrument_spectrum'){
      el.title='双击查看仪器采样与分析面板';
      el.addEventListener('dblclick',event=>{
        event.stopPropagation();
        selectNode(node.id);
        renderPropertyPanel(node);
      });
    }

    if(node.type==='flow_block'){
      el.title=pythonBound
        ?`已绑定 Python：${node.pythonBinding?.fileName||'unknown.py'}\n双击可重新绑定`
        :'双击绑定 Python 文件';
      el.addEventListener('dblclick',event=>{
        event.stopPropagation();
        openPythonBindingDialog(node.id);
      });
    }


    const ports=getNodePorts(node);
    ports.inputs.forEach((port,index)=>{
      const info=getPortInfo(node,'input',index);
      const portEl=document.createElement('button');
      portEl.type='button';
      portEl.className='node-port node-port--input';
      portEl.style.left=`${info.localX}px`;
      portEl.style.top=`${info.localY}px`;
      portEl.style.color=getPortTone(node,port,'input');
      portEl.title=getPortTooltip(port,'input');
      if(isPortConnected(node.id,'input',index)){
        portEl.classList.add('is-connected');
      }
      if(S.pendingConnection){
        portEl.classList.add('node-port--active');
      }
      portEl.innerHTML='<span class="node-port__inner"><</span>';
      appendPortLabel(portEl,port);
      portEl.addEventListener('click',event=>handlePortClick(event,node.id,'input',index));
      el.appendChild(portEl);
    });
    ports.outputs.forEach((port,index)=>{
      const info=getPortInfo(node,'output',index);
      const portEl=document.createElement('button');
      portEl.type='button';
      portEl.className=`node-port node-port--output${info.side==='top'?' node-port--top':''}`;
      portEl.style.left=`${info.localX}px`;
      portEl.style.top=`${info.localY}px`;
      portEl.style.color=getPortTone(node,port,'output');
      portEl.title=getPortTooltip(port,'output');
      if(isPortConnected(node.id,'output',index)){
        portEl.classList.add('is-connected');
      }
      if(S.pendingConnection&&S.pendingConnection.sourceNodeId===node.id&&(S.pendingConnection.sourcePortIndex||0)===index){
        portEl.classList.add('node-port--active');
      }
      portEl.innerHTML='<span class="node-port__inner"><</span>';
      appendPortLabel(portEl,port);
      portEl.addEventListener('click',event=>handlePortClick(event,node.id,'output',index));
      el.appendChild(portEl);
    });

    layer.appendChild(el);
  });
  document.getElementById('diagram-placeholder').style.display=S.modelNodes.length?'none':'flex';
  renderEdges();
}

function selectNode(id){
  const node=getNode(id);
  if(!node){return;}
  S.selBlk=id;
  S.selEdge=null;
  S.propertyPanelTab='overview';
  renderModelNodes();
  renderPropertyPanel(node);
  document.querySelectorAll('.props-tab').forEach(button=>{
    const tab=button.dataset.propsTab||'overview';
    button.classList.toggle('is-active',tab==='overview');
    button.setAttribute('aria-selected',tab==='overview'?'true':'false');
  });
}

function selBlk(id){selectNode(id);}

function selectEdge(id){
  const edge=getEdge(id);
  if(!edge){return;}
  if(S.pendingConnection){
    S.pendingConnection=null;
  }
  S.selEdge=id;
  S.selBlk=null;
  S.propertyPanelTab='overview';
  renderModelNodes();
  renderPropertyPanel(edge);
  document.querySelectorAll('.props-tab').forEach(button=>{
    const tab=button.dataset.propsTab||'overview';
    button.classList.toggle('is-active',tab==='overview');
    button.setAttribute('aria-selected',tab==='overview'?'true':'false');
  });
}

function deleteSelectedNode(){
  const node=getNode(S.selBlk);
  if(!node){return;}
  const removedName=node.props.name;
  const removedEdges=S.modelEdges.filter(edge=>edge.sourceNodeId===node.id||edge.targetNodeId===node.id).length;
  const protocolEdgeAffected=S.protocolInjectTargetId&&S.modelEdges.some(edge=>edge.id===S.protocolInjectTargetId&&(edge.sourceNodeId===node.id||edge.targetNodeId===node.id));

  S.modelNodes=S.modelNodes.filter(item=>item.id!==node.id);
  S.modelEdges=S.modelEdges.filter(edge=>edge.sourceNodeId!==node.id&&edge.targetNodeId!==node.id);
  S.faultedBlks=S.faultedBlks.filter(id=>id!==node.id);
  if(S.injectTargetId===node.id){
    S.injectTargetId='';
  }
  if(protocolEdgeAffected){
    S.protocolInjectTargetId='';
  }
  if(S.pendingConnection&&S.pendingConnection.sourceNodeId===node.id){
    S.pendingConnection=null;
  }
  S.selBlk=null;
  markTopologyDirty(getMutationScopeForType(node.type));
  syncAllPythonInputConnectionState();
  renderModelNodes();
  renderPropertyPanel(null);
  syncConfigTargets();
  updateUI();
  toast(`模块“${removedName}”已删除${removedEdges?`，并移除 ${removedEdges} 条连线`:''}`,'s');
}

function deleteSelectedEdge(){
  const edge=getEdge(S.selEdge);
  if(!edge){return;}
  const edgeName=edge.lineType==='can'?'CAN 总线':'普通连接线';
  S.modelEdges=S.modelEdges.filter(item=>item.id!==edge.id);
  if(S.protocolInjectTargetId===edge.id){
    S.protocolInjectTargetId='';
    S.protocolInjectSelectionMode='';
    S.protocolInjectSelectionId='';
  }
  S.selEdge=null;
  syncAllPythonInputConnectionState();
  markTopologyDirty(getMutationScopeForEdge(edge));
  renderModelNodes();
  renderPropertyPanel(null);
  updateUI();
  toast(`连线“${edgeName}”已删除`,'s');
}

function deleteCurrentSelection(){
  if(S.selEdge){
    deleteSelectedEdge();
    return;
  }
  if(S.selBlk){
    deleteSelectedNode();
  }
}

function syncConfigTargets(preferredId=''){
  const sel=document.getElementById('cftgt');
  if(!sel){return;}
  const currentValue=preferredId||sel.value;
  const nodes=getConfigurableNodes();
  if(nodes.length===0){
    sel.innerHTML='<option value="">请先创建系统建模组件</option>';
    return;
  }
  sel.innerHTML=nodes.map(node=>`<option value="${node.id}">${escapeHtml(node.props.name)} · ${COMPONENT_LIBRARY[node.type].label}</option>`).join('');
  sel.value=nodes.some(node=>node.id===currentValue)?currentValue:nodes[0].id;
}

function markFaultTarget(targetId){
  S.faultedBlks=targetId?[targetId]:[];
  renderModelNodes();
  if(S.selBlk&&getNode(S.selBlk)){renderPropertyPanel(getNode(S.selBlk));}
  else if(S.selEdge&&getEdge(S.selEdge)){renderPropertyPanel(getEdge(S.selEdge));}
}

function createNode(type,rawX,rawY){
  const meta=COMPONENT_LIBRARY[type];
  if(!meta){return;}
  const props=cloneDefaults(meta.defaults);
  const count=getNodeTypeCount(type);
  if(type==='signal_source'){props.name=`信号源 ${count}`;}
  if(type==='flow_block'){props.name=`流程块 ${count}`;}
  if(type==='simulation_block'){props.name=`仿真块 ${count}`;}
  if(type.startsWith('fault_')){props.name=`${meta.label} ${count}`;}
  if(type.startsWith('instrument_')){props.name=`${meta.label} ${count}`;}
  if(type.startsWith('link_')){props.name=`${meta.label} ${count}`;}

  if(type==='simulation_block'){
    normalizeSimulationInterfaces(props);
  }
  const size=type==='simulation_block'?getSimulationNodeSize(props):{width:meta.width,height:meta.height};
  const point={
    x:clamp(Math.round(rawX-size.width/2),CANVAS_STAGE.nodePadding,CANVAS_STAGE.width-size.width-CANVAS_STAGE.nodePadding),
    y:clamp(Math.round(rawY-size.height/2),CANVAS_STAGE.nodeMinY,CANVAS_STAGE.height-size.height-CANVAS_STAGE.nodePadding)
  };
  S.modelNodes.push({
    id:`node-${++S.nodeSeq}`,
    type,
    x:point.x,
    y:point.y,
    w:size.width,
    h:size.height,
    props,
    pythonBinding:type==='simulation_block'?createDefaultPythonBinding():null
  });
  markTopologyDirty(getMutationScopeForType(type));
  const node=S.modelNodes[S.modelNodes.length-1];
  renderModelNodes();
  syncConfigTargets(node.id);
  selectNode(node.id);
  updateUI();
  toast(`${meta.label} 已加入画布`,'s');
}

function initPaletteDrag(){
  document.querySelectorAll('.citem-draggable').forEach(item=>{
    item.addEventListener('dragstart',event=>{
      const type=item.dataset.component||'';
      S.dragType=type;
      item.classList.add('citem-dragging');
      event.dataTransfer.effectAllowed='copy';
      event.dataTransfer.setData('text/plain',type);
    });
    item.addEventListener('dragend',()=>{
      S.dragType=null;
      item.classList.remove('citem-dragging');
      document.getElementById('diagram').classList.remove('dragover');
    });
  });
}

function initCanvasDrop(){
  const diagram=document.getElementById('diagram');
  const viewport=getCanvasViewport();
  if(!viewport){return;}
  viewport.addEventListener('dragover',event=>{
    if(!S.sysLoaded){return;}
    event.preventDefault();
    diagram.classList.add('dragover');
    event.dataTransfer.dropEffect='copy';
  });
  viewport.addEventListener('dragleave',event=>{
    if(event.target===viewport){diagram.classList.remove('dragover');}
  });
  viewport.addEventListener('drop',event=>{
    event.preventDefault();
    diagram.classList.remove('dragover');
    if(!S.sysLoaded){toast('请先导入系统模型','w');return;}
    const type=event.dataTransfer.getData('text/plain')||S.dragType;
    if(!COMPONENT_LIBRARY[type]){return;}
    const point=clientToStagePoint(event.clientX,event.clientY);
    createNode(type,point.x,point.y);
  });
}

function bindCanvasInteractions(){
  const viewport=getCanvasViewport();
  if(!viewport){return;}

  viewport.addEventListener('wheel',event=>{
    if(!S.sysLoaded){return;}
    event.preventDefault();
    setCanvasZoom(S.canvasScale+(event.deltaY<0?0.08:-0.08),event.clientX,event.clientY);
  },{passive:false});

  viewport.addEventListener('pointerdown',event=>{
    if(event.button!==0){return;}
    const target=event.target;
    const edgeInteractive=target?.closest?.('.edge-hit, .edge-path, .edge-label');
    const edgeId=edgeInteractive?.dataset?.edgeId||findNearestEdgeIdByClientPoint(event.clientX,event.clientY);
    if(target.closest('.blk')||target.closest('.node-port')||edgeInteractive){return;}
    if(edgeId){
      selectEdge(edgeId);
      return;
    }
    if(S.pendingConnection){
      clearPendingConnection();
      return;
    }
    CANVAS_PAN.active=true;
    CANVAS_PAN.engaged=false;
    CANVAS_PAN.clearSelectionOnPointerUp=Boolean(S.selBlk||S.selEdge);
    CANVAS_PAN.pointerId=event.pointerId;
    CANVAS_PAN.startX=event.clientX;
    CANVAS_PAN.startY=event.clientY;
    CANVAS_PAN.originX=S.canvasOffsetX;
    CANVAS_PAN.originY=S.canvasOffsetY;
    if(viewport.setPointerCapture){
      viewport.setPointerCapture(event.pointerId);
    }
  });

  viewport.addEventListener('pointermove',event=>{
    if(S.pendingConnection){
      const point=clientToStagePoint(event.clientX,event.clientY);
      S.pendingConnection.x=point.x;
      S.pendingConnection.y=point.y;
      renderEdges();
    }

    if(NODE_DRAG.active&&NODE_DRAG.pointerId===event.pointerId){
      const node=getNode(NODE_DRAG.nodeId);
      if(!node){return;}
      if(!NODE_DRAG.engaged){
        if(!movedBeyondPointerThreshold(NODE_DRAG.startX,NODE_DRAG.startY,event.clientX,event.clientY)){return;}
        NODE_DRAG.engaged=true;
        const dragEl=document.getElementById(`b-${NODE_DRAG.nodeId}`);
        if(dragEl){
          dragEl.classList.add('is-dragging');
          if(dragEl.setPointerCapture){
            dragEl.setPointerCapture(event.pointerId);
          }
        }
      }
      const deltaX=(event.clientX-NODE_DRAG.startX)/S.canvasScale;
      const deltaY=(event.clientY-NODE_DRAG.startY)/S.canvasScale;
      node.x=clamp(Math.round(NODE_DRAG.originX+deltaX),CANVAS_STAGE.nodePadding,CANVAS_STAGE.width-node.w-CANVAS_STAGE.nodePadding);
      node.y=clamp(Math.round(NODE_DRAG.originY+deltaY),CANVAS_STAGE.nodeMinY,CANVAS_STAGE.height-node.h-CANVAS_STAGE.nodePadding);
      updateNodePositionDOM(node);
      renderEdges();
      return;
    }

    if(CANVAS_PAN.active&&CANVAS_PAN.pointerId===event.pointerId){
      if(!CANVAS_PAN.engaged){
        if(!movedBeyondPointerThreshold(CANVAS_PAN.startX,CANVAS_PAN.startY,event.clientX,event.clientY)){return;}
        CANVAS_PAN.engaged=true;
        viewport.classList.add('panning');
      }
      S.canvasOffsetX=CANVAS_PAN.originX+(event.clientX-CANVAS_PAN.startX);
      S.canvasOffsetY=CANVAS_PAN.originY+(event.clientY-CANVAS_PAN.startY);
      clampCanvasOffset();
      applyCanvasTransform();
    }
  });

  const endPointerInteraction=event=>{
    if(NODE_DRAG.active&&NODE_DRAG.pointerId===event.pointerId){
      const draggedNode=getNode(NODE_DRAG.nodeId);
      const draggedEl=document.getElementById(`b-${NODE_DRAG.nodeId}`);
      const wasDragging=NODE_DRAG.engaged;
      if(draggedEl){
        draggedEl.classList.remove('is-dragging');
      }
      NODE_DRAG.active=false;
      NODE_DRAG.engaged=false;
      NODE_DRAG.pointerId=null;
      NODE_DRAG.nodeId='';
      NODE_DRAG.clickSuppressUntil=wasDragging?Date.now()+220:0;
      if(draggedNode&&wasDragging){renderEdges();}
    }

    if(CANVAS_PAN.active&&CANVAS_PAN.pointerId===event.pointerId){
      if(!CANVAS_PAN.engaged&&CANVAS_PAN.clearSelectionOnPointerUp){
        clearCanvasSelection();
      }
      CANVAS_PAN.active=false;
      CANVAS_PAN.engaged=false;
      CANVAS_PAN.clearSelectionOnPointerUp=false;
      CANVAS_PAN.pointerId=null;
      viewport.classList.remove('panning');
    }
  };

  viewport.addEventListener('pointerup',endPointerInteraction);
  viewport.addEventListener('pointercancel',endPointerInteraction);

  const runtimeListeners=getRuntimeListenerStore();
  if(runtimeListeners.canvasWindowKeydown){
    window.removeEventListener('keydown',runtimeListeners.canvasWindowKeydown);
  }
  runtimeListeners.canvasWindowKeydown=event=>{
    if(event.key==='Escape'&&S.pendingConnection){
      clearPendingConnection();
      return;
    }
    const active=document.activeElement;
    const editing=active&&(
      active.tagName==='INPUT'||
      active.tagName==='TEXTAREA'||
      active.tagName==='SELECT'||
      active.isContentEditable
    );
    if((event.key==='Delete'||event.key==='Backspace')&&!editing&&!document.querySelector('.overlay.open')&&(S.selBlk||S.selEdge)){
      event.preventDefault();
      deleteCurrentSelection();
    }
  };
  window.addEventListener('keydown',runtimeListeners.canvasWindowKeydown);

  if(runtimeListeners.canvasWindowResize){
    window.removeEventListener('resize',runtimeListeners.canvasWindowResize);
  }
  runtimeListeners.canvasWindowResize=()=>{
    clampCanvasOffset();
    applyCanvasTransform();
  };
  window.addEventListener('resize',runtimeListeners.canvasWindowResize);
}

function buildPythonBindingPortRows(items,kind){
  if(!items.length){
    return '<div class="props-help">当前没有可用端口</div>';
  }
  return items.map(item=>{
    const status=kind==='inputs'
      ?(item.connected?'<span class="pv pv-ok">已连接</span>':'<span class="pv pv-fault">未连接</span>')
      :'<span class="pv pv-ok">已暴露</span>';
    const title=escapeHtml(item.displayName||item.varName||'-');
    const type=escapeHtml(item.type||'any');
    const note=item.comment?`<div class="props-help">${escapeHtml(item.comment)}</div>`:'';
    const defaultRow=kind==='inputs'&&item.default!==null&&item.default!==undefined&&item.default!==''
      ?`<div class="prow"><span class="pk">默认值<</span><span class="pv">${escapeHtml(item.default)}<</span></div>`
      :'';
    return `
      <div class="pgroup pgroup--compact">
        <div class="prow"><span class="pk">${title}<</span>${status}</div>
        <div class="prow"><span class="pk">类型<</span><span class="pv">${type}<</span></div>
        ${defaultRow}
        ${note}
      </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

function buildFlowBlockFields(node){
  const binding=ensureFlowNodePythonBinding(node);
  const bound=binding.bound;
  const bindingSummary=bound
    ?`
      <div class="pgroup">
        <div class="pglbl">Python 绑定</div>
        <div class="prow"><span class="pk">文件<</span><span class="pv">${escapeHtml(binding.fileName||'-')}<</span></div>
        <div class="prow"><span class="pk">模块<</span><span class="pv">${escapeHtml(binding.moduleName||'-')}<</span></div>
        <div class="prow"><span class="pk">入口函数<</span><span class="pv">${escapeHtml(binding.entryFunction||'process')}<</span></div>
        <div class="prow"><span class="pk">端口摘要<</span><span class="pv">${escapeHtml(getPythonBindingSummary(node))}<</span></div>
        ${binding.description?`<div class="props-help">${escapeHtml(binding.description)}</div>`:''}
      </div>
      <div class="pgroup">
        <div class="pglbl">输入端口</div>
        ${buildPythonBindingPortRows(binding.portMapping.inputs,'inputs')}
      </div>
      <div class="pgroup">
        <div class="pglbl">输出端口</div>
        ${buildPythonBindingPortRows(binding.portMapping.outputs,'outputs')}
      </div>
      <div class="pgroup">
        <div class="pglbl">中间变量</div>
        ${buildPythonBindingPortRows(binding.portMapping.middleVars,'middleVars')}
      </div>`
    :`
      <div class="pgroup">
        <div class="pglbl">Python 绑定</div>
        <div class="props-help">当前流程块尚未绑定 Python 文件。绑定后将按函数输入、输出和 @observable 中间变量自动生成端口。</div>
      </div>`;
  const legacyFields=bound?`
      <div style="display:none">
        <input id="prop-inputName" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.inputName)}">
        <select id="prop-inputFormat">${buildSelectOptions(PORT_FORMATS,node.props.inputFormat)}</select>
        <input id="prop-outputName" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.outputName)}">
        <select id="prop-outputFormat">${buildSelectOptions(PORT_FORMATS,node.props.outputFormat)}</select>
      </div>`:`
      <div class="props-field"><label>输入名称</label><input id="prop-inputName" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.inputName)}"></div>
      <div class="props-row">
        <div class="props-field"><label>输入类型</label><select id="prop-inputFormat">${buildSelectOptions(PORT_FORMATS,node.props.inputFormat)}</select></div>
        <div class="props-field"><label>输出类型</label><select id="prop-outputFormat">${buildSelectOptions(PORT_FORMATS,node.props.outputFormat)}</select></div>
      </div>
      <div class="props-field"><label>输出名称</label><input id="prop-outputName" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.outputName)}"></div>
      <div class="props-help">未绑定 Python 时，流程块按单输入单输出直通模块工作。</div>`;
  return `
    <div class="pgroup">
      <div class="pglbl">流程块设置</div>
      <div class="props-field"><label>模块名称</label><input id="prop-name" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.name)}"></div>
      ${legacyFields}
    </div>
    ${bindingSummary}`;
}

function renderPropertyPanel(node){
  const pe=document.getElementById('pe');
  const pd=document.getElementById('pd');
  if(!node){
    pe.style.display='flex';
    pd.style.display='none';
    pd.innerHTML='';
    return;
  }

  if(node.sourceNodeId&&node.targetNodeId&&!node.type){
    const sourceNode=getNode(node.sourceNodeId);
    const targetNode=getNode(node.targetNodeId);
    const edgeLabel=node.lineType==='can'?'CAN 总线':'普通连接线';
    const sourceName=sourceNode?.props?.name||node.sourceNodeId;
    const targetName=targetNode?.props?.name||node.targetNodeId;
    const sourcePortName=node.sourcePort?.displayName||node.sourcePort?.varName||`#${(node.sourcePortIndex||0)+1}`;
    const targetPortName=node.targetPort?.displayName||node.targetPort?.varName||`#${(node.targetPortIndex||0)+1}`;
    const protocolFault=node.injectedFault?.layer==='protocol'?node.injectedFault:null;
    pe.style.display='none';
    pd.style.display='block';
    pd.innerHTML=`
      <div class="pgroup">
        <div class="props-title">${edgeLabel}</div>
        <div class="props-sub">画布连线 ${node.id.replace('edge-','#')}</div>
      </div>
      <div class="pgroup">
        <div class="pglbl">连接信息</div>
        <div class="prow"><span class="pk">连线类型<</span><span class="pv">${edgeLabel}<</span></div>
        <div class="prow"><span class="pk">源节点<</span><span class="pv">${escapeHtml(sourceName)}<</span></div>
        <div class="prow"><span class="pk">源端口<</span><span class="pv">${escapeHtml(sourcePortName)}<</span></div>
        <div class="prow"><span class="pk">目标节点<</span><span class="pv">${escapeHtml(targetName)}<</span></div>
        <div class="prow"><span class="pk">目标端口<</span><span class="pv">${escapeHtml(targetPortName)}<</span></div>
        <div class="prow"><span class="pk">协议状态<</span><span class="pv ${protocolFault?'pv-fault':'pv-ok'}">${protocolFault?'已注入协议故障':'正常'}<</span></div>
        ${protocolFault?`<div class="prow"><span class="pk">协议故障<</span><span class="pv pv-fault">${escapeHtml(protocolFault.name)}<</span></div>`:''}
      </div>
      <div class="props-form">
        <div class="pgroup">
          <div class="props-help">${isProtocolInjectableEdge(node)?'当前连线为 CAN 总线，可在此导入协议层故障；普通连接线暂不支持协议注入。':'当前选中的是一条独立连线，可直接删除，不影响其他模块。'}</div>
        </div>
        <div class="props-actions">
          ${isProtocolInjectableEdge(node)?`<button class="props-secondary props-protocol-action" onclick="openProtocolFaultImport()">${protocolFault?'更换协议故障':'导入协议故障'}</button>`:''}
          <button class="props-danger" onclick="deleteSelectedEdge()">删除连线</button>
        </div>
      </div>`;
    return;
  }

  const meta=COMPONENT_LIBRARY[node.type];
  const fault=S.faultedBlks.includes(node.id)||Boolean(node.injectedFault);
  const pythonBound=isPythonBoundFlowBlock(node);
  const simulationPackageRows=pythonBound
    ?buildSimulationBlockPackageRows(node)
    :'';
  let fields='';

  if(node.type==='signal_source'){
    fields=`
      <div class="pgroup">
        <div class="pglbl">信号瀹氫箟</div>
        <div class="props-field"><label>模块名称</label><input id="prop-name" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.name)}"></div>
        <div class="props-row">
          <div class="props-field"><label>信号类型</label><select id="prop-waveType">${buildSelectOptions(['正弦','阶跃','常值'],node.props.waveType)}</select></div>
          <div class="props-field"><label>输出鏍煎紡</label><select id="prop-outputFormat">${buildSelectOptions(PORT_FORMATS,node.props.outputFormat)}</select></div>
        </div>
        <div class="props-row">
