  }else if(node.type==='flow_block'){
    fields=buildFlowBlockFields(node);
          <div class="props-field"><label>输出鏍煎紡</label><select id="prop-outputFormat">${buildSelectOptions(PORT_FORMATS,node.props.outputFormat)}</select></div>
        </div>
        <div class="props-field"><label>输出名称</label><input id="prop-outputName" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.outputName)}"></div>
        <div class="props-help">流程块用于定义系统中的输入、输出以及接口格式。</div>
      </div>`;
  }else if(node.type==='simulation_block'){
    fields=buildSimulationBlockFields(node);
  }else if(node.type.startsWith('fault_')){
    fields=`
      <div class="pgroup">
        <div class="pglbl">故障参数</div>
        <div class="props-field"><label>模块名称</label><input id="prop-name" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.name)}"></div>
        <div class="props-field"><label>故障类型</label><input id="prop-faultType" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.faultType)}"></div>
        <div class="props-row">
          <div class="props-field"><label>作用层级</label><select id="prop-layer">${buildSelectOptions(['物理层','电气层','协议层'],node.props.layer)}</select></div>
          <div class="props-field"><label>触发方式</label><select id="prop-trigger">${buildSelectOptions(['持续','渐变','瞬态','间歇'],node.props.trigger)}</select></div>
        </div>
      </div>`;
  }else if(node.type.startsWith('instrument_')){
    fields=`
      <div class="pgroup">
        <div class="pglbl">观测配置</div>
        <div class="props-field"><label>模块名称</label><input id="prop-name" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.name)}"></div>
        <div class="props-field"><label>观测类型</label><input id="prop-instrumentType" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.instrumentType)}"></div>
        <div class="props-row">
          <div class="props-field"><label>采样率</label><input id="prop-sampleRate" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.sampleRate)}"></div>
          <div class="props-field"><label>观测信号</label><input id="prop-signal" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.signal)}"></div>
        </div>
      </div>`;
  }else{
    fields=`
      <div class="pgroup">
        <div class="pglbl">杩炴帴瀹氫箟</div>
        <div class="props-field"><label>缁勪欢名称</label><input id="prop-name" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.name)}"></div>
        <div class="props-field"><label>杩炴帴类型</label><input id="prop-linkType" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.linkType)}"></div>
        <div class="props-row">
          <div class="props-field"><label>璧风偣端口</label><input id="prop-sourcePort" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.sourcePort)}"></div>
          <div class="props-field"><label>缁堢偣端口</label><input id="prop-targetPort" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.targetPort)}"></div>
        </div>
      </div>`;
  }

  pe.style.display='none';
  pd.style.display='block';
  const faultSummary=node.injectedFault
    ?`<div class="prow"><span class="pk">电气故障<</span><span class="pv pv-fault">${escapeHtml(node.injectedFault.name)}<</span></div>`
    :'';

  pd.innerHTML=`
    <div class="pgroup">
      <div class="props-title">${escapeHtml(node.props.name)}</div>
      <div class="props-sub">${pythonBound?(escapeHtml(node.pythonBinding?.fileName||'')+' - '):''}${meta.label} - Node ${node.id.replace('node-','#')}</div>
    </div>
    <div class="pgroup">
      <div class="pglbl">当前状态</div>
      <div class="prow"><span class="pk">鑺傜偣绫诲埆<</span><span class="pv">${meta.label}<</span></div>
      <div class="prow"><span class="pk">状态<</span><span class="pv ${fault?'pv-fault':'pv-ok'}">${fault?'已绑定故障':'正常'}<</span></div>
      ${pythonBound?`<div class="prow"><span class="pk">Python<</span><span class="pv pv-ok">${escapeHtml(getPythonBindingSummary(node))}<</span></div>`:''}
      ${simulationPackageRows}
      ${faultSummary}
    </div>
    <div class="props-form">
      ${fields}
      <div class="props-actions">
        ${node.type==='flow_block'?`<button class="props-secondary" onclick="openPythonBindingDialog('${node.id}')">${pythonBound?'Rebind Python':'Bind Python File'}</button>`:''}
        ${node.type==='flow_block'&&pythonBound?`<button class="props-secondary" onclick="unbindPythonBinding('${node.id}')">Unbind Python</button>`:''}
        ${isElectricalInjectableType(node.type)?`<button class="props-secondary props-fault-action" onclick="openElectricalFaultImport()">${node.injectedFault?'更换故障':'导入故障'}</button>`:''}
        <button class="props-save" onclick="saveSelectedNode()">保存设置</button>
        <button class="props-danger" onclick="deleteSelectedNode()">删除模块</button>
      </div>
    </div>`;
}

function saveSelectedNode(){
  const node=getNode(S.selBlk);
  if(!node){return;}
  if(node.type==='signal_source'){
    node.props.name=document.getElementById('prop-name').value.trim()||node.props.name;
    node.props.waveType=document.getElementById('prop-waveType').value;
    node.props.outputFormat=document.getElementById('prop-outputFormat').value;
    node.props.amplitude=document.getElementById('prop-amplitude').value.trim()||node.props.amplitude;
    node.props.frequency=document.getElementById('prop-frequency').value.trim()||node.props.frequency;
  }else if(node.type==='flow_block'){
    node.props.name=document.getElementById('prop-name').value.trim()||node.props.name;
    if(!isPythonBoundFlowBlock(node)){
      node.props.inputName=document.getElementById('prop-inputName').value.trim()||'\u8f93\u5165\u4fe1\u53f7';
      node.props.inputFormat=document.getElementById('prop-inputFormat').value;
      node.props.outputName=document.getElementById('prop-outputName').value.trim()||'\u8f93\u51fa\u4fe1\u53f7';
      node.props.outputFormat=document.getElementById('prop-outputFormat').value;
    }
  }else if(node.type==='simulation_block'){
    node.props.name=document.getElementById('prop-name').value.trim()||node.props.name;
    node.props.moduleType=document.getElementById('prop-moduleType').value;
    node.props.inputs=readSimulationInterfaceRows('\u8f93\u5165');
    node.props.outputs=readSimulationInterfaceRows('\u8f93\u51fa');
    node.props.middleVars=readSimulationInterfaceRows('\u4e2d\u95f4\u91cf');
    normalizeSimulationInterfaces(node.props);
    node.props.inputs=normalizeSimulationInterfaceList(
      node.props.inputs.slice(0,clampInterfaceCount(document.getElementById('sim-input-count')?.value,SIM_INTERFACE_LIMITS.inputs)),
      '\u8f93\u5165',
      node.props.inputs[0]?.type||'\u6807\u91cf',
      clampInterfaceCount(document.getElementById('sim-input-count')?.value,SIM_INTERFACE_LIMITS.inputs)
    );
    node.props.outputs=normalizeSimulationInterfaceList(
      node.props.outputs.slice(0,clampInterfaceCount(document.getElementById('sim-output-count')?.value,SIM_INTERFACE_LIMITS.outputs)),
      '\u8f93\u51fa',
      node.props.outputs[0]?.type||'\u6807\u91cf',
      clampInterfaceCount(document.getElementById('sim-output-count')?.value,SIM_INTERFACE_LIMITS.outputs)
    );
    node.props.middleVars=normalizeSimulationInterfaceList(
      node.props.middleVars.slice(0,clampInterfaceCount(document.getElementById('sim-middle-count')?.value,SIM_INTERFACE_LIMITS.middleVars)),
      '\u4e2d\u95f4\u91cf',
      node.props.middleVars[0]?.type||'\u6807\u91cf',
      clampInterfaceCount(document.getElementById('sim-middle-count')?.value,SIM_INTERFACE_LIMITS.middleVars)
    );
    node.props.ffunctionNote=document.getElementById('prop-ffunctionNote').value.trim()||'\u5f53\u524d\u9884\u7559 Python \u51fd\u6570\u63a5\u53e3\uff0c\u53ef\u5728\u540e\u7eed\u5bfc\u5165\u51fd\u6570\u5b9a\u4e49\u3002';
    applyNodeGeometry(node);
    pruneInvalidEdgesForNode(node);
  }else if(node.type.startsWith('fault_')){
    node.props.name=document.getElementById('prop-name').value.trim()||node.props.name;
    node.props.faultType=document.getElementById('prop-faultType').value.trim()||node.props.faultType;
    node.props.layer=document.getElementById('prop-layer').value;
    node.props.trigger=document.getElementById('prop-trigger').value;
  }else if(node.type.startsWith('instrument_')){
    node.props.name=document.getElementById('prop-name').value.trim()||node.props.name;
    node.props.instrumentType=document.getElementById('prop-instrumentType').value.trim()||node.props.instrumentType;
    node.props.sampleRate=document.getElementById('prop-sampleRate').value.trim()||node.props.sampleRate;
    node.props.signal=document.getElementById('prop-signal').value.trim()||node.props.signal;
  }else{
    node.props.name=document.getElementById('prop-name').value.trim()||node.props.name;
    node.props.linkType=document.getElementById('prop-linkType').value.trim()||node.props.linkType;
    node.props.sourcePort=document.getElementById('prop-sourcePort').value.trim()||node.props.sourcePort;
    node.props.targetPort=document.getElementById('prop-targetPort').value.trim()||node.props.targetPort;
  }
  markTopologyDirty(getMutationScopeForType(node.type));
  renderModelNodes();
  renderPropertyPanel(node);
  syncConfigTargets(node.id);
  updateUI();
  toast(`模块「${node.props.name}」设置已保存`,'s');
}

// ─── 鍒嗙粍折叠 ───
function toggleGroup(id){
  const body=document.getElementById(id);
  const arr=document.getElementById('arr-'+id);
  const open=body.style.display!=='none';
  body.style.display=open?'none':'block';
  arr.classList.toggle('open',!open);
}

// ─── 右上角按钮 ───
function doImportSys(){
  const btn=document.getElementById('btn-imp-sys');
  btn.textContent='导入中…';
  btn.disabled=true;
  setTimeout(()=>{
    let restored=false;
    btn.textContent='导入系统模型';
    btn.disabled=false;
    S.sysLoaded=true;
    S.step=1;
    document.getElementById('empty').style.display='none';
    document.getElementById('diagram').classList.add('on');
    handleCanvasZoomReset();
    try{
      const raw=window.localStorage?.getItem(WORKBENCH_STORAGE_KEY);
      if(raw){
        restoreSystemModelSnapshot(JSON.parse(raw));
        S.systemSaved=true;
        S.step=S.modelNodes.length?2:1;
        restored=S.modelNodes.length>0;
      }else{
        clearPendingConnection();
        renderModelNodes();
        renderPropertyPanel(null);
      }
    }catch(error){
      console.warn('Failed to restore saved system model',error);
      clearPendingConnection();
      renderModelNodes();
      renderPropertyPanel(null);
    }
    toast(restored?'已恢复已保存的系统模型':'系统建模画布已就绪，请拖拽组件开始建模','s');
    updateUI();
  },1000);
}

function doSaveSys(){
  if(!S.sysLoaded){toast('请先导入系统模型','w');return;}
  if(S.modelNodes.length===0){toast('请至少添加一个组件后再保存','w');return;}
  try{
    const snapshot=createSystemModelSnapshot();
    window.localStorage?.setItem(WORKBENCH_STORAGE_KEY,JSON.stringify(snapshot));
  }catch(error){
    console.warn('Failed to persist system model snapshot',error);
    toast('系统模型保存失败，请稍后重试','w');
    return;
  }
  S.systemSaved=true;
  S.step=2;
  toast('系统模型已保存','s');
  updateUI();
}

function doImportFault(){
  if(!S.sysLoaded){toast('请先导入系统模型','w');return;}
  if(getLoadedSystemNodeCount()===0){toast('请先在系统建模页拖入组件','w');return;}
  renderFaultCatalogList();
  openOv('ov-ifm');
}


function doSaveRes(){
  if(!S.simDone){toast('请先完成仿真后再保存结果','w');return;}
  toast('仿真结果已保存','s');
}

// ─── 导入故障妯″瀷弹窗 ───
function simulateFileImport(){
  toast('本地故障模型文件导入口已预留，当前可先使用模板库和示例模型完成流程。','w');
}

function selectFaultFile(el){
  const id=el?.dataset?.faultId;
  if(id){selectFaultCatalogModel(id);}
}

function updateSelectedTplSummary(){
  document.getElementById('sel-cnt').textContent=`已选 ${S.selTpls.length} 个故障模板`;
  document.getElementById('sel-list').innerHTML=S.selTpls.length===0
    ?'<div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--textd);text-align:center;margin-top:6px">暂无</div>'
    :S.selTpls.map(item=>`<div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--purple);padding:3px 6px;border-radius:3px;background:var(--purple-bg);margin-bottom:2px;border:1px solid #ddd6fe">• ${item.name}</div>`).join('');
}

function openFaultBuild(defaultLayer='physical'){
  curCat=defaultLayer;
  document.querySelectorAll('.tpl-cat').forEach((el,index)=>{
    const cat=index===0?'physical':index===1?'electrical':'protocol';
    el.classList.toggle('on',cat===curCat);
  });
  renderTpls(curCat);
  closeOv('ov-ifm');
  openOv('ov-tpl');
}

function backToImport(){
  closeOv('ov-tpl');
  renderFaultCatalogList();
  openOv('ov-ifm');
}

function confirmImportFault(){
  const selected=getFaultCatalogModel(S.selectedFaultCatalogId);
  if(!selected){toast('请先选择一个故障模型','w');return;}
  ensureImportedFaultModel(selected);
  closeOv('ov-ifm');
  renderFaultCatalogList();
  toast(`故障模型“${selected.name}”已导入工作区`,'s');
  updateUI();
}

// ─── 模板库 ───
function setCat(el,cat){
  document.querySelectorAll('.tpl-cat').forEach(e=>e.classList.remove('on'));
  el.classList.add('on');curCat=cat;renderTpls(cat);
}

function renderTpls(cat){
  const g=document.getElementById('tgrid');g.innerHTML='';
  (TPLS[cat]||[]).forEach(t=>{
    const sel=S.selTpls.some(s=>s.id===t.id);
    const d=document.createElement('div');
    d.className='tcard'+(sel?' on':'');
    d.innerHTML=`<div class="tcard-name">${t.name}</div>
      <div class="tcard-desc">${t.desc}</div>
      <div class="tcard-tags">${t.tags.map(tag=>`<span class="ttag" style="background:color-mix(in srgb,${t.c} 10%,#fff);color:${t.c};border:1px solid color-mix(in srgb,${t.c} 20%,#e5e7eb)">${tag}<</span>`).join('')}</div>`;
    d.onclick=()=>toggleTpl({...t,layer:cat},d);
    g.appendChild(d);
  });
  showTplDetail({...((TPLS[cat]||[])[0]||{}),layer:cat});
}

function toggleTpl(t,card){
  const i=S.selTpls.findIndex(s=>s.id===t.id);
  if(i>=0){S.selTpls.splice(i,1);card.classList.remove('on');}
  else{S.selTpls.push(t);card.classList.add('on');}
  updateSelectedTplSummary();
  showTplDetail(t);
}

function showTplDetail(t){
  if(!t?.id){
    document.getElementById('tdetail').innerHTML='<div class="tdph">→ 选择模板查看详情</div>';
    return;
  }
  document.getElementById('tdetail').innerHTML=`
    <div class="tdtitle">${t.name}</div>
    <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text2);line-height:1.5;margin-bottom:10px">${t.desc}</div>
    <div class="tdlbl">故障层级</div><div class="tdval">${getLayerLabel(t.layer)}</div>
    <div class="tdlbl">故障类别</div><div class="tdval">${t.tags[0]}</div>
    <div class="tdlbl">持续特性</div><div class="tdval">${t.tags[1]||'—'}</div>
    <div class="tdlbl">适用场景</div>
    <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text2);margin-top:3px;line-height:1.5">系统建模模块 / 信号链路<br>故障传播与退化仿真</div>
    <div class="tdlbl">骞呭害鑼冨洿</div><div class="tdval">卤0.01 ~ 卤10.0</div>`;
}

function confirmFM(){
  if(S.selTpls.length===0){toast('请至少选择一个故障模板','w');return;}
  const createdModels=S.selTpls.map(item=>{
    const model={
      id:`fm-${item.layer}-${item.id}`,
      name:item.name,
      layer:item.layer,
      desc:item.desc,
      tags:item.tags,
      createdAt:new Date().toLocaleDateString('zh-CN'),
      origin:'template',
      templateId:item.id
    };
    return upsertAvailableFaultModel(model);
  });
  if(createdModels[0]){
    S.selectedFaultCatalogId=createdModels[0].id;
  }
  renderFaultCatalogList();
  closeOv('ov-tpl');
  openOv('ov-ifm');
  toast(`已新建${S.selTpls.length}个故障模型，返回导入页面继续入库`,'s');
  S.selTpls=[];
  updateSelectedTplSummary();
  updateUI();
}

function getCurrentElectricalSelection(){
  if(S.injectSelectionMode==='imported'){
    return getImportedFaultModel(S.injectSelectionId);
  }
  if(S.injectSelectionMode==='template'){
    return (TPLS.electrical||[]).find(item=>item.id===S.injectSelectionId)||null;
  }
  return null;
}

function selectElectricalInject(mode,id){
  S.injectSelectionMode=mode;
  S.injectSelectionId=id;
  renderElectricalInjectModal();
}

function renderElectricalInjectModal(){
  const target=getNode(S.injectTargetId);
  const importedList=document.getElementById('einj-import-list');
  const targetCard=document.getElementById('einj-target');
  const grid=document.getElementById('einj-template-grid');
  const detail=document.getElementById('einj-detail-body');
  const hint=document.getElementById('einj-foot-hint');
  if(!importedList||!targetCard||!grid||!detail||!hint){return;}

  if(!target){
    importedList.innerHTML='';
    targetCard.innerHTML='';
    grid.innerHTML='';
    detail.innerHTML='<div class="einj-empty">未选择目标模块。</div>';
    hint.textContent='请选择一个流程块或仿真块。';
    return;
  }

  const importedElectrical=S.importedFaultModels.filter(model=>model.layer==='electrical');
  if(importedElectrical.length===0){
    importedList.innerHTML='<div class="ifm-empty">当前还没有已导入的电气层故障模型。可先从右上角导入，或直接在右侧模板库中选择并注入。</div>';
  }else{
    importedList.innerHTML=importedElectrical.map(model=>`
      <div class="ifm-item${S.injectSelectionMode==='imported'&&S.injectSelectionId===model.id?' on':''}" onclick="selectElectricalInject('imported','${model.id}')">
        <div class="ifm-icon">⚡</div>
        <div style="min-width:0;flex:1">
          <div class="ifm-name">${escapeHtml(model.name)}</div>
          <div class="ifm-meta">${escapeHtml(buildFaultCatalogMeta(model))}</div>
        </div>
        <span class="ifm-state">已导入</span>
      </div>`).join('');
  }

  targetCard.innerHTML=`
    <div class="einj-target-kicker">目标模块</div>
    <div class="einj-target-name">${escapeHtml(target.props.name)}</div>
    <div class="einj-target-sub">电气层故障将以模块内部编辑的形式作用在当前 ${COMPONENT_LIBRARY[target.type].label} 上，无需额外拖拽故障块。</div>
    ${target.injectedFault?`<div class="einj-current">已注入：${escapeHtml(target.injectedFault.name)}</div>`:''}`;

  grid.innerHTML=(TPLS.electrical||[]).map(template=>`
    <div class="einj-card${S.injectSelectionMode==='template'&&S.injectSelectionId===template.id?' on':''}" onclick="selectElectricalInject('template','${template.id}')">
      <div class="einj-card-name">${escapeHtml(template.name)}</div>
      <div class="einj-card-desc">${escapeHtml(template.desc)}</div>
      <div class="einj-tags">${template.tags.map(tag=>`<span class="einj-tag">${escapeHtml(tag)}<</span>`).join('')}</div>
    </div>`).join('');

  const selected=getCurrentElectricalSelection();
  if(!selected){
    detail.innerHTML='<div class="einj-empty">先从左侧已导入模型或中间模板库中选择一个电气层故障，再执行导入并注入。</div>';
    hint.textContent='请选择一个电气层故障模型。';
    return;
  }

  const selectedName=selected.name;
  const selectedDesc=selected.desc||'未提供说明';
  const selectedTags=selected.tags||[];
  const selectedLayer=S.injectSelectionMode==='imported'?getLayerLabel(selected.layer):'电气层模板';
  const sourceLabel=S.injectSelectionMode==='imported'?'已导入模型':'模板直注';
  detail.innerHTML=`
    <div class="tdtitle">${escapeHtml(selectedName)}</div>
    <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text2);line-height:1.6;margin-bottom:10px">${escapeHtml(selectedDesc)}</div>
    <div class="einj-row"><span>来源<</span><span>${sourceLabel}<</span></div>
    <div class="einj-row"><span>层级<</span><span>${selectedLayer}<</span></div>
    <div class="einj-row"><span>作用对象<</span><span>${escapeHtml(target.props.name)}<</span></div>
    <div class="tdlbl">标签</div>
    <div class="einj-tags" style="margin-top:6px">${selectedTags.map(tag=>`<span class="einj-tag">${escapeHtml(tag)}<</span>`).join('')}</div>
    <div class="tdlbl">注入璇存槑</div>
    <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text2);line-height:1.7;margin-top:4px">确认后将把该电气层故障绑定到当前模块，模块卡片会标红，并纳入后续仿真分析。</div>`;
  hint.textContent=`已选：${selectedName}，确认后将注入到 ${target.props.name}`;
}

function openElectricalFaultImport(){
  const node=getNode(S.selBlk);
  if(!node||!isElectricalInjectableType(node.type)){return;}
  S.injectTargetId=node.id;
  if(node.injectedFault&&getImportedFaultModel(node.injectedFault.modelId)){
    S.injectSelectionMode='imported';
    S.injectSelectionId=node.injectedFault.modelId;
  }else{
    S.injectSelectionMode='';
    S.injectSelectionId='';
  }
  renderElectricalInjectModal();
  openOv('ov-elec');
}

function confirmElectricalFaultInjection(){
  const target=getNode(S.injectTargetId);
  if(!target){toast('当前没有可注入的目标模块','w');return;}
  const selected=getCurrentElectricalSelection();
  if(!selected){toast('请先选择一个电气层故障模型','w');return;}

  let faultModel=selected;
  if(S.injectSelectionMode==='template'){
    const existing=S.availableFaultModels.find(model=>model.layer==='electrical'&&(model.templateId===selected.id||model.name===selected.name));
    faultModel=existing||upsertAvailableFaultModel({
      id:`fm-electrical-${selected.id}`,
      name:selected.name,
      layer:'electrical',
      desc:selected.desc,
      tags:selected.tags,
      createdAt:new Date().toLocaleDateString('zh-CN'),
      origin:'template',
      templateId:selected.id
    });
  }

  const importedModel=ensureImportedFaultModel(faultModel);
  target.injectedFault={
    modelId:importedModel.id,
    name:importedModel.name,
    layer:'electrical',
    tags:cloneDefaults(importedModel.tags||[]),
    desc:importedModel.desc||''
  };
  if(!S.faultedBlks.includes(target.id)){
    S.faultedBlks.push(target.id);
  }
  renderFaultCatalogList();
  markTopologyDirty('fault');
  closeOv('ov-elec');
  renderModelNodes();
  renderPropertyPanel(target);
  updateUI();
  toast(`已将电气层故障「${importedModel.name}」注入到 ${target.props.name}`,'s');
}

function getCurrentProtocolSelection(){
  if(S.protocolInjectSelectionMode==='imported'){
    return getImportedFaultModel(S.protocolInjectSelectionId);
  }
  if(S.protocolInjectSelectionMode==='template'){
    return (TPLS.protocol||[]).find(item=>item.id===S.protocolInjectSelectionId)||null;
  }
  return null;
}

function selectProtocolInject(mode,id){
  S.protocolInjectSelectionMode=mode;
  S.protocolInjectSelectionId=id;
  renderProtocolInjectModal();
}

function renderProtocolInjectModal(){
  const target=getEdge(S.protocolInjectTargetId);
  const importedList=document.getElementById('pinj-import-list');
  const targetCard=document.getElementById('pinj-target');
  const grid=document.getElementById('pinj-template-grid');
  const detail=document.getElementById('pinj-detail-body');
  const hint=document.getElementById('pinj-foot-hint');
  if(!importedList||!targetCard||!grid||!detail||!hint){return;}

  if(!target||!isProtocolInjectableEdge(target)){
    importedList.innerHTML='';
    targetCard.innerHTML='';
    grid.innerHTML='';
    detail.innerHTML='<div class="einj-empty">未选择可注入的 CAN 总线。</div>';
    hint.textContent='请选择一条 CAN 总线。';
    return;
  }

  const sourceNode=getNode(target.sourceNodeId);
  const targetNode=getNode(target.targetNodeId);
  const sourceName=sourceNode?.props?.name||target.sourceNodeId;
  const targetName=targetNode?.props?.name||target.targetNodeId;
  const importedProtocol=S.importedFaultModels.filter(model=>model.layer==='protocol');

  if(importedProtocol.length===0){
    importedList.innerHTML='<div class="ifm-empty">当前还没有已导入的CAN 协议层故障模型。可先从右上角导入，或直接在右侧模板库中选择并注入。</div>';
  }else{
    importedList.innerHTML=importedProtocol.map(model=>`
      <div class="ifm-item${S.protocolInjectSelectionMode==='imported'&&S.protocolInjectSelectionId===model.id?' on':''}" onclick="selectProtocolInject('imported','${model.id}')">
        <div class="ifm-icon">协</div>
        <div style="min-width:0;flex:1">
          <div class="ifm-name">${escapeHtml(model.name)}</div>
          <div class="ifm-meta">${escapeHtml(buildFaultCatalogMeta(model))}</div>
        </div>
        <span class="ifm-state">已导入</span>
      </div>`).join('');
  }

  targetCard.innerHTML=`
    <div class="einj-target-kicker">目标连线</div>
    <div class="einj-target-name">CAN 总线</div>
    <div class="einj-target-sub">连接 ${escapeHtml(sourceName)} → ${escapeHtml(targetName)}。协议层故障会直接作用在这条 CAN 通信链路上。</div>
    ${target.injectedFault?`<div class="einj-current">已注入：${escapeHtml(target.injectedFault.name)}</div>`:''}`;

  grid.innerHTML=(TPLS.protocol||[]).map(template=>`
    <div class="einj-card${S.protocolInjectSelectionMode==='template'&&S.protocolInjectSelectionId===template.id?' on':''}" onclick="selectProtocolInject('template','${template.id}')">
      <div class="einj-card-name">${escapeHtml(template.name)}</div>
      <div class="einj-card-desc">${escapeHtml(template.desc)}</div>
      <div class="einj-tags">${template.tags.map(tag=>`<span class="einj-tag">${escapeHtml(tag)}<</span>`).join('')}</div>
    </div>`).join('');

  const selected=getCurrentProtocolSelection();
  if(!selected){
    detail.innerHTML='<div class="einj-empty">先从左侧已导入模型或中间模板库中选择一个CAN 协议层故障，再执行导入并注入。</div>';
    hint.textContent='请选择一个 CAN 协议层故障模型。';
    return;
  }

  const selectedName=selected.name;
  const selectedDesc=selected.desc||'未提供说明';
  const selectedTags=selected.tags||[];
  const selectedKind=selected.faultKind||selected.tags?.[0]||'协议层故障';
  const sourceLabel=S.protocolInjectSelectionMode==='imported'?'已导入模型':'模板直注';
  detail.innerHTML=`
    <div class="tdtitle">${escapeHtml(selectedName)}</div>
    <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text2);line-height:1.6;margin-bottom:10px">${escapeHtml(selectedDesc)}</div>
    <div class="einj-row"><span>来源<</span><span>${sourceLabel}<</span></div>
    <div class="einj-row"><span>层级<</span><span>协议层</span></div>
    <div class="einj-row"><span>故障类型<</span><span>${escapeHtml(selectedKind)}<</span></div>
    <div class="einj-row"><span>作用对象<</span><span>CAN 总线<</span></div>
    <div class="tdlbl">标签</div>
    <div class="einj-tags" style="margin-top:6px">${selectedTags.map(tag=>`<span class="einj-tag">${escapeHtml(tag)}<</span>`).join('')}</div>
    <div class="tdlbl">注入璇存槑</div>
    <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text2);line-height:1.7;margin-top:4px">确认后将把该协议层故障绑定到当前 CAN 总线上，连线会标红并切换为虚线，用于后续仿真分析。</div>`;
  hint.textContent=`已选：${selectedName}，确认后将注入到当前 CAN 总线`;
}

function openProtocolFaultImport(){
  const edge=getEdge(S.selEdge);
  if(!isProtocolInjectableEdge(edge)){
    toast('当前仅支持对 CAN 总线导入协议层故障','w');
    return;
  }
  S.protocolInjectTargetId=edge.id;
  if(edge.injectedFault&&getImportedFaultModel(edge.injectedFault.modelId)){
    S.protocolInjectSelectionMode='imported';
    S.protocolInjectSelectionId=edge.injectedFault.modelId;
  }else{
    S.protocolInjectSelectionMode='';
    S.protocolInjectSelectionId='';
  }
  renderProtocolInjectModal();
  openOv('ov-proto');
}

function confirmProtocolFaultInjection(){
  const target=getEdge(S.protocolInjectTargetId);
  if(!isProtocolInjectableEdge(target)){
    toast('当前没有可注入的 CAN 总线','w');
    return;
  }
  const selected=getCurrentProtocolSelection();
  if(!selected){
    toast('请先选择一个 CAN 协议层故障模型','w');
    return;
  }

  let faultModel=selected;
  if(S.protocolInjectSelectionMode==='template'){
    const existing=S.availableFaultModels.find(model=>model.layer==='protocol'&&(model.templateId===selected.id||model.name===selected.name));
    faultModel=existing||upsertAvailableFaultModel({
      id:`fm-protocol-${selected.id}`,
      name:selected.name,
      layer:'protocol',
      desc:selected.desc,
      tags:selected.tags,
      faultKind:selected.faultKind||selected.tags?.[0]||'协议层故障',
      faultCode:selected.faultCode||'',
      createdAt:new Date().toLocaleDateString('zh-CN'),
      origin:'template',
      templateId:selected.id
    });
  }

  const importedModel=ensureImportedFaultModel(faultModel);
  target.injectedFault={
    modelId:importedModel.id,
    name:importedModel.name,
    layer:'protocol',
    tags:cloneDefaults(importedModel.tags||[]),
    desc:importedModel.desc||'',
    faultKind:importedModel.faultKind||importedModel.tags?.[0]||'协议层故障',
    faultCode:importedModel.faultCode||''
  };
  renderFaultCatalogList();
  markTopologyDirty('fault');
  closeOv('ov-proto');
  renderEdges();
  renderPropertyPanel(target);
  updateUI();
  toast(`已将协议层故障「${importedModel.name}」注入到当前 CAN 总线`,'s');
}

// ─── 故障配置 ───
function setLayer(el,l){
  document.querySelectorAll('.lbtn').forEach(e=>e.classList.remove('on'));
  el.classList.add('on');S.activeLayer=l;upPrev();
}

function upPrev(){
  const s=parseFloat(document.getElementById('cfs')?.value)||5;
  const d=parseFloat(document.getElementById('cfd')?.value)||3;
  const tot=parseFloat(document.getElementById('cftot')?.value)||20;
  const mag=parseFloat(document.getElementById('cfmag')?.value)||0.5;
  const typ=document.getElementById('cftype')?.value||'';
  const svg=document.getElementById('ctlsvg');if(!svg)return;
  const W=svg.clientWidth||170,H=72,mid=H/2;
  const tx=t=>(t/tot)*W;
  const sx=tx(s),ex=tx(Math.min(s+d,tot));
  document.getElementById('tlr').setAttribute('x',sx);
  document.getElementById('tlr').setAttribute('width',ex-sx);
  document.getElementById('tll').setAttribute('x1',sx);document.getElementById('tll').setAttribute('x2',sx);
  let np=[],fp=[];
  for(let i=0;i<=60;i++){
    const t=(i/60)*tot,x=tx(t),y=mid+Math.sin(t*2)*10;
    np.push(`${x},${y}`);
    let fy=y;
    if(t>=s&&t<=s+d){
      if(typ.includes('卡死'))fy=mid+18;
      else if(typ.includes('婕傜Щ'))fy=y+(t-s)*mag*4;
      else fy=y+mag*18;
    }
    fp.push(`${x},${Math.max(4,Math.min(H-4,fy))}`);
  }
  document.getElementById('tln').setAttribute('points',np.join(' '));
  document.getElementById('tlf').setAttribute('points',fp.join(' '));
  const tgt=document.getElementById('cftgt')?.selectedOptions?.[0]?.textContent||'未选择目标';
  document.getElementById('csumm').innerHTML=`
    <div class="srow"><span class="sk">目标<</span><span class="sv">${tgt.split('路')[0].trim()}<</span></div>
    <div class="srow"><span class="sk">层级<</span><span class="sv">${S.activeLayer}<</span></div>
    <div class="srow"><span class="sk">类型<</span><span class="sv">${typ.split('(')[0].trim()}<</span></div>
    <div class="srow"><span class="sk">起始<</span><span class="sv">${s}s<</span></div>
    <div class="srow"><span class="sk">鏃堕暱<</span><span class="sv">${d}s<</span></div>
    <div class="srow"><span class="sk">骞呭害<</span><span class="sv">${mag}<</span></div>`;
}

function confirmFC(){
  const targetId=document.getElementById('cftgt')?.value||'';
  markFaultTarget(targetId);
  S.simDone=false;
  S.step=3;
  closeOv('ov-cfg');
  toast('故障配置已保存，可以开始运行仿真','s');
  updateUI();
}

// ─── 示波器与仿真运行时 ───
function getScopeNodes(){
  return S.modelNodes.filter(node=>node.type==='instrument_scope');
}

function getAuxInstrumentNodes(){
  return S.modelNodes.filter(node=>node.type==='instrument_logger'||node.type==='instrument_spectrum');
}

function getConnectedScopeNodes(){
  return getScopeNodes().filter(node=>getIncomingEdgesForNode(node.id).length>0);
}

function getIncomingEdgesForNode(nodeId){
  return S.modelEdges
    .filter(edge=>edge.targetNodeId===nodeId)
    .sort((a,b)=>(a.targetPortIndex||0)-(b.targetPortIndex||0)||a.id.localeCompare(b.id));
}

function getOutgoingEdgesForNode(nodeId){
  return S.modelEdges.filter(edge=>edge.sourceNodeId===nodeId);
}

function createRuntimeBucket(){
  return {nodeStates:{},edgeStates:{},scopeSamples:{},instrumentSamples:{}};
}

const SIM = {
  inited:false,
  running:false,
  paused:false,
  hasSamples:false,
  timer:null,
  time:0,
  stepIndex:0,
  duration:10,
  stepSize:0.1,
  datasetName:'test',
  realtime:false,
  activeScopeId:'',
  scopeWindows:{},
  scopeWindowZ:10,
  actual:createRuntimeBucket(),
  reference:createRuntimeBucket()
};

function clearSimLoop(){
  if(SIM.timer){
    clearInterval(SIM.timer);
    SIM.timer=null;
  }
}

function getNodeSeed(id){
  return Number(String(id||'').replace(/\D/g,''))||1;
}

function noiseAt(seed,stepIndex,time){
  const raw=Math.sin(seed*12.9898+stepIndex*78.233+time*5.173)*43758.5453;
  const frac=raw-Math.floor(raw);
  return frac*2-1;
}

function parseScalar(value,fallback=0){
  const parsed=Number.parseFloat(String(value).replace(/[^\d+\-.eE]/g,''));
  return Number.isFinite(parsed)?parsed:fallback;
}

function ensureScopeSelection(preferredId=''){
  if(preferredId&&getNode(preferredId)?.type==='instrument_scope'){
    SIM.activeScopeId=preferredId;
    return;
  }
  if(getNode(SIM.activeScopeId)?.type==='instrument_scope'){return;}
  SIM.activeScopeId=getScopeNodes()[0]?.id||'';
}

function ensureScopeWindowStore(){
  if(!SIM.scopeWindows){SIM.scopeWindows={};}
  if(!Number.isFinite(SIM.scopeWindowZ)){SIM.scopeWindowZ=10;}
}

function getScopeWindowHostMetrics(){
  const host=document.getElementById('scope-window-layer');
  const viewport=getCanvasViewport();
  const target=host||viewport;
  const rect=target?.getBoundingClientRect?.();
  return {
    width:Math.max(
      host?.clientWidth||0,
      viewport?.clientWidth||0,
      Math.round(rect?.width||0),
      window.innerWidth||0,
      320
    ),
    height:Math.max(
      host?.clientHeight||0,
      viewport?.clientHeight||0,
      Math.round(rect?.height||0),
      window.innerHeight||0,
      240
    )
  };
}

function clampScopeWindowPosition(scopeWindow){
  if(!scopeWindow){return scopeWindow;}
  const hostMetrics=getScopeWindowHostMetrics();
  const maxX=Math.max(SCOPE_WINDOW_LAYOUT.gutter,hostMetrics.width-SCOPE_WINDOW_LAYOUT.defaultWidth-SCOPE_WINDOW_LAYOUT.gutter);
  const maxY=Math.max(SCOPE_WINDOW_LAYOUT.reservedTop,hostMetrics.height-SCOPE_WINDOW_LAYOUT.estimatedHeight-SCOPE_WINDOW_LAYOUT.gutter);
  scopeWindow.x=clamp(Math.round(scopeWindow.x),SCOPE_WINDOW_LAYOUT.gutter,maxX);
  scopeWindow.y=clamp(Math.round(scopeWindow.y),SCOPE_WINDOW_LAYOUT.reservedTop,maxY);
  return scopeWindow;
}

function listOpenScopeWindows(){
  ensureScopeWindowStore();
  return Object.values(SIM.scopeWindows).filter(scopeWindow=>scopeWindow.open!==false&&getNode(scopeWindow.scopeId));
}

function ensureScopeWindow(scopeId){
  ensureScopeWindowStore();
  const existing=SIM.scopeWindows[scopeId];
  if(existing){
    existing.open=true;
    return existing;
  }
  const index=Object.keys(SIM.scopeWindows).length;
  const created={
    scopeId,
    open:true,
    mode:'overlay',
    x:SCOPE_WINDOW_LAYOUT.gutter+index*SCOPE_WINDOW_LAYOUT.cascadeX,
    y:SCOPE_WINDOW_LAYOUT.reservedTop+index*SCOPE_WINDOW_LAYOUT.cascadeY,
    z:++SIM.scopeWindowZ
  };
  SIM.scopeWindows[scopeId]=clampScopeWindowPosition(created);
  return created;
}

function focusScopeWindow(scopeId){
  const scopeWindow=ensureScopeWindow(scopeId);
  scopeWindow.z=++SIM.scopeWindowZ;
  SIM.activeScopeId=scopeId;
  return scopeWindow;
}

function closeScopeWindow(scopeId){
  ensureScopeWindowStore();
  if(SIM.scopeWindows[scopeId]){
    SIM.scopeWindows[scopeId].open=false;
  }
  renderScopeWindows();
}

function renderScopeWindows(){
  const host=document.getElementById('scope-window-layer');
  if(!host){return;}
  host.innerHTML=listOpenScopeWindows()
    .sort((left,right)=>left.z-right.z)
    .map(scopeWindow=>{
      const node=getNode(scopeWindow.scopeId);
      return `
        <section class="scope-window" data-scope-id="${scopeWindow.scopeId}" style="left:${scopeWindow.x}px;top:${scopeWindow.y}px;z-index:${scopeWindow.z}">
          <header class="scope-window__header" data-scope-drag-handle="${scopeWindow.scopeId}" onmousedown="startScopeWindowDrag(event,'${scopeWindow.scopeId}')" onpointerdown="startScopeWindowDrag(event,'${scopeWindow.scopeId}')">
            <div class="scope-window__title">${escapeHtml(node?.props?.name||node?.name||'示波器')}</div>
            <button type="button" class="scope-window__close" data-scope-close="${scopeWindow.scopeId}">关闭</button>
          </header>
          <div class="scope-window__plot">
            <canvas data-scope-role="wave-canvas"></canvas>
          </div>
        </section>`;
    })
    .join('');
  host.querySelectorAll('.scope-window').forEach(el=>{
    el.addEventListener('pointerdown',()=>{
      focusScopeWindow(el.dataset.scopeId||'');
      renderScopeWindows();
    });
  });
  host.querySelectorAll('[data-scope-drag-handle]').forEach(header=>{
    header.addEventListener('mousedown',event=>{
      startScopeWindowDrag(event,header.dataset.scopeDragHandle||'');
    });
  });
  host.querySelectorAll('[data-scope-close]').forEach(btn=>{
    btn.addEventListener('click',event=>{
      event.stopPropagation();
      closeScopeWindow(btn.dataset.scopeClose||'');
    });
  });
}

function ensureNodeRuntime(bucket,node){
  if(!bucket.nodeStates[node.id]){
    bucket.nodeStates[node.id]={
      lastOutput:0,
      lastInput:0,
      lastOutputs:[0],
      lastInputValues:[],
      lastMiddleValues:[],
      prevInput:0,
      prevAggregateInput:0,
      integrator:0,
      firstOrder:0
    };
  }
  return bucket.nodeStates[node.id];
}

function ensureEdgeRuntime(bucket,edge){
  if(!bucket.edgeStates[edge.id]){
    bucket.edgeStates[edge.id]={lastOutput:0,delayQueue:[],history:[]};
  }
  return bucket.edgeStates[edge.id];
}

function pushLimitedSample(list,sample,limit=720){
  list.push(sample);
  if(list.length>limit){
    list.splice(0,list.length-limit);
  }
}

function hasSimulationFaults(){
  return S.modelNodes.some(node=>node.type.startsWith('fault_')||Boolean(node.injectedFault))
    || S.modelEdges.some(edge=>Boolean(edge.injectedFault));
}

function canInitializeSimulation(){
  if(!S.sysLoaded){return false;}
  if(!S.modelNodes.some(node=>node.type==='signal_source')){return false;}
  if(getConnectedScopeNodes().length===0){return false;}
  if(findInputCouplingConflicts().length>0){return false;}
  return true;
}

function resetSimulationRuntime(){
  clearSimLoop();
  SIM.time=0;
  SIM.stepIndex=0;
  SIM.hasSamples=false;
  SIM.actual=createRuntimeBucket();
  SIM.reference=createRuntimeBucket();
  getScopeNodes().forEach(node=>{
    SIM.actual.scopeSamples[node.id]=[];
    SIM.reference.scopeSamples[node.id]=[];
  });
  ensureScopeSelection();
  S.simDone=false;
  if(S.systemSaved&&S.step===3){
    S.step=2;
  }
}

function getSimulationLoopInterval(){
  if(SIM.realtime){
    return clamp(Math.round(SIM.stepSize*1000),80,400);
  }
  return 40;
}

function updateSimbarVisualState(){
  const runBtn=document.getElementById('sbtn-run');
  if(runBtn){
    runBtn.classList.toggle('active',SIM.running&&!SIM.paused);
  }
  document.getElementById('run-icon').textContent='▶';
  document.getElementById('run-lbl').textContent=SIM.running&&!SIM.paused?'运行中':'运行';
  document.getElementById('pause-lbl').textContent=SIM.paused?'继续':'鏆傚仠';
}

function simEnableButtons(init,run,step,pause,stop){
  const ids=['sbtn-init','sbtn-run','sbtn-step','sbtn-pause','sbtn-stop'];
  const vals=[init,run,step,pause,stop];
  ids.forEach((id,i)=>{
    const el=document.getElementById(id);
    if(vals[i]) el.classList.remove('sim-btn-disabled');
    else el.classList.add('sim-btn-disabled');
  });
  updateSimbarVisualState();
}

function updateSimbarEnabled(){
  if(!S.sysLoaded){simEnableButtons(false,false,false,false,false);return;}
  if(!SIM.inited){
    simEnableButtons(canInitializeSimulation(),false,false,false,false);
    return;
  }
  if(SIM.running&&!SIM.paused){simEnableButtons(false,false,false,true,true);return;}
  if(SIM.paused){simEnableButtons(false,true,true,true,true);return;}
  simEnableButtons(true,true,true,false,false);
}

function findInputCouplingConflicts(){
  const seen=new Map();
  const conflicts=[];
  S.modelEdges.forEach(edge=>{
    const key=`${edge.targetNodeId}:${edge.targetPortIndex||0}`;
    if(seen.has(key)){
      conflicts.push(seen.get(key),edge);
    }else{
      seen.set(key,edge);
    }
  });
  return [...new Map(conflicts.map(edge=>[edge.id,edge])).values()];
}

function validateSimulationTopology(){
  if(!S.sysLoaded){toast('请先导入系统模型','w');return false;}
  if(!S.modelNodes.some(node=>node.type==='signal_source')){
    toast('请至少放置一个信号源','w');
    return false;
  }
  if(getScopeNodes().length===0){
    toast('请至少放置一个示波器用于观察信号','w');
    return false;
  }
  if(getConnectedScopeNodes().length===0){
    toast('请至少让一个示波器接入信号链路，才能查看波形','w');
    return false;
  }
  const conflicts=findInputCouplingConflicts();
  if(conflicts.length){
    selectEdge(conflicts[0].id);
    toast('检测到同一输入端口存在多条连线，请先删除多余连线以避免信号耦合','w');
    return false;
  }
  return true;
}

function computeSourceSignal(node,time){
  const amplitude=parseScalar(node.props.amplitude,1);
  const frequency=parseScalar(node.props.frequency,1);
  if(node.props.waveType==='闃惰穬'){
    const stepTime=Math.max(0.2,frequency);
    return time>=stepTime?amplitude:0;
  }
  if(node.props.waveType==='常值'){
    return amplitude;
  }
  return amplitude*Math.sin(2*Math.PI*frequency*time);
}

function applyElectricalFault(node,inputValue,outputValue,time){
  if(!node.injectedFault){return outputValue;}
  const modelId=node.injectedFault.modelId||'';
  const importedModel=modelId?getImportedFaultModel(modelId):null;
  const faultValue=parseScalar(importedModel?.defaultValue,0);
  if(modelId==='motor_efficiency_loss'){
    const efficiency=faultValue>0?faultValue:0.55;
    return outputValue*efficiency;
  }
  if(modelId==='motor_lock'){
    return 0;
  }
  if(modelId==='motor_thrust_saturation'){
    const saturation=faultValue>0?faultValue:8;
    return Math.max(-saturation,Math.min(saturation,outputValue));
  }
  const name=node.injectedFault.name||'';
  if(name.includes('过流')){
    return Math.abs(inputValue)>1.2?0:outputValue*0.78;
  }
  if(name.includes('短路')||name.includes('断路')||name.includes('开路')){
    return 0;
  }
  if(name.includes('电压')){
    return outputValue*(0.94+0.08*Math.sin(time*7.4));
  }
  return outputValue*0.85;
}

function applyPhysicalFaultNode(node,inputValue,time,modeKey){
  if(modeKey==='reference'){return inputValue;}
  if(node.type==='fault_bias'){
    return inputValue+0.5;
  }
  if(node.type==='fault_noise'){
    return inputValue+noiseAt(getNodeSeed(node.id),SIM.stepIndex,time)*0.22;
  }
  return inputValue;
}

function flipBitValue(value){
  const scaled=Math.round(value*256);
  return (scaled^0b1000)/256;
}

function transmitEdgeSignal(edge,value,modeKey,time){
  const bucket=modeKey==='reference'?SIM.reference:SIM.actual;
  const edgeState=ensureEdgeRuntime(bucket,edge);
  const base=Array.isArray(value)
    ?value.map(sanitizeSignalValue)
    :(Number.isFinite(value)?value:0);
  let nextValue=base;

  if(modeKey==='actual'&&edge.injectedFault?.layer==='protocol'&&!Array.isArray(base)){
    const kind=edge.injectedFault.faultKind||'';
    const faultCode=edge.injectedFault.faultCode||'';
    const held=Number.isFinite(edgeState.lastOutput)?edgeState.lastOutput:0;
    if(faultCode==='loss'||kind==='丢包'){
      nextValue=noiseAt(getNodeSeed(edge.id),SIM.stepIndex,time)>0.55?held:base;
    }else if(faultCode==='delay'||kind==='延迟'){
      const delaySteps=clamp(Math.round(0.35/Math.max(SIM.stepSize,0.001)),1,8);
      edgeState.delayQueue.push(base);
      nextValue=edgeState.delayQueue.length>delaySteps?edgeState.delayQueue.shift():held;
    }else if(faultCode==='bitflip'||kind==='位翻转'){
      nextValue=flipBitValue(base);
    }else if(faultCode==='replay'||kind==='重放'){
      if(edgeState.history.length>6&&SIM.stepIndex>6&&SIM.stepIndex%10===0){
        nextValue=edgeState.history[Math.max(0,edgeState.history.length-6)];
      }else{
        nextValue=base;
      }
    }
  }

  edgeState.lastOutput=nextValue;
  pushLimitedSample(edgeState.history,Array.isArray(base)?sanitizeSignalValue(base[0]??0):base,40);
  return nextValue;
}

function sanitizeSignalValue(value){
  if(Array.isArray(value)){
    return value.map(sanitizeSignalValue);
  }
  return Number.isFinite(value)?value:0;
}

function resolveNodeInputValues(node,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting){
  const inputPorts=getNodePorts(node).inputs;
  if(!inputPorts.length){return [];}
  const incoming=getIncomingEdgesForNode(node.id);
  return inputPorts.map((_,portIndex)=>{
    const edge=incoming.find(item=>(item.targetPortIndex||0)===portIndex);
    if(!edge){return 0;}
    const upstream=resolveNodeOutput(edge.sourceNodeId,edge.sourcePortIndex||0,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting);
    return transmitEdgeSignal(edge,upstream,modeKey,time);
  });
}

function buildSimulationResult(node,nodeState,inputValues,modeKey,time,dt){
  normalizeSimulationInterfaces(node.props);
  const primaryInput=sanitizeSignalValue(inputValues[0]||0);
  const aggregateInput=inputValues.length
    ?inputValues.reduce((sum,value)=>sum+sanitizeSignalValue(value),0)
    :0;
  const activeInput=inputValues.length>1?aggregateInput:primaryInput;
  let coreOutput=0;
  let stateValue=0;

  if(node.props.moduleType==='微分'){
    coreOutput=(activeInput-(nodeState.prevAggregateInput||0))/Math.max(dt,0.001);
    stateValue=activeInput;
  }else if(node.props.moduleType==='积分'){
    nodeState.integrator=(nodeState.integrator||0)+activeInput*dt;
    coreOutput=nodeState.integrator;
    stateValue=nodeState.integrator;
  }else{
    const tau=1;
    const previous=nodeState.firstOrder||0;
    const alpha=dt/(tau+dt);
    coreOutput=previous+alpha*(activeInput-previous);
    nodeState.firstOrder=coreOutput;
    stateValue=nodeState.firstOrder;
  }

  nodeState.prevInput=primaryInput;
  nodeState.prevAggregateInput=activeInput;
  if(modeKey==='actual'){
    coreOutput=applyElectricalFault(node,activeInput,coreOutput,time);
  }

  const outputValues=node.props.outputs.map((_,index)=>{
    if(index===0){return sanitizeSignalValue(coreOutput);}
    if(index===1){return sanitizeSignalValue(stateValue);}
    if(index===2){return sanitizeSignalValue(aggregateInput);}
    return sanitizeSignalValue(coreOutput+(index*0.12*aggregateInput));
  });

  const middleValues=node.props.middleVars.map((_,index)=>{
    if(index===0){return sanitizeSignalValue(primaryInput);}
    if(index===1){return sanitizeSignalValue(aggregateInput);}
    if(index===2){return sanitizeSignalValue(stateValue);}
    if(index===3){return sanitizeSignalValue(coreOutput);}
    return sanitizeSignalValue((coreOutput+aggregateInput+primaryInput)/(index+1));
  });

  return {outputs:outputValues,middleValues};
}

function getPythonBindingDefaultValue(port){
  return window.__GZ_PYTHON_RUNTIME__?.getPythonBindingDefaultValue
    ?window.__GZ_PYTHON_RUNTIME__.getPythonBindingDefaultValue(port)
    :0;
}

function readPythonExecutionValue(collection,item,index){
  if(Array.isArray(collection)){
    return collection[index];
  }
  if(!collection||typeof collection!=='object'){
    return undefined;
  }
  if(item?.varName&&Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(collection,item.varName)){
    return collection[item.varName];
  }
  if(item?.displayName&&Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(collection,item.displayName)){
    return collection[item.displayName];
  }
  return undefined;
}

function executeBoundFlowBlock(node,nodeState,inputValues,modeKey,time,dt){
  const binding=ensureFlowNodePythonBinding(node);
  const runtime=window.__GZ_PYTHON_RUNTIME__;
  if(!binding.bound||typeof runtime?.executeFlowBlockPythonBindingSync!=='function'){
    const passthrough=sanitizeSignalValue(inputValues[0]||0);
    return {outputs:[passthrough],middleValues:[]};
  }

  const execution=runtime.executeFlowBlockPythonBindingSync({
    nodeId:node.id,
    binding,
    inputValues,
    mode:modeKey,
    time,
    dt,
    adapterMode:binding.executionMode||'mock',
    adapterEndpoint:binding.executionConfig?.endpoint,
    applyElectricalFault:value=>applyElectricalFault(node,inputValues[0]||0,value,time)
  });

  nodeState.lastPythonPayload=execution.payload||null;
  nodeState.lastPythonResult=execution.response||null;
  return {
    outputs:(execution.outputs||[]).map(sanitizeSignalValue),
    middleValues:(execution.middleValues||[]).map(sanitizeSignalValue)
  };
}

function resolveNodeOutputs(nodeId,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting){
  if(cache.has(nodeId)){return cache.get(nodeId);}
  const node=getNode(nodeId);
  if(!node){
    return {outputs:[0],middleValues:[]};
  }
  const bucket=modeKey==='reference'?SIM.reference:SIM.actual;
  const nodeState=ensureNodeRuntime(bucket,node);
  if(visiting.has(nodeId)){
    return {
      outputs:nodeState.lastOutputs?.length?nodeState.lastOutputs:[nodeState.lastOutput||0],
      middleValues:nodeState.lastMiddleValues||[]
    };
  }
  visiting.add(nodeId);
  const inputValues=resolveNodeInputValues(node,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting);
  let resolved={outputs:[0],middleValues:[]};

  if(node.type==='signal_source'){
    resolved={outputs:[computeSourceSignal(node,time)],middleValues:[]};
  }else if(node.type==='flow_block'){
    resolved=isPythonBoundFlowBlock(node)
      ?executeBoundFlowBlock(node,nodeState,inputValues,modeKey,time,dt)
      :{outputs:[sanitizeSignalValue(inputValues[0]||0)],middleValues:[]};
  }else if(node.type==='simulation_block'){
    resolved=buildSimulationResult(node,nodeState,inputValues,modeKey,time,dt);
  }else if(node.type.startsWith('fault_')){
    resolved={outputs:[applyPhysicalFaultNode(node,sanitizeSignalValue(inputValues[0]||0),time,modeKey)],middleValues:[]};
  }else if(node.type.startsWith('instrument_')){
    resolved={outputs:[sanitizeSignalValue(inputValues[0]||0)],middleValues:[]};
  }else{
    resolved={outputs:[sanitizeSignalValue(inputValues[0]||0)],middleValues:[]};
  }

  resolved.outputs=(resolved.outputs||[0]).map(sanitizeSignalValue);
  resolved.middleValues=(resolved.middleValues||[]).map(sanitizeSignalValue);
  nodeState.lastInputValues=inputValues.slice();
  nodeState.lastInput=inputValues[0]||0;
  nodeState.lastOutputs=resolved.outputs.slice();
  nodeState.lastMiddleValues=resolved.middleValues.slice();
  nodeState.lastOutput=nodeState.lastOutputs[0]||0;
  visiting.delete(nodeId);
  cache.set(nodeId,resolved);
  return resolved;
}

function resolveNodeOutput(nodeId,outputIndex,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting){
  const node=getNode(nodeId);
  const resolved=resolveNodeOutputs(nodeId,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting);
  if(!node){return 0;}
  if(node.type==='simulation_block'||(node.type==='flow_block'&&isPythonBoundFlowBlock(node))){
    const mainCount=node.type==='simulation_block'
      ?(normalizeSimulationInterfaces(node.props),node.props.outputs.length)
      :(node.pythonBinding?.portMapping?.outputs?.length||0);
    if(outputIndex<mainCount){
      return sanitizeSignalValue(resolved.outputs[outputIndex]??resolved.outputs[0]??0);
    }
    return sanitizeSignalValue(resolved.middleValues[outputIndex-mainCount]??resolved.outputs[0]??0);
  }
  return sanitizeSignalValue(resolved.outputs[outputIndex]??resolved.outputs[0]??0);
}

function resolveNodeInput(node,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting){
  return resolveNodeInputValues(node,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting)[0]||0;
}

function resolveNodeSignal(nodeId,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting){
  return resolveNodeOutput(nodeId,0,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting);
}

function recordScopeSamples(time,dt){
  const actualCache=new Map();
  const referenceCache=new Map();
  const actualVisiting=new Set();
  const referenceVisiting=new Set();
  getScopeNodes().forEach(scopeNode=>{
    const actualValue=resolveNodeSignal(scopeNode.id,'actual',time,dt,actualCache,actualVisiting);
    const referenceValue=resolveNodeSignal(scopeNode.id,'reference',time,dt,referenceCache,referenceVisiting);
    pushLimitedSample(SIM.actual.scopeSamples[scopeNode.id],{t:time,v:actualValue});
    pushLimitedSample(SIM.reference.scopeSamples[scopeNode.id],{t:time,v:referenceValue});
  });
}

function runSimulationTick(){
  if(!SIM.inited){return false;}
  if(SIM.time>=SIM.duration){return true;}
  const time=SIM.time;
  const dt=SIM.stepSize;
  recordScopeSamples(time,dt);
  SIM.stepIndex+=1;
  SIM.time=Number((SIM.time+dt).toFixed(6));
  SIM.hasSamples=true;
  S.step=3;
  if(document.getElementById('ov-scope').classList.contains('open')){
    drawScope();
  }
  updateUI();
  return SIM.time>=SIM.duration;
}

function startSimulationLoop(){
  clearSimLoop();
  SIM.timer=setInterval(()=>{
    if(!SIM.running||SIM.paused){return;}
    const completed=runSimulationTick();
    if(completed){
      simStop('completed');
    }
  },getSimulationLoopInterval());
}

function getScopeSignalName(scopeNode){
  const incoming=getIncomingEdgesForNode(scopeNode.id)[0];
  if(!incoming){return '未接入信号';}
  const sourceNode=getNode(incoming.sourceNodeId);
  if(!sourceNode){return '上游信号';}
  const outputPort=getNodePorts(sourceNode).outputs[incoming.sourcePortIndex||0];
  if(outputPort){
    return `${sourceNode.props?.name||'上游信号'} · ${outputPort.label}`;
  }
  return sourceNode.props?.name||'上游信号';
}

function updateScopeChrome(){
  ensureScopeSelection();
  const scopeNode=getNode(SIM.activeScopeId);
  const scopeTitle=document.getElementById('scope-title');
  const scopeMeta=document.getElementById('scope-meta');
  const sc1Lbl=document.getElementById('sc1-lbl');
  const sc2Lbl=document.getElementById('sc2-lbl');
  if(!scopeNode){
    scopeTitle.textContent='示波器 · 波形查看';
    scopeMeta.textContent='当前没有示波器模块';
    sc1Lbl.textContent='CH1 · 时域波形';
    sc2Lbl.textContent='CH2 · 频谱';
    return null;
  }
  const signalName=getScopeSignalName(scopeNode);
  scopeTitle.textContent=`示波器 · ${scopeNode.props.name}`;
  scopeMeta.textContent=SIM.hasSamples
    ?`${SIM.datasetName} · t=${SIM.time.toFixed(2)}s / ${SIM.duration.toFixed(2)}s · Δt=${SIM.stepSize.toFixed(3)}s · ${signalName}`
    :`${SIM.datasetName} · 等待仿真数据 · ${signalName}`;
  sc1Lbl.textContent=`CH1 · ${signalName}`;
  sc2Lbl.textContent=`CH2 · ${scopeNode.props.name} 频谱`;
  return scopeNode;
}

function drawScopeGrid(ctx,width,height){
  ctx.clearRect(0,0,width,height);
  ctx.fillStyle='#f9fbfe';
  ctx.fillRect(0,0,width,height);
  ctx.strokeStyle='#eaf2fb';
  ctx.lineWidth=0.5;
  for(let x=0;x<width;x+=40){
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(x,0);
    ctx.lineTo(x,height);
    ctx.stroke();
  }
  ctx.strokeStyle='#e2eef8';
  for(let y=0;y<height;y+=25){
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(0,y);
    ctx.lineTo(width,y);
    ctx.stroke();
  }
}

function drawScopeEmpty(ctx,width,height,message){
  drawScopeGrid(ctx,width,height);
  ctx.fillStyle='#b3c8da';
  ctx.font='12px "Microsoft YaHei UI","Segoe UI",sans-serif';
  ctx.textAlign='center';
  ctx.fillText(message,width/2,height/2);
  ctx.textAlign='left';
}

function drawWaveSeries(ctx,width,height,series,color,getX,getY){
  if(series.length<1){return;}
  ctx.strokeStyle=color;
  ctx.lineWidth=1.7;
  ctx.beginPath();
  series.forEach((sample,index)=>{
    const x=getX(sample.t,index,series.length);
    const y=getY(sample.v);
    if(index===0){ctx.moveTo(x,y);}else{ctx.lineTo(x,y);}
  });
  ctx.stroke();
}

function buildSpectrum(values,binCount=24){
  if(values.length<4){return new Array(binCount).fill(0);}
  const bins=[];
  for(let k=1;k<=binCount;k++){
    let real=0;
    let imag=0;
    values.forEach((value,index)=>{
      const angle=2*Math.PI*k*index/values.length;
      real+=value*Math.cos(angle);
      imag-=value*Math.sin(angle);
    });
    bins.push(Math.sqrt(real*real+imag*imag)/values.length);
  }
  const maxValue=Math.max(...bins,1e-6);
  return bins.map(value=>value/maxValue);
}

function openScope(scopeId=''){
  ensureScopeSelection(scopeId||S.selBlk);
  if(!SIM.activeScopeId){
    toast('当前没有可打开的示波器模块','w');
    return;
  }
  openOv('ov-scope');
  setTimeout(drawScope,60);
}

function focusScopeLatest(){
  drawScope();
}

function togCmp(){
  S.cmpMode=!S.cmpMode;
  document.getElementById('scmp').classList.toggle('on',S.cmpMode);
  document.getElementById('sleg-f').style.display=S.cmpMode?'flex':'none';
  drawScope();
}

function drawScope(){
  const scopeNode=updateScopeChrome();
  const ch1=document.getElementById('sc1');
  const ch2=document.getElementById('sc2');
  if(!ch1||!ch2){return;}
  ch1.width=ch1.offsetWidth;
  ch1.height=ch1.offsetHeight;
  ch2.width=ch2.offsetWidth;
  ch2.height=ch2.offsetHeight;
  const ctx1=ch1.getContext('2d');
  const ctx2=ch2.getContext('2d');
  if(!scopeNode){
    drawScopeEmpty(ctx1,ch1.width,ch1.height,'请先在画布中放置示波器');
    drawScopeEmpty(ctx2,ch2.width,ch2.height,'等待频谱数据');
    return;
  }

  const actualSeries=(SIM.actual.scopeSamples[scopeNode.id]||[]).slice(-240);
  const referenceSeries=(SIM.reference.scopeSamples[scopeNode.id]||[]).slice(-240);
  if(actualSeries.length===0){
    drawScopeEmpty(ctx1,ch1.width,ch1.height,'双击示波器后，开始仿真即可看到波形');
    drawScopeEmpty(ctx2,ch2.width,ch2.height,'暂无频谱数据');
    return;
  }

  drawScopeGrid(ctx1,ch1.width,ch1.height);
  const visibleSeries=S.cmpMode&&referenceSeries.length?referenceSeries.concat(actualSeries):actualSeries;
  let minValue=Math.min(...visibleSeries.map(item=>item.v));
  let maxValue=Math.max(...visibleSeries.map(item=>item.v));
  if(Math.abs(maxValue-minValue)<1e-6){
    maxValue+=1;
    minValue-=1;
  }else{
    const padding=(maxValue-minValue)*0.18;
    maxValue+=padding;
    minValue-=padding;
  }
  const startTime=actualSeries[0].t;
  const endTime=actualSeries[actualSeries.length-1].t||startTime+SIM.stepSize;
  const span=Math.max(endTime-startTime,SIM.stepSize);
  const getX=time=>18+((time-startTime)/span)*(ch1.width-36);
  const getY=value=>12+(maxValue-value)/(maxValue-minValue)*(ch1.height-24);
  const zeroY=getY(0);
  if(zeroY>=8&&zeroY<=ch1.height-8){
    ctx1.strokeStyle='#c2d6ea';
    ctx1.lineWidth=0.8;
    ctx1.beginPath();
    ctx1.moveTo(0,zeroY);
    ctx1.lineTo(ch1.width,zeroY);
    ctx1.stroke();
  }
  if(S.cmpMode&&referenceSeries.length){
    drawWaveSeries(ctx1,ch1.width,ch1.height,referenceSeries,'#1d6fbf',getX,getY);
    drawWaveSeries(ctx1,ch1.width,ch1.height,actualSeries,'#dc2626',getX,getY);
  }else{
    drawWaveSeries(ctx1,ch1.width,ch1.height,actualSeries,'#1d6fbf',getX,getY);
  }
  ctx1.fillStyle='#94b4cc';
  ctx1.font='8px JetBrains Mono,monospace';
  ctx1.fillText(`${startTime.toFixed(1)}s`,4,ch1.height-4);
  ctx1.fillText(`${endTime.toFixed(1)}s`,ch1.width-32,ch1.height-4);

  drawScopeGrid(ctx2,ch2.width,ch2.height);
  const actualSpectrum=buildSpectrum(actualSeries.map(item=>item.v));
  const referenceSpectrum=buildSpectrum(referenceSeries.map(item=>item.v));
  const binWidth=ch2.width/actualSpectrum.length;
  actualSpectrum.forEach((value,index)=>{
    const x=index*binWidth;
    const height=value*(ch2.height-18);
    const gradient=ctx2.createLinearGradient(x,ch2.height-height,x,ch2.height);
    gradient.addColorStop(0,S.cmpMode?'rgba(220,38,38,0.85)':'rgba(29,111,191,0.88)');
    gradient.addColorStop(1,'rgba(74,158,255,0.08)');
    ctx2.fillStyle=gradient;
    ctx2.fillRect(x+1,ch2.height-height,Math.max(binWidth-2,2),height);
    if(S.cmpMode&&referenceSpectrum[index]!=null){
      const refHeight=referenceSpectrum[index]*(ch2.height-18);
      ctx2.fillStyle='rgba(29,111,191,0.24)';
      ctx2.fillRect(x+1,ch2.height-refHeight,Math.max(binWidth-2,2),refHeight);
    }
  });
  ctx2.fillStyle='#94b4cc';
  ctx2.font='8px JetBrains Mono,monospace';
  ctx2.fillText('0Hz',3,ch2.height-4);
  ctx2.fillText(`${(0.5/Math.max(SIM.stepSize,0.001)).toFixed(1)}Hz`,Math.max(ch2.width-42,3),ch2.height-4);
}

// ─── 仿真控制栏 ───
function simInit(silent=false){
  if(!validateSimulationTopology()){return;}
  const autoSaved=!S.systemSaved;
  if(autoSaved){
    S.systemSaved=true;
    if(S.step<2){S.step=2;}
  }
  SIM.datasetName=document.getElementById('sim-name').value.trim()||'test';
  SIM.duration=Math.max(parseScalar(document.getElementById('sim-dur').value,10),0.1);
  SIM.stepSize=Math.max(parseScalar(document.getElementById('sim-step').value,0.1),0.001);
  SIM.realtime=document.getElementById('sim-rt').checked;
  SIM.inited=true;
  SIM.running=false;
  SIM.paused=false;
  resetSimulationRuntime();
  updateSimbarEnabled();
  updateUI();
  if(document.getElementById('ov-scope').classList.contains('open')){
    drawScope();
  }
  if(!silent){
    if(autoSaved){
      toast(`系统模型已自动保存，并完成仿真初始化：${SIM.datasetName} · 时长 ${SIM.duration}s · 步长 ${SIM.stepSize}s`,'s');
      return;
    }
    toast(`仿真初始化完成：${SIM.datasetName} · 时长 ${SIM.duration}s · 步长 ${SIM.stepSize}s`,'s');
  }
}

function simRun(){
  if(!SIM.inited){
    simInit();
    if(!SIM.inited){return;}
  }
  if(SIM.time>=SIM.duration){
    simInit(true);
  }
  SIM.realtime=document.getElementById('sim-rt').checked;
  SIM.running=true;
  SIM.paused=false;
  startSimulationLoop();
  updateSimbarEnabled();
  updateUI();
  toast('仿真开始运行','s');
}

function simStep(){
  if(!SIM.inited){
    simInit();
    if(!SIM.inited){return;}
  }
  if(SIM.time>=SIM.duration){
    toast('当前仿真已经结束，请重新初始化后再步进','w');
    return;
  }
  const completed=runSimulationTick();
  updateSimbarEnabled();
  if(completed){
    simStop('completed');
  }else{
    toast(`步进完成 · t = ${SIM.time.toFixed(2)}s`,'s');
  }
}

function simPause(){
  if(!SIM.running){return;}
  SIM.paused=!SIM.paused;
  if(SIM.paused){
    clearSimLoop();
    toast('仿真已暂停','w');
  }else{
    startSimulationLoop();
    toast('仿真继续运行','s');
  }
  updateSimbarEnabled();
  updateUI();
}

function simStop(mode='manual'){
  clearSimLoop();
  const hasData=SIM.hasSamples;
  SIM.running=false;
  SIM.paused=false;
  S.simDone=hasData;
  if(hasData){
    S.step=3;
  }
  updateSimbarEnabled();
  updateUI();
  if(mode==='completed'){
    toast('仿真已完成，结果可保存','s');
  }else{
    toast(hasData?'仿真已终止，结果可保存':'仿真已终止','s');
  }
}

function onRtToggle(el){
  SIM.realtime=el.checked;
  if(SIM.running&&!SIM.paused){
    startSimulationLoop();
  }
  toast(el.checked?'实时模式已开启':'实时模式已关闭', el.checked?'s':'w');
}
function ensurePythonBindingRuntimeStyles(){
  if(document.getElementById('python-binding-runtime-style')){return;}
  const style=document.createElement('style');
  style.id='python-binding-runtime-style';
  style.textContent=`
    .blk.python-bound{border-color:rgba(49,114,222,0.92);box-shadow:0 16px 28px rgba(40,102,196,0.18);}
    .node-card__python-chip{position:absolute;left:10px;top:8px;z-index:2;display:inline-flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;min-width:22px;height:22px;padding:0 6px;border-radius:999px;background:linear-gradient(135deg,#387dff 0%,#63a7ff 100%);color:#fff;font:700 10px/1 "JetBrains Mono","Consolas",monospace;box-shadow:0 8px 18px rgba(56,125,255,0.22);}
    .node-port.is-connected .node-port__inner{background:currentColor;box-shadow:0 0 0 2px rgba(255,255,255,0.9),0 0 0 4px rgba(56,125,255,0.18);}
    .node-port__label{position:absolute;font:600 10px/1.15 "JetBrains Mono","Consolas",monospace;color:#365a84;white-space:nowrap;pointer-events:none;}
    .node-port--input .node-port__label{right:100%;margin-right:9px;top:50%;transform:translateY(-50%);text-align:right;}
    .node-port--output .node-port__label{left:100%;margin-left:9px;top:50%;transform:translateY(-50%);}
    .node-port--top .node-port__label{left:50%;bottom:100%;margin-bottom:8px;transform:translateX(-50%);}
    .pgroup--compact{padding:10px 12px;gap:8px;}
  `;
  document.head.appendChild(style);
}

if(!window.__GZ_PYTHON_BINDING_EVENTS__){
  window.__GZ_PYTHON_BINDING_EVENTS__=true;
  const runtimeListeners=getRuntimeListenerStore();
  runtimeListeners.pythonBindingConfirm=event=>{
    if(event?.detail?.nodeId&&event?.detail?.binding){
      applyPythonBindingToNode(event.detail.nodeId,event.detail.binding);
    }
  };
  runtimeListeners.pythonBindingUnbind=event=>{
    unbindPythonBinding(event?.detail?.nodeId||'');
  };
  window.addEventListener('gz:python-binding-confirm',runtimeListeners.pythonBindingConfirm);
  window.addEventListener('gz:python-binding-unbind',runtimeListeners.pythonBindingUnbind);
}

function buildPythonBindingPortRows(items,kind){
  if(!items.length){
    return '<div class="props-help">?????????</div>';
  }
  return items.map(item=>{
    const status=kind==='inputs'
      ?(item.connected?'<span class="pv pv-ok">???</span>':'<span class="pv pv-fault">???</span>')
      :'<span class="pv pv-ok">已暴露</span>';
    const title=escapeHtml(item.displayName||item.varName||'-');
    const type=escapeHtml(item.type||'any');
    const note=item.comment?`<div class="props-help">${escapeHtml(item.comment)}</div>`:'';
    const defaultRow=kind==='inputs'&&item.default!==null&&item.default!==undefined&&item.default!==''
      ?`<div class="prow"><span class="pk">???</span><span class="pv">${escapeHtml(item.default)}<</span></div>`
      :'';
    return `
      <div class="pgroup pgroup--compact">
        <div class="prow"><span class="pk">${title}<</span>${status}</div>
        <div class="prow"><span class="pk">类型<</span><span class="pv">${type}<</span></div>
        ${defaultRow}
        ${note}
      </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

function buildFlowBlockFields(node){
  const binding=ensureFlowNodePythonBinding(node);
  const bound=binding.bound;
  const bindingSummary=bound
    ?`
      <div class="pgroup">
        <div class="pglbl">Python 绑定</div>
        <div class="prow"><span class="pk">文件<</span><span class="pv">${escapeHtml(binding.fileName||'-')}<</span></div>
        <div class="prow"><span class="pk">模块<</span><span class="pv">${escapeHtml(binding.moduleName||'-')}<</span></div>
        <div class="prow"><span class="pk">鍏ュ彛鍑芥暟<</span><span class="pv">${escapeHtml(binding.entryFunction||'process')}<</span></div>
        <div class="prow"><span class="pk">????<</span><span class="pv">${escapeHtml(getPythonBindingSummary(node))}<</span></div>
        ${binding.description?`<div class="props-help">${escapeHtml(binding.description)}</div>`:''}
      </div>
      <div class="pgroup">
        <div class="pglbl">输入端口</div>
        ${buildPythonBindingPortRows(binding.portMapping.inputs,'inputs')}
      </div>
      <div class="pgroup">
        <div class="pglbl">输出端口</div>
        ${buildPythonBindingPortRows(binding.portMapping.outputs,'outputs')}
      </div>
      <div class="pgroup">
        <div class="pglbl">中间变量</div>
        ${buildPythonBindingPortRows(binding.portMapping.middleVars,'middleVars')}
      </div>`
    :`
      <div class="pgroup">
        <div class="pglbl">Python 绑定</div>
        <div class="props-help">当前流程块尚未绑定 Python 文件。绑定后会根据函数输入、输出和 @observable 中间变量自动生成端口。</div>
      </div>`;

  const legacyFields=bound?`
      <div style="display:none">
        <input id="prop-inputName" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.inputName)}">
        <select id="prop-inputFormat">${buildSelectOptions(PORT_FORMATS,node.props.inputFormat)}</select>
        <input id="prop-outputName" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.outputName)}">
        <select id="prop-outputFormat">${buildSelectOptions(PORT_FORMATS,node.props.outputFormat)}</select>
      </div>`:`
      <div class="props-field"><label>输入名称</label><input id="prop-inputName" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.inputName)}"></div>
      <div class="props-row">
        <div class="props-field"><label>输入鏍煎紡</label><select id="prop-inputFormat">${buildSelectOptions(PORT_FORMATS,node.props.inputFormat)}</select></div>
        <div class="props-field"><label>输出鏍煎紡</label><select id="prop-outputFormat">${buildSelectOptions(PORT_FORMATS,node.props.outputFormat)}</select></div>
      </div>
      <div class="props-field"><label>输出名称</label><input id="prop-outputName" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.outputName)}"></div>
      <div class="props-help">未绑定Python 时，流程块按单输入单输出的直通模块工作。</div>`;

  return `
    <div class="pgroup">
      <div class="pglbl">流程块设置</div>
      <div class="props-field"><label>模块名称</label><input id="prop-name" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.name)}"></div>
      ${legacyFields}
    </div>
    ${bindingSummary}`;
}

function renderPropertyPanel(node){
  const pe=document.getElementById('pe');
  const pd=document.getElementById('pd');
  if(!node){
    pe.style.display='flex';
    pd.style.display='none';
    pd.innerHTML='';
    return;
  }

  if(node.sourceNodeId&&node.targetNodeId&&!node.type){
    const sourceNode=getNode(node.sourceNodeId);
    const targetNode=getNode(node.targetNodeId);
    const edgeLabel=node.lineType==='can'?'CAN 总线':'普通连接线';
    const sourceName=sourceNode?.props?.name||node.sourceNodeId;
    const targetName=targetNode?.props?.name||node.targetNodeId;
    const sourcePortName=node.sourcePort?.displayName||node.sourcePort?.varName||`#${(node.sourcePortIndex||0)+1}`;
    const targetPortName=node.targetPort?.displayName||node.targetPort?.varName||`#${(node.targetPortIndex||0)+1}`;
    const protocolFault=node.injectedFault?.layer==='protocol'?node.injectedFault:null;
    pe.style.display='none';
    pd.style.display='block';
    pd.innerHTML=`
      <div class="pgroup">
        <div class="props-title">${edgeLabel}</div>
        <div class="props-sub">画布连线 ${node.id.replace('edge-','#')}</div>
      </div>
      <div class="pgroup">
        <div class="pglbl">连接信息</div>
        <div class="prow"><span class="pk">连线类型<</span><span class="pv">${edgeLabel}<</span></div>
        <div class="prow"><span class="pk">源节点<</span><span class="pv">${escapeHtml(sourceName)}<</span></div>
        <div class="prow"><span class="pk">源端口<</span><span class="pv">${escapeHtml(sourcePortName)}<</span></div>
        <div class="prow"><span class="pk">目标节点<</span><span class="pv">${escapeHtml(targetName)}<</span></div>
        <div class="prow"><span class="pk">目标端口<</span><span class="pv">${escapeHtml(targetPortName)}<</span></div>
        <div class="prow"><span class="pk">协议状态<</span><span class="pv ${protocolFault?'pv-fault':'pv-ok'}">${protocolFault?'已注入协议故障':'正常'}<</span></div>
        ${protocolFault?`<div class="prow"><span class="pk">协议故障<</span><span class="pv pv-fault">${escapeHtml(protocolFault.name)}<</span></div>`:''}
      </div>
      <div class="props-form">
        <div class="pgroup">
          <div class="props-help">${isProtocolInjectableEdge(node)?'当前连线为 CAN 总线，可在此导入协议层故障；普通连接线暂不支持协议注入。':'当前选中的是一条独立连线，可直接删除，不影响其他模块。'}</div>
        </div>
        <div class="props-actions">
          ${isProtocolInjectableEdge(node)?`<button class="props-secondary props-protocol-action" onclick="openProtocolFaultImport()">${protocolFault?'更换协议故障':'导入协议故障'}</button>`:''}
          <button class="props-danger" onclick="deleteSelectedEdge()">删除连线</button>
        </div>
      </div>`;
    return;
  }

  const meta=COMPONENT_LIBRARY[node.type];
  const fault=S.faultedBlks.includes(node.id)||Boolean(node.injectedFault);
  const pythonBound=isPythonBoundFlowBlock(node);
  const simulationPackageRows=pythonBound
    ?buildSimulationBlockPackageRows(node)
    :'';
  let fields='';

  if(node.type==='signal_source'){
    fields=`
      <div class="pgroup">
        <div class="pglbl">信号瀹氫箟</div>
        <div class="props-field"><label>模块名称</label><input id="prop-name" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.name)}"></div>
        <div class="props-row">
          <div class="props-field"><label>信号类型</label><select id="prop-waveType">${buildSelectOptions(['正弦','阶跃','常值'],node.props.waveType)}</select></div>
          <div class="props-field"><label>输出鏍煎紡</label><select id="prop-outputFormat">${buildSelectOptions(PORT_FORMATS,node.props.outputFormat)}</select></div>
        </div>
        <div class="props-row">
          <div class="props-field"><label>幅值</label><input id="prop-amplitude" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.amplitude)}"></div>
          <div class="props-field"><label>频率 / 周期</label><input id="prop-frequency" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.frequency)}"></div>
        </div>
        <div class="props-help">信号源用于提供系统建模阶段的输入激励，可在后续继续扩展波形编辑。</div>
      </div>`;
  }else if(node.type==='flow_block'){
    fields=buildFlowBlockFields(node);
  }else if(node.type==='simulation_block'){
    fields=buildSimulationBlockFields(node);
  }else if(node.type.startsWith('fault_')){
    fields=`
      <div class="pgroup">
        <div class="pglbl">故障参数</div>
        <div class="props-field"><label>模块名称</label><input id="prop-name" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.name)}"></div>
        <div class="props-field"><label>故障类型</label><input id="prop-faultType" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.faultType)}"></div>
        <div class="props-row">
          <div class="props-field"><label>作用层级</label><select id="prop-layer">${buildSelectOptions(['物理层','电气层','协议层'],node.props.layer)}</select></div>
          <div class="props-field"><label>触发方式</label><select id="prop-trigger">${buildSelectOptions(['持续','渐变','瞬态','间歇'],node.props.trigger)}</select></div>
        </div>
      </div>`;
  }else if(node.type.startsWith('instrument_')){
    fields=`
      <div class="pgroup">
        <div class="pglbl">观测配置</div>
        <div class="props-field"><label>模块名称</label><input id="prop-name" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.name)}"></div>
        <div class="props-field"><label>观测类型</label><input id="prop-instrumentType" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.instrumentType)}"></div>
        <div class="props-row">
          <div class="props-field"><label>采样率</label><input id="prop-sampleRate" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.sampleRate)}"></div>
          <div class="props-field"><label>观测信号</label><input id="prop-signal" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.signal)}"></div>
        </div>
      </div>`;
  }else{
    fields=`
      <div class="pgroup">
        <div class="pglbl">杩炴帴瀹氫箟</div>
        <div class="props-field"><label>缁勪欢名称</label><input id="prop-name" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.name)}"></div>
        <div class="props-field"><label>杩炴帴类型</label><input id="prop-linkType" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.linkType)}"></div>
        <div class="props-row">
          <div class="props-field"><label>璧风偣端口</label><input id="prop-sourcePort" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.sourcePort)}"></div>
          <div class="props-field"><label>缁堢偣端口</label><input id="prop-targetPort" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.targetPort)}"></div>
        </div>
      </div>`;
  }

  pe.style.display='none';
  pd.style.display='block';
  const faultSummary=node.injectedFault
    ?`<div class="prow"><span class="pk">电气故障<</span><span class="pv pv-fault">${escapeHtml(node.injectedFault.name)}<</span></div>`
    :'';

  pd.innerHTML=`
    <div class="pgroup">
      <div class="props-title">${escapeHtml(node.props.name)}</div>
      <div class="props-sub">${pythonBound?(escapeHtml(node.pythonBinding?.fileName||'')+' · '):''}${meta.label} · 节点 ${node.id.replace('node-','#')}</div>
    </div>
    <div class="pgroup">
      <div class="pglbl">当前状态</div>
      <div class="prow"><span class="pk">鑺傜偣绫诲埆<</span><span class="pv">${meta.label}<</span></div>
      <div class="prow"><span class="pk">状态<</span><span class="pv ${fault?'pv-fault':'pv-ok'}">${fault?'已绑定故障':'正常'}<</span></div>
      ${pythonBound?`<div class="prow"><span class="pk">Python<</span><span class="pv pv-ok">${escapeHtml(getPythonBindingSummary(node))}<</span></div>`:''}
      ${simulationPackageRows}
      ${faultSummary}
    </div>
    <div class="props-form">
      ${fields}
      <div class="props-actions">
        ${node.type==='instrument_scope'?`<button class="props-secondary" onclick="openScope('${node.id}')">查看波形</button>`:''}
        ${node.type==='flow_block'?`<button class="props-secondary" onclick="openPythonBindingDialog('${node.id}')">${pythonBound?'重新绑定 Python':'绑定 Python 文件'}</button>`:''}
        ${node.type==='flow_block'&&pythonBound?`<button class="props-secondary" onclick="unbindPythonBinding('${node.id}')">解除 Python 绑定</button>`:''}
        ${isElectricalInjectableType(node.type)?`<button class="props-secondary props-fault-action" onclick="openElectricalFaultImport()">${node.injectedFault?'更换故障':'导入故障'}</button>`:''}
        <button class="props-save" onclick="saveSelectedNode()">保存设置</button>
        <button class="props-danger" onclick="deleteSelectedNode()">删除模块</button>
      </div>
    </div>`;
}

// ─── Toast ───
let toastT;
function toast(msg,type='w'){
  const el=document.getElementById('toast');
  const ti=document.getElementById('ti');
  const tm=document.getElementById('tm');
  el.className='toast '+(type==='s'?'toast-s':'toast-w')+' on';
  ti.className=type==='s'?'ti-s':'ti-w';
  ti.textContent=type==='s'?'成功':'⚡';
  tm.textContent=msg;
  clearTimeout(toastT);
  toastT=setTimeout(()=>el.classList.remove('on'),3500);
}
