syncConfigTargets = function(preferredId=''){
  const sel=document.getElementById('cftgt');
  if(!sel){return;}
  const currentValue=preferredId||sel.value;
  const nodes=getConfigurableNodes();
  if(nodes.length===0){
    sel.innerHTML='<option value="">请先创建系统建模组件</option>';
    return;
  }
  sel.innerHTML=nodes.map(node=>`<option value="${node.id}">${escapeHtml(node.props.name)} · ${COMPONENT_LIBRARY[node.type].label}</option>`).join('');
  sel.value=nodes.some(node=>node.id===currentValue)?currentValue:nodes[0].id;
};

renderFaultCatalogList = function(){
  __legacyRenderFaultCatalogList();
  const title=document.getElementById('ifm-selected-model');
  if(title){
    const selected=getFaultCatalogModel(S.selectedFaultCatalogId);
    title.textContent=selected?`已选：${selected.name} · ${getLayerLabel(selected.layer)}`:'已选：未选择故障模型';
  }
  const container=document.getElementById('ifm-list-container');
  if(container&&container.textContent.includes('当前')){
    const importedIds=new Set(S.importedFaultModels.map(model=>model.id));
    if(S.availableFaultModels.length===0){
      container.innerHTML='<div class="ifm-empty">当前没有可导入的故障模型，请先从模板库新建。</div>';
      return;
    }
    container.innerHTML='';
    S.availableFaultModels.forEach(model=>{
      const item=document.createElement('div');
      const imported=importedIds.has(model.id);
      item.className=`ifm-item${S.selectedFaultCatalogId===model.id?' on':''}${imported?' is-imported':''}`;
      item.dataset.faultId=model.id;
      const icon=model.layer==='electrical'?'&#9889;':model.layer==='physical'?'&#128295;':'&#128225;';
      item.innerHTML=`
        <div class="ifm-icon ifm-icon--${model.layer}">${icon}</div>
        <div style="min-width:0;flex:1">
          <div class="ifm-name">${escapeHtml(model.name)}</div>
          <div class="ifm-meta">${escapeHtml(buildFaultCatalogMeta(model))}</div>
        </div>
        ${imported?'<span class="ifm-state">已导入<</span>':''}`;
      item.onclick=()=>selectFaultCatalogModel(model.id);
      container.appendChild(item);
    });
  }
};

updateSelectedTplSummary = function(){
  const counter=document.getElementById('sel-cnt');
  const list=document.getElementById('sel-list');
  if(counter){counter.textContent=`已选 ${S.selTpls.length} 个故障模板`;}
  if(list){
    list.innerHTML=S.selTpls.length===0
      ?'<div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--textd);text-align:center;margin-top:6px">暂无</div>'
      :S.selTpls.map(item=>`<div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--purple);padding:3px 6px;border-radius:3px;background:var(--purple-bg);margin-bottom:2px;border:1px solid #ddd6fe">• ${item.name}</div>`).join('');
  }
};

confirmImportFault = function(){
  const selected=getFaultCatalogModel(S.selectedFaultCatalogId);
  if(!selected){toast('请先选择一个故障模型','w');return;}
  ensureImportedFaultModel(selected);
  closeOv('ov-ifm');
  renderFaultCatalogList();
  toast(`故障模型“${selected.name}”已导入工作区`,'s');
  updateUI();
};

showTplDetail = function(t){
  const detail=document.getElementById('tdetail');
  if(!detail){return;}
  if(!t?.id){
    detail.innerHTML='<div class="tdph">→ 选择模板查看详情</div>';
    return;
  }
  detail.innerHTML=`
    <div class="tdtitle">${escapeHtml(t.name)}</div>
    <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text2);line-height:1.6;margin-bottom:10px">${escapeHtml(t.desc||'')}</div>
    <div class="tdlbl">故障层级</div><div class="tdval">${getLayerLabel(t.layer)}</div>
    <div class="tdlbl">故障类别</div><div class="tdval">${escapeHtml(t.tags?.[0]||'故障')}</div>
    <div class="tdlbl">持续特性</div><div class="tdval">${escapeHtml(t.tags?.[1]||'—')}</div>
    <div class="tdlbl">适用场景</div>
    <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text2);margin-top:3px;line-height:1.5">系统建模模块 / 信号链路<br>故障传播与退化仿真</div>
    <div class="tdlbl">幅值范围</div><div class="tdval">±0.01 ~ ±10.0</div>`;
};

computeSourceSignal = function(node,time){
  const amplitude=parseScalar(node.props.amplitude,1);
  const frequency=parseScalar(node.props.frequency,1);
  if(node.props.waveType==='阶跃'){
    const stepTime=Math.max(0.2,frequency);
    return time>=stepTime?amplitude:0;
  }
  if(node.props.waveType==='常值'){
    return amplitude;
  }
  return amplitude*Math.sin(2*Math.PI*frequency*time);
};

applyElectricalFault = function(node,inputValue,outputValue,time){
  if(!node.injectedFault){return outputValue;}
  const modelId=node.injectedFault.modelId||'';
  const importedModel=modelId?getImportedFaultModel(modelId):null;
  const faultValue=parseScalar(importedModel?.defaultValue,0);
  if(modelId==='motor_efficiency_loss'){
    const efficiency=faultValue>0?faultValue:0.55;
    return outputValue*efficiency;
  }
  if(modelId==='motor_lock'){
    return 0;
  }
  if(modelId==='motor_thrust_saturation'){
    const saturation=faultValue>0?faultValue:8;
    return Math.max(-saturation,Math.min(saturation,outputValue));
  }
  const name=node.injectedFault.name||'';
  if(name.includes('过流')){
    return Math.abs(inputValue)>1.2?0:outputValue*0.78;
  }
  if(name.includes('短路')||name.includes('断路')||name.includes('开路')){
    return 0;
  }
  if(name.includes('漂移')){
    return outputValue+Math.min(0.4,time*0.08);
  }
  return outputValue;
};

getScopeSignalName = function(scopeNode){
  const incoming=getIncomingEdgesForNode(scopeNode.id)[0];
  if(!incoming){return '未接入信号';}
  const sourceNode=getNode(incoming.sourceNodeId);
  if(!sourceNode){return '上游信号';}
  const outputPort=getNodePorts(sourceNode).outputs[incoming.sourcePortIndex||0];
  if(outputPort){
    return `${sourceNode.props?.name||'上游信号'} · ${outputPort.label}`;
  }
  return sourceNode.props?.name||'上游信号';
};

validateSimulationTopology = function(){
  if(!S.sysLoaded){toast('请先导入系统模型','w');return false;}
  if(!S.modelNodes.some(node=>node.type==='signal_source')){
    toast('请至少放置一个信号源','w');
    return false;
  }
  if(getScopeNodes().length===0){
    toast('请至少放置一个示波器用于观察信号','w');
    return false;
  }
  if(getConnectedScopeNodes().length===0){
    toast('请至少让一个示波器接入信号链路，才能查看波形','w');
    return false;
  }
  const conflicts=findInputCouplingConflicts();
  if(conflicts.length){
    selectEdge(conflicts[0].id);
    toast('检测到同一输入端口存在多条连线，请先删除多余连线以避免信号耦合','w');
    return false;
  }
  return true;
};

updateSimbarVisualState = function(){
  const runBtn=document.getElementById('sbtn-run');
  const runLbl=document.getElementById('run-lbl');
  const pauseLbl=document.getElementById('pause-lbl');
  if(runBtn){
    runBtn.classList.toggle('active',SIM.running&&!SIM.paused);
  }
  if(runLbl){
    runLbl.textContent=SIM.running&&!SIM.paused?'运行中':'运行';
  }
  if(pauseLbl){
    pauseLbl.textContent=SIM.paused?'继续':'暂停';
  }
};

simInit = function(silent=false){
  __legacySimInit(true);
  if(!SIM.inited||silent){return;}
  const autoSaved=S.systemSaved;
  if(autoSaved&&SIM.time===0&&SIM.stepIndex===0){
    toast(`仿真初始化完成：${SIM.datasetName} · 时长 ${SIM.duration}s · 步长 ${SIM.stepSize}s`,'s');
  }
};

simStep = function(){
  if(!SIM.inited){
    simInit();
    if(!SIM.inited){return;}
  }
  if(SIM.time>=SIM.duration){
    toast('当前仿真已结束，请重新初始化后再步进','w');
    return;
  }
  const completed=runSimulationTick();
  updateSimbarEnabled();
  if(completed){
    simStop('completed');
  }else{
    toast(`步进完成 · t = ${SIM.time.toFixed(2)}s`,'s');
  }
};

simPause = function(){
  if(!SIM.running){return;}
  SIM.paused=!SIM.paused;
  if(SIM.paused){
    clearSimLoop();
    toast('仿真已暂停','w');
  }else{
    startSimulationLoop();
    toast('仿真继续运行','s');
  }
  updateSimbarEnabled();
  updateUI();
};

simStop = function(mode='manual'){
  __legacySimStop(mode);
};

function getSimulationSampleRateLabel(){
  const stepSize=Number(SIM?.stepSize);
  if(!Number.isFinite(stepSize)||stepSize<=0){return '-';}
  const hz=1/stepSize;
  return `${Number(hz.toFixed(hz>=10?0:1))} Hz`;
}

function publishSimulationRuntimeSummary(status='updated'){
  const statusBar=window.__GZ_STATUS_BAR__;
  if(!statusBar?.publishSimulationSummary){
    return {ok:false,reason:'missing-statusbar-runtime'};
  }
  return statusBar.publishSimulationSummary({
    datasetName:SIM?.datasetName||document.getElementById('sim-name')?.value?.trim?.()||'test',
    duration:SIM?.duration||parseScalar(document.getElementById('sim-dur')?.value,0),
    elapsedSeconds:SIM?.time||0,
    faults:S?.faultModels??S?.importedFaultModels?.length??0,
    sampleRate:getSimulationSampleRateLabel(),
    status,
    stepIndex:SIM?.stepIndex||0,
    stepSize:SIM?.stepSize||parseScalar(document.getElementById('sim-step')?.value,0)
  });
}

const __statusSummarySimInit = simInit;
const __statusSummarySimRun = simRun;
const __statusSummarySimStep = simStep;
const __statusSummarySimPause = simPause;
const __statusSummarySimStop = simStop;

simInit = function(silent=false){
  __statusSummarySimInit(silent);
  if(!SIM.inited||silent){return;}
  window.__GZ_STATUS_BAR__?.pushEntry?.({
    level:'info',
    source:'仿真控制',
    message:`初始化 ${SIM.datasetName} · ${SIM.duration}s · step ${SIM.stepSize}s`
  });
};

simRun = function(){
  __statusSummarySimRun();
  if(SIM.running&&!SIM.paused){
    window.__GZ_STATUS_BAR__?.pushEntry?.({
      level:'ok',
      source:'仿真控制',
      message:`运行 ${SIM.datasetName} · ${SIM.duration}s · ${getSimulationSampleRateLabel()}`
    });
  }
};

simStep = function(){
  const beforeStep=SIM.stepIndex;
  __statusSummarySimStep();
  if(SIM.hasSamples&&SIM.stepIndex!==beforeStep){
    publishSimulationRuntimeSummary(SIM.time>=SIM.duration?'completed':'stepped');
  }
};

simPause = function(){
  const beforePaused=SIM.paused;
  __statusSummarySimPause();
  if(SIM.hasSamples&&SIM.paused!==beforePaused){
    publishSimulationRuntimeSummary(SIM.paused?'paused':'running');
  }
};

simStop = function(mode='manual'){
  __statusSummarySimStop(mode);
  if(SIM.hasSamples){
    publishSimulationRuntimeSummary(mode==='completed'?'completed':'stopped');
  }
};

Object.assign(window,{publishSimulationRuntimeSummary});

// --- Final UI/runtime cleanup: Chinese text, instrument inspector, middle variable assignment ---
COMPONENT_LIBRARY.middle_var_assign = {
  label:'中间变量赋值块',
  badge:'赋值',
  className:'b-assign',
  width:176,
  height:82,
  defaults:{
    name:'中间变量赋值块',
    targetNodeId:'',
    targetVarName:'',
    assignMode:'constant',
    constantValue:'0'
  }
};

const __legacyCreateNodeClean = createNode;
const __legacyBuildSimulationResultClean = buildSimulationResult;
const __legacyResolveNodeOutputsClean = resolveNodeOutputs;
const __legacyOpenPythonBindingDialog = openPythonBindingDialog;
const __legacyApplyPythonBindingToNode = applyPythonBindingToNode;
const __legacyUnbindPythonBinding = unbindPythonBinding;
const __legacyBuildNodeSubtitleClean = buildNodeSubtitle;

function buildNamedOptions(options, selectedValue){
  return options.map(option=>{
    const value=typeof option==='string'?option:option.value;
    const label=typeof option==='string'?option:(option.label||option.value);
    return `<option value="${escapeHtml(value)}"${String(value)===String(selectedValue)?' selected':''}>${escapeHtml(label)}</option>`;
  }).join('');
}

function getSimulationMiddleVarDefinitions(node){
  if(!node||node.type!=='simulation_block'){
    return [];
  }
  if(isPythonBoundFlowBlock(node)){
    return (ensureFlowNodePythonBinding(node).portMapping.middleVars||[]).map((item,index)=>({
      name:item.displayName||item.varName||`middle_${index}`,
      type:item.type||'标量',
      varName:item.varName||`middle_${index}`,
      displayName:item.displayName||item.varName||`middle_${index}`
    }));
  }
  normalizeSimulationInterfaces(node.props);
  return (node.props.middleVars||[]).map((item,index)=>({
    name:item.name||`中间量 ${index+1}`,
    type:item.type||'标量',
    varName:item.name||`中间量_${index+1}`,
    displayName:item.name||`中间量 ${index+1}`
  }));
}

function getMiddleAssignmentTargetNodes(){
  return S.modelNodes.filter(node=>node.type==='simulation_block');
}

function getMiddleAssignmentTargetVarOptions(node){
  const targetId=node?.props?.targetNodeId||getMiddleAssignmentTargetNodes()[0]?.id||'';
  const targetNode=getNode(targetId);
  return getSimulationMiddleVarDefinitions(targetNode);
}

function buildInstrumentFields(node){
  return `
    <div class="pgroup">
      <div class="pglbl">测量配置</div>
      <div class="props-field"><label>模块名称</label><input id="prop-name" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.name)}"></div>
      <div class="props-row">
        <div class="props-field"><label>仪器类型</label><input value="${escapeHtml(node.props.instrumentType||COMPONENT_LIBRARY[node.type].label)}" disabled></div>
        <div class="props-field"><label>采样率</label><input id="prop-sampleRate" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.sampleRate||'64kHz')}"></div>
      </div>
      <div class="props-field"><label>观测信号</label><input id="prop-signal" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.signal||'未接入信号')}"></div>
      <div class="props-help">测量仪器用于观察链路中的波形、频谱或记录结果。示波器支持双击直接查看波形。</div>
    </div>`;
}

function buildMiddleAssignmentFields(node){
  const targetNodes=getMiddleAssignmentTargetNodes();
  const activeTargetId=node.props.targetNodeId&&targetNodes.some(item=>item.id===node.props.targetNodeId)
    ?node.props.targetNodeId
    :(targetNodes[0]?.id||'');
  const targetNode=getNode(activeTargetId);
  const varOptions=getSimulationMiddleVarDefinitions(targetNode);
  const activeVarName=node.props.targetVarName&&varOptions.some(item=>item.name===node.props.targetVarName)
    ?node.props.targetVarName
    :(varOptions[0]?.name||'');

  return `
    <div class="pgroup">
      <div class="pglbl">赋值配置</div>
      <div class="props-field"><label>模块名称</label><input id="prop-name" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.name)}"></div>
      <div class="props-row">
        <div class="props-field"><label>目标仿真块</label><select id="prop-targetNodeId" onchange="refreshMiddleAssignEditor()">${targetNodes.length
          ?targetNodes.map(item=>`<option value="${item.id}"${item.id===activeTargetId?' selected':''}>${escapeHtml(item.props.name)}</option>`).join('')
          :'<option value="">请先创建仿真块</option>'}</select></div>
        <div class="props-field"><label>目标中间变量</label><select id="prop-targetVarName">${varOptions.length
          ?varOptions.map(item=>`<option value="${escapeHtml(item.name)}"${item.name===activeVarName?' selected':''}>${escapeHtml(`${item.name} / ${item.type}`)}</option>`).join('')
          :'<option value="">暂无可写变量</option>'}</select></div>
      </div>
      <div class="props-row">
        <div class="props-field"><label>赋值方式</label><select id="prop-assignMode" onchange="refreshMiddleAssignEditor()">${buildNamedOptions([{value:'input',label:'输入覆盖'},{value:'constant',label:'常值覆盖'}],node.props.assignMode||'constant')}</select></div>
        <div class="props-field"><label>常值</label><input id="prop-constantValue" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.constantValue||'0')}" ${node.props.assignMode==='input'?'disabled':''}></div>
      </div>
      <div class="props-help">中间变量赋值块用于将输入信号或常值写入目标仿真块的中间变量。当前顶部端口仍作为观测输出存在，赋值操作通过该模块在运行时完成。</div>
    </div>`;
}

function refreshMiddleAssignEditor(){
  const node=getNode(S.selBlk);
  if(!node||node.type!=='middle_var_assign'){
    return;
  }
  const nextTarget=document.getElementById('prop-targetNodeId')?.value;
  const nextMode=document.getElementById('prop-assignMode')?.value;
  if(nextTarget!==undefined){
    node.props.targetNodeId=nextTarget;
  }
  if(nextMode!==undefined){
    node.props.assignMode=nextMode;
  }
  renderPropertyPanel(node);
}

function getMiddleAssignmentResolvedTarget(node){
  const targetNode=getNode(node?.props?.targetNodeId||'');
  if(!targetNode||targetNode.type!=='simulation_block'){
    return null;
  }
  const defs=getSimulationMiddleVarDefinitions(targetNode);
  const targetVar=defs.find(item=>item.name===node.props.targetVarName)||defs[0]||null;
  if(!targetVar){
    return null;
  }
  return {targetNode,targetVar};
}

function clearAssignedMiddleValues(bucket){
  if(!bucket?.nodeState){
    return;
  }
  Object.values(bucket.nodeState).forEach(nodeState=>{
    if(nodeState&&nodeState.assignedMiddleValues){
      nodeState.assignedMiddleValues={};
    }
  });
}

function readMiddleAssignmentValue(node,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting){
  if(node.props.assignMode==='input'){
    const inputValues=resolveNodeInputValues(node,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting);
    return sanitizeSignalValue(inputValues[0]??0);
  }
  return sanitizeSignalValue(parseScalar(node.props.constantValue,0));
}

function applyMiddleAssignmentsForMode(modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting){
  const bucket=modeKey==='reference'?SIM.reference:SIM.actual;
  S.modelNodes.filter(node=>node.type==='middle_var_assign').forEach(node=>{
    const targetInfo=getMiddleAssignmentResolvedTarget(node);
    const nodeState=ensureNodeRuntime(bucket,node);
    if(!targetInfo){
      nodeState.lastAssignedValue=0;
      return;
    }
    const value=readMiddleAssignmentValue(node,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting);
    nodeState.lastAssignedValue=value;
    const targetState=ensureNodeRuntime(bucket,targetInfo.targetNode);
    if(!targetState.assignedMiddleValues){
      targetState.assignedMiddleValues={};
    }
    targetState.assignedMiddleValues[targetInfo.targetVar.name]=value;
  });
}

function primeSimulationNodeStateFromAssignments(node,nodeState){
  const assigned=nodeState?.assignedMiddleValues||{};
  const middleDefs=getSimulationMiddleVarDefinitions(node);
  const firstVar=middleDefs[0];
  if(!firstVar||!Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(assigned,firstVar.name)){
    return;
  }
  const seed=sanitizeSignalValue(assigned[firstVar.name]);
  if(node.props.moduleType==='积分'){
    nodeState.integrator=seed;
  }else if(node.props.moduleType==='微分'){
    nodeState.prevAggregateInput=seed;
  }else{
    nodeState.firstOrder=seed;
  }
}

function applyAssignedMiddleValues(node,nodeState,resolved){
  const assigned=nodeState?.assignedMiddleValues||{};
  const middleDefs=getSimulationMiddleVarDefinitions(node);
  if(!resolved.middleValues){
    resolved.middleValues=[];
  }
  const firstAssignedName=middleDefs[0]?.name;
  const firstAssignedValue=firstAssignedName&&Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(assigned,firstAssignedName)
    ?sanitizeSignalValue(assigned[firstAssignedName])
    :undefined;
  middleDefs.forEach((item,index)=>{
    if(Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(assigned,item.name)){
      resolved.middleValues[index]=sanitizeSignalValue(assigned[item.name]);
    }
  });
  if(firstAssignedValue!==undefined&&resolved.outputs?.length){
    resolved.outputs[0]=firstAssignedValue;
    if(resolved.outputs.length>1){
      resolved.outputs[1]=firstAssignedValue;
    }
  }
  return resolved;
}

toast = function(msg,type='w'){
  const el=document.getElementById('toast');
  const ti=document.getElementById('ti');
  const tm=document.getElementById('tm');
  if(!el||!ti||!tm){return;}
  el.className=`toast ${type==='s'?'toast-s':'toast-w'} on`;
  ti.className=type==='s'?'ti-s':'ti-w';
  ti.textContent=type==='s'?'成功':'提示';
  tm.textContent=msg;
  clearTimeout(toastT);
  toastT=setTimeout(()=>el.classList.remove('on'),3500);
};

openPythonBindingDialog = function(nodeId=''){
  const target=getNode(nodeId||S.selBlk);
  if(!target||target.type!=='simulation_block'){
    toast('请先选中仿真块，再绑定 Python 文件','w');
    return;
  }
  return __legacyOpenPythonBindingDialog(nodeId);
};

applyPythonBindingToNode = function(nodeId,binding){
  const node=getNode(nodeId);
  if(!node||node.type!=='simulation_block'){return;}
  node.pythonBinding=cloneDefaults(binding);
  applyNodeGeometry(node);
  const removedEdges=pruneInvalidEdgesForNode(node);
  syncAllPythonInputConnectionState();
  markTopologyDirty('system');
  renderModelNodes();
  selectNode(node.id);
  syncConfigTargets(node.id);
  updateUI();
  toast(`已为 ${node.props.name} 绑定 ${binding.fileName}${removedEdges?`，并清理 ${removedEdges} 条失效连线`:''}`,'s');
};

unbindPythonBinding = function(nodeId=''){
  const node=getNode(nodeId||S.selBlk);
  if(!node||node.type!=='simulation_block'){
    return;
  }
  const binding=ensureFlowNodePythonBinding(node);
  if(!binding.bound){
    toast('当前仿真块尚未绑定 Python 文件','w');
    return;
  }
  node.pythonBinding=createDefaultPythonBinding();
  applyNodeGeometry(node);
  const removedEdges=pruneInvalidEdgesForNode(node);
  syncAllPythonInputConnectionState();
  markTopologyDirty('system');
  renderModelNodes();
  selectNode(node.id);
  syncConfigTargets(node.id);
  updateUI();
  toast(`已解除 ${node.props.name} 的 Python 绑定${removedEdges?`，并清理 ${removedEdges} 条失效连线`:''}`,'s');
};

getNodePorts = function(node){
  if(!node){
    return {inputs:[],outputs:[]};
  }
  if(node.type==='signal_source'){
    return {
      inputs:[],
      outputs:[{key:'signal',label:node.props.outputFormat||'输出',kind:'output',side:'right'}]
    };
  }
  if(node.type==='flow_block'){
    return {
      inputs:[{key:'input',label:node.props.inputName||'输入',kind:'input',side:'left'}],
      outputs:[{key:'output',label:node.props.outputName||'输出',kind:'output',side:'right'}]
    };
  }
  if(node.type==='simulation_block'){
    if(isPythonBoundFlowBlock(node)){
      const binding=ensureFlowNodePythonBinding(node);
      return {
        inputs:binding.portMapping.inputs.map((item,index)=>({
          key:`input-${index}`,
          label:item.displayName||item.varName||`input_${index}`,
          kind:'input',
          side:'left',
          meta:item
        })),
        outputs:[
          ...binding.portMapping.outputs.map((item,index)=>({
            key:`output-${index}`,
            label:item.displayName||item.varName||`output_${index}`,
            kind:'output',
            side:'right',
            meta:item
          })),
          ...binding.portMapping.middleVars.map((item,index)=>({
            key:`middle-${index}`,
            label:item.displayName||item.varName||`middle_${index}`,
            kind:'middle',
            side:'top',
            meta:item
          }))
        ]
      };
    }
    const groups=getSimulationPortSets(node.props);
    return {
      inputs:groups.inputs.map((item,index)=>({
        key:`input-${index}`,
        label:`输入 ${index+1} · ${item.name} / ${item.type}`,
        kind:'input',
        side:'left'
      })),
      outputs:getSimulationFlatOutputs(node.props).map((item,index)=>({
        key:`${item.kind}-${item.index}`,
        label:`${item.kind==='middle'?'中间量':'输出'} ${item.index+1} · ${item.name} / ${item.type}`,
        kind:item.kind,
        side:item.side,
        portIndex:index
      }))
    };
  }
  if(node.type==='middle_var_assign'){
    return {
      inputs:[{key:'assign-input',label:'赋值输入',kind:'input',side:'left'}],
      outputs:[]
    };
  }
  if(node.type.startsWith('fault_')){
    return {
      inputs:[{key:'input',label:'故障输入',kind:'input',side:'left'}],
      outputs:[{key:'output',label:'故障输出',kind:'output',side:'right'}]
    };
  }
  if(node.type.startsWith('instrument_')){
    return {
      inputs:[{key:'input',label:'观测输入',kind:'input',side:'left'}],
      outputs:[]
    };
  }
  return {inputs:[],outputs:[]};
};

buildNodeSubtitle = function(node){
  const props=node.props||{};
  const faultNote=node.injectedFault?' · 电气故障':'';
  if(node.type==='middle_var_assign'){
    const targetInfo=getMiddleAssignmentResolvedTarget(node);
    const targetName=targetInfo?.targetNode?.props?.name||'未选择目标';
    const varName=targetInfo?.targetVar?.name||'未选择变量';
    const modeLabel=props.assignMode==='input'?'输入覆盖':'常值覆盖';
    return `${targetName} · ${varName} · ${modeLabel}`;
  }
  switch(node.type){
    case 'signal_source':
      return `${props.waveType||'正弦'} · 幅值 ${props.amplitude} · ${props.outputFormat||'标量'}`;
    case 'flow_block':
      return `${props.inputName||'输入'} → ${props.outputName||'输出'} · ${props.outputFormat||'标量'}${faultNote}`;
    case 'simulation_block':
      normalizeSimulationInterfaces(props);
      return `${props.inputs.length}输入 · ${props.outputs.length}输出 · ${props.middleVars.length}中间变量 · ${props.moduleType||'一阶函数'}${faultNote}`;
    case 'instrument_scope':
      return `${props.instrumentType||'示波器'} · 双击查看波形`;
    case 'instrument_spectrum':
    case 'instrument_logger':
      return `${props.instrumentType||COMPONENT_LIBRARY[node.type].label} · 采样率 ${props.sampleRate||'未设置'}`;
    default:
      return __legacyBuildNodeSubtitleClean(node);
  }
};

createNode = function(type,rawX,rawY){
  if(type==='subsystem_block'){
    const result=__legacyCreateNodeClean(type,rawX,rawY);
    const node=getNode(S.selBlk)||S.modelNodes[S.modelNodes.length-1];
    if(!node){return result;}
    node.props.name=`子系统块 ${getNodeTypeCount(type)}`;
    ensureSubsystemCanvasNode(node);
    renderModelNodes();
    syncConfigTargets(node.id);
    selectNode(node.id);
    updateUI();
    return result;
  }
  if(type!=='middle_var_assign'){
    return __legacyCreateNodeClean(type,rawX,rawY);
  }
  const meta=COMPONENT_LIBRARY[type];
  if(!meta){return;}
  const props=cloneDefaults(meta.defaults);
  props.name=`中间变量赋值块 ${getNodeTypeCount(type)}`;
  const point={
    x:clamp(Math.round(rawX-meta.width/2),CANVAS_STAGE.nodePadding,CANVAS_STAGE.width-meta.width-CANVAS_STAGE.nodePadding),
    y:clamp(Math.round(rawY-meta.height/2),CANVAS_STAGE.nodeMinY,CANVAS_STAGE.height-meta.height-CANVAS_STAGE.nodePadding)
  };
  S.modelNodes.push({
    id:`node-${++S.nodeSeq}`,
    type,
    x:point.x,
    y:point.y,
    w:meta.width,
    h:meta.height,
    props,
    pythonBinding:null
  });
  markTopologyDirty('system');
  const node=S.modelNodes[S.modelNodes.length-1];
  renderModelNodes();
  syncConfigTargets(node.id);
  selectNode(node.id);
  updateUI();
  toast(`${meta.label} 已加入画布`,'s');
};

renderModelNodes = function(){
  const layer=document.getElementById('node-layer');
  if(!layer){return;}
  layer.innerHTML='';
  S.modelNodes.forEach(node=>{
    applyNodeGeometry(node);
    const meta=COMPONENT_LIBRARY[node.type];
    const faulted=S.faultedBlks.includes(node.id)||Boolean(node.injectedFault);
    const pythonBound=node.type==='simulation_block'&&isPythonBoundFlowBlock(node);
    const el=document.createElement('div');
    el.id=`b-${node.id}`;
    el.className=`blk ${meta.className}${S.selBlk===node.id?' sel':''}${faulted?' faulted':''}${pythonBound?' python-bound':''}`;
    el.style.left=`${node.x}px`;
    el.style.top=`${node.y}px`;
    el.style.width=`${node.w}px`;
    el.style.height=`${node.h}px`;
    if(node.type==='simulation_block'){
      const topPortCount=getSimulationMiddleVarDefinitions(node).length;
      el.style.paddingTop=`${topPortCount?18:10}px`;
      el.style.paddingBottom='10px';
    }else{
      el.style.paddingTop='';
      el.style.paddingBottom='';
    }

    const nodeTitle=pythonBound?(node.pythonBinding?.fileName||node.props.name):node.props.name;
    const nodeSubtitle=buildNodeSubtitle(node);
    const showInlinePortLabels=!(pythonBound&&node.type==='simulation_block');
    el.innerHTML=`
      <div class="fbadge">F</div>
      ${pythonBound?'<div class="node-card__python-chip">Py</div>':''}
      <div class="blk-kicker">${pythonBound?'已绑定 Python':(faulted&&!isFaultNodeType(node.type)?`${meta.badge} 故障`:meta.badge)}</div>
      <div class="blk-lbl">${escapeHtml(nodeTitle)}</div>
      <div class="blk-sub">${escapeHtml(nodeSubtitle)}</div>`;

    el.addEventListener('pointerdown',event=>beginNodeDrag(event,node.id));
    el.addEventListener('click',event=>{
      if(event.target.closest('.node-port')){return;}
      if(Date.now()<NODE_DRAG.clickSuppressUntil){return;}
      selectNode(node.id);
      const now=Date.now();
      const isDouble=NODE_DOUBLE_CLICK.nodeId===node.id&&(now-NODE_DOUBLE_CLICK.timestamp)<320;
      NODE_DOUBLE_CLICK.nodeId=node.id;
      NODE_DOUBLE_CLICK.timestamp=now;
      if(!isDouble){return;}
      if(node.type==='instrument_scope'){
        openScope(node.id);
      }else if(node.type==='simulation_block'){
        openPythonBindingDialog(node.id);
      }else if(node.type==='subsystem_block'){
        openSubsystemCanvas(node.id);
      }
    });

    if(node.type==='instrument_scope'){
      el.title='双击查看示波器';
      el.addEventListener('dblclick',event=>{
        event.stopPropagation();
        openScope(node.id);
      });
    }else if(node.type==='simulation_block'){
      el.title=pythonBound
        ?`已绑定 Python：${node.pythonBinding?.fileName||'unknown.py'}\n双击可重新绑定`
        :'双击绑定 Python 文件';
      el.addEventListener('dblclick',event=>{
        event.stopPropagation();
        openPythonBindingDialog(node.id);
      });
    }else if(node.type==='middle_var_assign'){
      el.title='将输入信号或常值写入目标仿真块的中间变量';
    }

    const ports=getNodePorts(node);
    ports.inputs.forEach((port,index)=>{
      const info=getPortInfo(node,'input',index);
      const portEl=document.createElement('button');
      portEl.type='button';
      portEl.className='node-port node-port--input';
      portEl.style.left=`${info.localX}px`;
      portEl.style.top=`${info.localY}px`;
      portEl.style.color=getPortTone(node,port,'input');
      portEl.title=getPortTooltip(port,'input');
      if(isPortConnected(node.id,'input',index)){
        portEl.classList.add('is-connected');
      }
      if(S.pendingConnection){
        portEl.classList.add('node-port--active');
      }
      portEl.innerHTML='<span class="node-port__inner"><</span>';
      if(showInlinePortLabels){
        appendPortLabel(portEl,port);
      }
      portEl.addEventListener('click',event=>handlePortClick(event,node.id,'input',index));
      el.appendChild(portEl);
    });

    ports.outputs.forEach((port,index)=>{
      const info=getPortInfo(node,'output',index);
      const portEl=document.createElement('button');
      portEl.type='button';
      portEl.className=`node-port node-port--output${info.side==='top'?' node-port--top':''}`;
      portEl.style.left=`${info.localX}px`;
      portEl.style.top=`${info.localY}px`;
      portEl.style.color=getPortTone(node,port,'output');
      portEl.title=getPortTooltip(port,'output');
      if(isPortConnected(node.id,'output',index)){
        portEl.classList.add('is-connected');
      }
      if(S.pendingConnection&&S.pendingConnection.sourceNodeId===node.id&&(S.pendingConnection.sourcePortIndex||0)===index){
        portEl.classList.add('node-port--active');
      }
      portEl.innerHTML='<span class="node-port__inner"><</span>';
      if(showInlinePortLabels){
        appendPortLabel(portEl,port);
      }
      portEl.addEventListener('click',event=>handlePortClick(event,node.id,'output',index));
      el.appendChild(portEl);
    });

    layer.appendChild(el);
  });
  renderEdges();
  const placeholder=document.getElementById('diagram-placeholder');
  if(placeholder){
    placeholder.style.display=S.modelNodes.length?'none':'flex';
  }
};

renderPropertyPanel = function(node){
  if(!node||node.sourceNodeId&&node.targetNodeId&&!node.type){
    return __legacyRenderPropertyPanel(node);
  }
  if(node.type!=='signal_source'&&node.type!=='flow_block'&&node.type!=='simulation_block'&&node.type!=='middle_var_assign'&&node.type!=='subsystem_block'&&!node.type.startsWith('instrument_')){
    return __legacyRenderPropertyPanel(node);
  }

  const pe=document.getElementById('pe');
  const pd=document.getElementById('pd');
  const meta=COMPONENT_LIBRARY[node.type];
  const fault=S.faultedBlks.includes(node.id)||Boolean(node.injectedFault);
  const pythonBound=node.type==='simulation_block'&&isPythonBoundFlowBlock(node);
  let fields='';

  if(node.type==='signal_source'){
    fields=`
      <div class="pgroup">
        <div class="pglbl">信号定义</div>
        <div class="props-field"><label>模块名称</label><input id="prop-name" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.name)}"></div>
        <div class="props-row">
          <div class="props-field"><label>信号类型</label><select id="prop-waveType">${buildSelectOptions(['正弦','阶跃','常值'],node.props.waveType)}</select></div>
          <div class="props-field"><label>输出格式</label><select id="prop-outputFormat">${buildSelectOptions(PORT_FORMATS,node.props.outputFormat)}</select></div>
        </div>
        <div class="props-row">
          <div class="props-field"><label>幅值</label><input id="prop-amplitude" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.amplitude)}"></div>
          <div class="props-field"><label>频率 / 周期</label><input id="prop-frequency" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.frequency)}"></div>
        </div>
        <div class="props-help">信号源用于提供系统建模阶段的输入激励，可继续作为 Python 仿真块或流程块的上游输入。</div>
      </div>`;
  }else if(node.type==='flow_block'){
    fields=buildFlowBlockFields(node);
  }else if(node.type==='simulation_block'){
    fields=buildSimulationBlockFields(node);
  }else if(node.type==='middle_var_assign'){
    fields=buildMiddleAssignmentFields(node);
  }else if(node.type==='subsystem_block'){
    const canvas=ensureSubsystemCanvasNode(node);
    fields=`
      <div class="pgroup">
        <div class="pglbl">子系统设置</div>
        <div class="props-field"><label>模块名称</label><input id="prop-name" value="${escapeHtml(node.props.name)}"></div>
        <div class="props-field"><label>模块说明</label><textarea id="prop-description" rows="3" placeholder="可填写子系统职责、输入输出说明">${escapeHtml(node.props.description||'')}</textarea></div>
        <div class="prow"><span class="pk">子画布 ID</span><span class="pv">${escapeHtml(node.targetCanvasId||canvas?.id||'--')}<</span></div>
      </div>`;
  }else if(node.type.startsWith('instrument_')){
    fields=buildInstrumentFields(node);
  }
  const simulationPackageRows=node.type==='simulation_block'&&pythonBound
    ?buildSimulationBlockPackageRows(node)
    :'';

  const subtitle=pythonBound
    ?`${escapeHtml(node.pythonBinding?.fileName||'')} · ${meta.label} · 节点 ${node.id.replace('node-','#')}`
    :`${meta.label} · 节点 ${node.id.replace('node-','#')}`;
  const faultSummary=node.injectedFault
    ?`<div class="prow"><span class="pk">电气故障<</span><span class="pv pv-fault">${escapeHtml(node.injectedFault.name)}<</span></div>`
    :'';
  const extraAction=node.type==='instrument_scope'
    ?`<button class="props-secondary" onclick="openScope('${node.id}')">查看波形</button>`
    :'';

  pe.style.display='none';
  pd.style.display='block';
  pd.innerHTML=`
    <div class="pgroup">
      <div class="props-title">${escapeHtml(node.props.name)}</div>
      <div class="props-sub">${subtitle}</div>
    </div>
    <div class="pgroup">
      <div class="pglbl">当前状态</div>
      <div class="prow"><span class="pk">节点类别<</span><span class="pv">${meta.label}<</span></div>
      <div class="prow"><span class="pk">状态<</span><span class="pv ${fault?'pv-fault':'pv-ok'}">${fault?'已绑定故障':'正常'}<</span></div>
      ${pythonBound?`<div class="prow"><span class="pk">Python<</span><span class="pv pv-ok">${escapeHtml(getPythonBindingSummary(node))}<</span></div>`:''}
      ${faultSummary}
    </div>
    <div class="props-form">
      ${fields}
      <div class="props-actions">
        ${node.type==='simulation_block'?`<button class="props-secondary" onclick="openPythonBindingDialog('${node.id}')">${pythonBound?'重新绑定 Python':'绑定 Python 文件'}</button>`:''}
        ${node.type==='simulation_block'&&pythonBound?`<button class="props-secondary" onclick="unbindPythonBinding('${node.id}')">解除 Python 绑定</button>`:''}
        ${isElectricalInjectableType(node.type)?`<button class="props-secondary props-fault-action" onclick="openElectricalFaultImport()">${node.injectedFault?'更换故障':'导入故障'}</button>`:''}
        ${extraAction}
        <button class="props-save" onclick="saveSelectedNode()">保存设置</button>
        <button class="props-danger" onclick="deleteSelectedNode()">删除模块</button>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  if(node.type==='simulation_block'){
    updateModelPackageStatus(node);
  }
};

saveSelectedNode = function(){
  const node=getNode(S.selBlk);
  if(!node){return;}
  if(node.type==='signal_source'){
    node.props.name=document.getElementById('prop-name').value.trim()||node.props.name;
    node.props.waveType=document.getElementById('prop-waveType').value;
    node.props.outputFormat=document.getElementById('prop-outputFormat').value;
    node.props.amplitude=document.getElementById('prop-amplitude').value.trim()||node.props.amplitude;
    node.props.frequency=document.getElementById('prop-frequency').value.trim()||node.props.frequency;
  }else if(node.type==='flow_block'){
    node.props.name=document.getElementById('prop-name').value.trim()||node.props.name;
    node.props.inputName=document.getElementById('prop-inputName').value.trim()||'输入信号';
    node.props.inputFormat=document.getElementById('prop-inputFormat').value;
    node.props.outputName=document.getElementById('prop-outputName').value.trim()||'输出信号';
    node.props.outputFormat=document.getElementById('prop-outputFormat').value;
  }else if(node.type==='simulation_block'){
    node.props.name=document.getElementById('prop-name').value.trim()||node.props.name;
    if(!isPythonBoundFlowBlock(node)){
      node.props.moduleType=document.getElementById('prop-moduleType').value;
      node.props.inputs=readSimulationInterfaceRows('输入');
      node.props.outputs=readSimulationInterfaceRows('输出');
      node.props.middleVars=readSimulationInterfaceRows('中间量');
      normalizeSimulationInterfaces(node.props);
      node.props.inputs=normalizeSimulationInterfaceList(
        node.props.inputs.slice(0,clampInterfaceCount(document.getElementById('sim-input-count')?.value,SIM_INTERFACE_LIMITS.inputs)),
        '输入',
        node.props.inputs[0]?.type||'标量',
        clampInterfaceCount(document.getElementById('sim-input-count')?.value,SIM_INTERFACE_LIMITS.inputs)
      );
      node.props.outputs=normalizeSimulationInterfaceList(
        node.props.outputs.slice(0,clampInterfaceCount(document.getElementById('sim-output-count')?.value,SIM_INTERFACE_LIMITS.outputs)),
        '输出',
        node.props.outputs[0]?.type||'标量',
        clampInterfaceCount(document.getElementById('sim-output-count')?.value,SIM_INTERFACE_LIMITS.outputs)
      );
      node.props.middleVars=normalizeSimulationInterfaceList(
        node.props.middleVars.slice(0,clampInterfaceCount(document.getElementById('sim-middle-count')?.value,SIM_INTERFACE_LIMITS.middleVars)),
        '中间量',
        node.props.middleVars[0]?.type||'标量',
        clampInterfaceCount(document.getElementById('sim-middle-count')?.value,SIM_INTERFACE_LIMITS.middleVars)
      );
      node.props.ffunctionNote=document.getElementById('prop-ffunctionNote').value.trim()||'当前预留 Python 函数接口，可在后续导入函数定义。';
      applyNodeGeometry(node);
      pruneInvalidEdgesForNode(node);
    }
  }else if(node.type==='middle_var_assign'){
    node.props.name=document.getElementById('prop-name').value.trim()||node.props.name;
    node.props.targetNodeId=document.getElementById('prop-targetNodeId').value;
    const options=getSimulationMiddleVarDefinitions(getNode(node.props.targetNodeId));
    const selectedVar=document.getElementById('prop-targetVarName').value;
    node.props.targetVarName=options.some(item=>item.name===selectedVar)?selectedVar:(options[0]?.name||'');
    node.props.assignMode=document.getElementById('prop-assignMode').value;
    node.props.constantValue=document.getElementById('prop-constantValue').value.trim()||'0';
  }else if(node.type==='subsystem_block'){
    node.props.name=document.getElementById('prop-name').value.trim()||node.props.name;
    node.props.description=document.getElementById('prop-description')?.value.trim()||'';
    const canvas=ensureSubsystemCanvasNode(node);
    if(canvas){
      canvas.name=node.props.name;
    }
  }else if(node.type.startsWith('instrument_')){
    node.props.name=document.getElementById('prop-name').value.trim()||node.props.name;
    node.props.sampleRate=document.getElementById('prop-sampleRate').value.trim()||node.props.sampleRate;
    node.props.signal=document.getElementById('prop-signal').value.trim()||node.props.signal;
  }else{
    return __legacySaveSelectedNode();
  }

  markTopologyDirty(getMutationScopeForType(node.type));
  renderModelNodes();
  renderPropertyPanel(node);
  syncConfigTargets(node.id);
  updateUI();
};

buildSimulationResult = function(node,nodeState,inputValues,modeKey,time,dt){
  primeSimulationNodeStateFromAssignments(node,nodeState);
  const resolved=__legacyBuildSimulationResultClean(node,nodeState,inputValues,modeKey,time,dt);
  return applyAssignedMiddleValues(node,nodeState,resolved);
};

function getCanvasNodeById(canvasId,nodeId){
  return S.canvases?.[canvasId]?.nodes?.find(node=>node.id===nodeId)||null;
}

function getIncomingEdgesForCanvasNode(canvasId,nodeId){
  return (S.canvases?.[canvasId]?.edges||[])
    .filter(edge=>edge.targetNodeId===nodeId)
    .sort((a,b)=>(a.targetPortIndex||0)-(b.targetPortIndex||0)||a.id.localeCompare(b.id));
}

function getSubsystemBoundaryNodeForPort(canvasId,role,interfacePortId){
  const nodeType=role==='input'?'subsystem_in_port':'subsystem_out_port';
  return (S.canvases?.[canvasId]?.nodes||[]).find(node=>
    node.type===nodeType&&node.props?.interfacePortId===interfacePortId
  )||null;
}

function finalizeResolvedNodeOutputs(node,nodeState,inputValues,resolved){
  resolved.outputs=(resolved.outputs||[0]).map(sanitizeSignalValue);
  resolved.middleValues=(resolved.middleValues||[]).map(sanitizeSignalValue);
  nodeState.lastInputValues=inputValues.slice();
  nodeState.lastInput=inputValues[0]||0;
  nodeState.lastOutputs=resolved.outputs.slice();
  nodeState.lastMiddleValues=resolved.middleValues.slice();
  nodeState.lastOutput=nodeState.lastOutputs[0]||0;
  return resolved;
}

function resolveCanvasNodeOutput(canvasId,nodeId,outputIndex,modeKey,time,dt,context){
  const node=getCanvasNodeById(canvasId,nodeId);
  const resolved=resolveCanvasNodeOutputs(canvasId,nodeId,modeKey,time,dt,context);
  if(!node){return 0;}
  if(node.type==='simulation_block'){
    normalizeSimulationInterfaces(node.props);
    const mainCount=node.props.outputs.length;
    if(outputIndex<mainCount){
      return sanitizeSignalValue(resolved.outputs[outputIndex]??resolved.outputs[0]??0);
    }
    return sanitizeSignalValue(resolved.middleValues[outputIndex-mainCount]??resolved.outputs[0]??0);
  }
  return sanitizeSignalValue(resolved.outputs[outputIndex]??resolved.outputs[0]??0);
}

function evaluateSubsystemOutputsFromInputs(node,inputValues,modeKey,time,dt){
  const canvas=ensureSubsystemCanvasNode(node);
  const intf=ensureSubsystemInterface(node);
  const boundaryInputs={};
  intf.inputs.forEach((item,index)=>{
    boundaryInputs[item.id]=sanitizeSignalValue(inputValues[index]??0);
  });
  const context={
    cache:new Map(),
    visiting:new Set(),
    boundaryInputs
  };
  return {
    outputs:intf.outputs.map(item=>{
      const outputNode=getSubsystemBoundaryNodeForPort(canvas.id,'output',item.id);
      return outputNode
        ?resolveCanvasNodeOutput(canvas.id,outputNode.id,0,modeKey,time,dt,context)
        :0;
    }),
    middleValues:[]
  };
}

function resolveCanvasNodeOutputs(canvasId,nodeId,modeKey,time,dt,context){
  const cacheKey=`${canvasId}:${nodeId}`;
  if(context.cache.has(cacheKey)){
    return context.cache.get(cacheKey);
  }
  const node=getCanvasNodeById(canvasId,nodeId);
  if(!node){
    return {outputs:[0],middleValues:[]};
  }
  const bucket=modeKey==='reference'?SIM.reference:SIM.actual;
  const nodeState=ensureNodeRuntime(bucket,node);
  if(context.visiting.has(cacheKey)){
    const responsePoint={
      outputs:nodeState.lastOutputs?.length?nodeState.lastOutputs:[nodeState.lastOutput||0],
      middleValues:nodeState.lastMiddleValues||[]
    };
  }
  context.visiting.add(cacheKey);
  const inputPorts=getNodePorts(node).inputs||[];
  const incoming=getIncomingEdgesForCanvasNode(canvasId,node.id);
  const inputValues=node.type==='subsystem_in_port'
    ?[]
    :inputPorts.map((_,portIndex)=>{
      const edge=incoming.find(item=>(item.targetPortIndex||0)===portIndex);
      if(!edge){return 0;}
      const upstream=resolveCanvasNodeOutput(canvasId,edge.sourceNodeId,edge.sourcePortIndex||0,modeKey,time,dt,context);
      return transmitEdgeSignal(edge,upstream,modeKey,time);
    });
  let resolved={outputs:[0],middleValues:[]};
  if(node.type==='signal_source'){
    resolved={outputs:[computeSourceSignal(node,time)],middleValues:[]};
  }else if(node.type==='flow_block'){
    resolved=isPythonBoundFlowBlock(node)
      ?executeBoundFlowBlock(node,nodeState,inputValues,modeKey,time,dt)
      :{outputs:[sanitizeSignalValue(inputValues[0]||0)],middleValues:[]};
  }else if(node.type==='simulation_block'){
    resolved=isPythonBoundFlowBlock(node)
      ?applyAssignedMiddleValues(node,nodeState,executeBoundFlowBlock(node,nodeState,inputValues,modeKey,time,dt))
      :buildSimulationResult(node,nodeState,inputValues,modeKey,time,dt);
  }else if(node.type==='subsystem_in_port'){
    resolved={outputs:[sanitizeSignalValue(context.boundaryInputs?.[node.props?.interfacePortId]??0)],middleValues:[]};
  }else if(node.type==='subsystem_out_port'){
    resolved={outputs:[sanitizeSignalValue(inputValues[0]||0)],middleValues:[]};
  }else if(node.type==='subsystem_block'){
    resolved=evaluateSubsystemOutputsFromInputs(node,inputValues,modeKey,time,dt);
  }else if(node.type?.startsWith('fault_')){
    resolved={outputs:[applyPhysicalFaultNode(node,sanitizeSignalValue(inputValues[0]||0),time,modeKey)],middleValues:[]};
  }else if(node.type?.startsWith('instrument_')){
    resolved={outputs:[sanitizeSignalValue(inputValues[0]||0)],middleValues:[]};
  }else{
    resolved={outputs:[sanitizeSignalValue(inputValues[0]||0)],middleValues:[]};
  }
  finalizeResolvedNodeOutputs(node,nodeState,inputValues,resolved);
  context.visiting.delete(cacheKey);
  context.cache.set(cacheKey,resolved);
  return resolved;
}

resolveNodeOutputs = function(nodeId,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting){
  const node=getNode(nodeId);
  if(node?.type==='middle_var_assign'){
    if(cache.has(nodeId)){
      return cache.get(nodeId);
    }
    const bucket=modeKey==='reference'?SIM.reference:SIM.actual;
    const nodeState=ensureNodeRuntime(bucket,node);
    const value=readMiddleAssignmentValue(node,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting);
    nodeState.lastAssignedValue=value;
    const resolved={outputs:[value],middleValues:[]};
    cache.set(nodeId,resolved);
    return resolved;
  }
  if(node?.type==='subsystem_block'){
    if(cache.has(nodeId)){
      return cache.get(nodeId);
    }
    const bucket=modeKey==='reference'?SIM.reference:SIM.actual;
    const nodeState=ensureNodeRuntime(bucket,node);
    if(visiting.has(nodeId)){
      return {
        outputs:nodeState.lastOutputs?.length?nodeState.lastOutputs:[nodeState.lastOutput||0],
        middleValues:nodeState.lastMiddleValues||[]
      };
    }
    visiting.add(nodeId);
    const inputValues=resolveNodeInputValues(node,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting);
    const resolved=finalizeResolvedNodeOutputs(
      node,
      nodeState,
      inputValues,
      evaluateSubsystemOutputsFromInputs(node,inputValues,modeKey,time,dt)
    );
    visiting.delete(nodeId);
    cache.set(nodeId,resolved);
    return resolved;
  }
  if(node?.type==='simulation_block'&&isPythonBoundFlowBlock(node)){
    if(cache.has(nodeId)){
      return cache.get(nodeId);
    }
    const bucket=modeKey==='reference'?SIM.reference:SIM.actual;
    const nodeState=ensureNodeRuntime(bucket,node);
    if(visiting.has(nodeId)){
      return {
        outputs:nodeState.lastOutputs?.length?nodeState.lastOutputs:[nodeState.lastOutput||0],
        middleValues:nodeState.lastMiddleValues||[]
      };
    }
    visiting.add(nodeId);
    const inputValues=resolveNodeInputValues(node,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting);
    const resolved=finalizeResolvedNodeOutputs(
      node,
      nodeState,
      inputValues,
      applyAssignedMiddleValues(node,nodeState,executeBoundFlowBlock(node,nodeState,inputValues,modeKey,time,dt))
    );
    visiting.delete(nodeId);
    cache.set(nodeId,resolved);
    return resolved;
  }
  const resolved=__legacyResolveNodeOutputsClean(nodeId,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting);
  if(node?.type==='simulation_block'&&isPythonBoundFlowBlock(node)){
    const bucket=modeKey==='reference'?SIM.reference:SIM.actual;
    return applyAssignedMiddleValues(node,ensureNodeRuntime(bucket,node),resolved);
  }
  return resolved;
};

function getNodeFromCanvas(canvasId,nodeId){
  return getCanvasRecord(canvasId)?.nodes?.find(node=>node.id===nodeId)||null;
}

function getIncomingEdgesForNodeFromCanvas(canvasId,nodeId){
  return (getCanvasRecord(canvasId)?.edges||[])
    .filter(edge=>edge.targetNodeId===nodeId)
    .sort((a,b)=>(a.targetPortIndex||0)-(b.targetPortIndex||0)||a.id.localeCompare(b.id));
}

function findCanvasIdForNodeId(nodeId,preferredCanvasId=''){
  if(preferredCanvasId&&getNodeFromCanvas(preferredCanvasId,nodeId)){
    return preferredCanvasId;
  }
  return Object.keys(S.canvases||{}).find(canvasId=>getNodeFromCanvas(canvasId,nodeId))||'';
}

function getCanvasTargetNodeForMiddleAssignment(node,canvasId){
  const targetNode=getNodeFromCanvas(canvasId,node?.props?.targetNodeId||'');
  if(!targetNode||targetNode.type!=='simulation_block'){
    return null;
  }
  const defs=getSimulationMiddleVarDefinitions(targetNode);
  const targetVar=defs.find(item=>item.name===node.props.targetVarName)||defs[0]||null;
  if(!targetVar){
    return null;
  }
  return {targetNode,targetVar};
}

function resetAssignedMiddleValuesBucket(bucket){
  Object.values(bucket?.nodeStates||{}).forEach(nodeState=>{
    if(nodeState&&nodeState.assignedMiddleValues){
      nodeState.assignedMiddleValues={};
    }
  });
}

function resolveNodeInputValuesInCanvas(node,canvasId,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting){
  const inputPorts=getNodePorts(node).inputs;
  if(!inputPorts.length){
    return [];
  }
  const incoming=getIncomingEdgesForNodeFromCanvas(canvasId,node.id);
  return inputPorts.map((_,portIndex)=>{
    const edge=incoming.find(item=>(item.targetPortIndex||0)===portIndex);
    if(!edge){
      return 0;
    }
    const upstream=resolveNodeOutputInCanvas(
      edge.sourceNodeId,
      canvasId,
      edge.sourcePortIndex||0,
      modeKey,
      time,
      dt,
      cache,
      visiting
    );
    return transmitEdgeSignal(edge,upstream,modeKey,time);
  });
}

function readMiddleAssignmentValueInCanvas(node,canvasId,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting){
  if(node.props.assignMode==='input'){
    const inputValues=resolveNodeInputValuesInCanvas(node,canvasId,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting);
    return sanitizeSignalValue(inputValues[0]??0);
  }
  return sanitizeSignalValue(parseScalar(node.props.constantValue,0));
}

function applyMiddleAssignmentsForCanvas(modeKey,canvasId,time,dt,cache,visiting){
  const bucket=modeKey==='reference'?SIM.reference:SIM.actual;
  (getCanvasRecord(canvasId)?.nodes||[])
    .filter(node=>node.type==='middle_var_assign')
    .forEach(node=>{
      const targetInfo=getCanvasTargetNodeForMiddleAssignment(node,canvasId);
      const nodeState=ensureNodeRuntime(bucket,node);
      if(!targetInfo){
        nodeState.lastAssignedValue=0;
        return;
      }
      const value=readMiddleAssignmentValueInCanvas(node,canvasId,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting);
      nodeState.lastAssignedValue=value;
      const targetState=ensureNodeRuntime(bucket,targetInfo.targetNode);
      if(!targetState.assignedMiddleValues){
        targetState.assignedMiddleValues={};
      }
      targetState.assignedMiddleValues[targetInfo.targetVar.name]=value;
    });
}

function applyMiddleAssignmentsForAllCanvases(modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting){
  Object.keys(S.canvases||{}).forEach(canvasId=>{
    applyMiddleAssignmentsForCanvas(modeKey,canvasId,time,dt,cache,visiting);
  });
}

function resolveSubsystemInputBoundary(node,canvasId,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting){
  const childCanvas=getCanvasRecord(canvasId);
  const parentNodeId=childCanvas?.parentSubsystemNodeId||'';
  const parentCanvasId=findCanvasIdForNodeId(parentNodeId,S.rootCanvasId);
  const parentNode=getNodeFromCanvas(parentCanvasId,parentNodeId);
  if(!parentNode){
    return {outputs:[0],middleValues:[]};
  }
  const intf=ensureSubsystemInterface(parentNode);
  const inputIndex=intf.inputs.findIndex(item=>item.id===node.props?.interfacePortId);
  if(inputIndex<0){
    return {outputs:[0],middleValues:[]};
  }
  const parentInputValues=resolveNodeInputValuesInCanvas(parentNode,parentCanvasId,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting);
  return {outputs:[sanitizeSignalValue(parentInputValues[inputIndex]??0)],middleValues:[]};
}

function resolveSubsystemBlockOutputs(node,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting){
  const childCanvasId=node.targetCanvasId||ensureSubsystemCanvasNode(node)?.id||'';
  const intf=ensureSubsystemInterface(node);
  const outputs=intf.outputs.map(item=>{
    const boundaryNodeId=getSubsystemBoundaryNodeId(node.id,'output',item.id);
    return resolveNodeOutputInCanvas(boundaryNodeId,childCanvasId,0,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting);
  });
  return {outputs:outputs.length?outputs:[0],middleValues:[]};
}

function resolveNodeOutputsInCanvas(nodeId,canvasId,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting){
  if(cache.has(nodeId)){
    return cache.get(nodeId);
  }
  const effectiveCanvasId=findCanvasIdForNodeId(nodeId,canvasId);
  const node=getNodeFromCanvas(effectiveCanvasId,nodeId);
  if(!node){
    return {outputs:[0],middleValues:[]};
  }
  const bucket=modeKey==='reference'?SIM.reference:SIM.actual;
  const nodeState=ensureNodeRuntime(bucket,node);
  if(visiting.has(nodeId)){
    return {
      outputs:nodeState.lastOutputs?.length?nodeState.lastOutputs:[nodeState.lastOutput||0],
      middleValues:nodeState.lastMiddleValues||[]
    };
  }
  visiting.add(nodeId);

  if(node.type==='middle_var_assign'){
    const value=readMiddleAssignmentValueInCanvas(node,effectiveCanvasId,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting);
    nodeState.lastAssignedValue=value;
    const resolved={outputs:[value],middleValues:[]};
    cache.set(nodeId,resolved);
    visiting.delete(nodeId);
    return resolved;
  }

  const inputValues=resolveNodeInputValuesInCanvas(node,effectiveCanvasId,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting);
  let resolved={outputs:[0],middleValues:[]};

  if(node.type==='signal_source'){
    resolved={outputs:[computeSourceSignal(node,time)],middleValues:[]};
  }else if(node.type==='subsystem_block'){
    resolved=resolveSubsystemBlockOutputs(node,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting);
  }else if(node.type==='subsystem_in_port'){
    resolved=resolveSubsystemInputBoundary(node,effectiveCanvasId,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting);
  }else if(node.type==='flow_block'){
    resolved={outputs:[sanitizeSignalValue(inputValues[0]||0)],middleValues:[]};
  }else if(node.type==='simulation_block'){
    resolved=isPythonBoundFlowBlock(node)
      ?applyAssignedMiddleValues(node,nodeState,executeBoundFlowBlock(node,nodeState,inputValues,modeKey,time,dt))
      :buildSimulationResult(node,nodeState,inputValues,modeKey,time,dt);
  }else if(node.type.startsWith('fault_')){
    resolved={outputs:[applyPhysicalFaultNode(node,sanitizeSignalValue(inputValues[0]||0),time,modeKey)],middleValues:[]};
  }else{
    resolved={outputs:[sanitizeSignalValue(inputValues[0]||0)],middleValues:[]};
  }

  resolved.outputs=(resolved.outputs||[0]).map(sanitizeSignalValue);
  resolved.middleValues=(resolved.middleValues||[]).map(sanitizeSignalValue);
  nodeState.lastInputValues=inputValues.slice();
  nodeState.lastInput=inputValues[0]||0;
  nodeState.lastOutputs=resolved.outputs.slice();
  nodeState.lastMiddleValues=resolved.middleValues.slice();
  nodeState.lastOutput=nodeState.lastOutputs[0]||0;
  visiting.delete(nodeId);
  cache.set(nodeId,resolved);
  return resolved;
}

function resolveNodeOutputInCanvas(nodeId,canvasId,outputIndex,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting){
  const effectiveCanvasId=findCanvasIdForNodeId(nodeId,canvasId);
  const node=getNodeFromCanvas(effectiveCanvasId,nodeId);
  const resolved=resolveNodeOutputsInCanvas(nodeId,effectiveCanvasId,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting);
  if(!node){
    return 0;
  }
  if(node.type==='simulation_block'){
    const mainCount=isPythonBoundFlowBlock(node)
      ?(node.pythonBinding?.portMapping?.outputs?.length||0)
      :(normalizeSimulationInterfaces(node.props),node.props.outputs.length);
    if(outputIndex<mainCount){
      return sanitizeSignalValue(resolved.outputs[outputIndex]??resolved.outputs[0]??0);
    }
    return sanitizeSignalValue(resolved.middleValues[outputIndex-mainCount]??resolved.outputs[0]??0);
  }
  return sanitizeSignalValue(resolved.outputs[outputIndex]??resolved.outputs[0]??0);
}

resolveNodeOutputs = function(nodeId,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting){
  return resolveNodeOutputsInCanvas(nodeId,findCanvasIdForNodeId(nodeId,S.activeCanvasId),modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting);
};

resolveNodeOutput = function(nodeId,outputIndex,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting){
  return resolveNodeOutputInCanvas(nodeId,findCanvasIdForNodeId(nodeId,S.activeCanvasId),outputIndex,modeKey,time,dt,cache,visiting);
};

recordScopeSamples = function(time,dt){
  const actualCache=new Map();
  const referenceCache=new Map();
  const actualVisiting=new Set();
  const referenceVisiting=new Set();
  resetAssignedMiddleValuesBucket(SIM.actual);
  resetAssignedMiddleValuesBucket(SIM.reference);
  applyMiddleAssignmentsForAllCanvases('actual',time,dt,actualCache,actualVisiting);
  applyMiddleAssignmentsForAllCanvases('reference',time,dt,referenceCache,referenceVisiting);
  getScopeNodes().forEach(scopeNode=>{
    const actualValue=resolveNodeSignal(scopeNode.id,'actual',time,dt,actualCache,actualVisiting);
    const referenceValue=resolveNodeSignal(scopeNode.id,'reference',time,dt,referenceCache,referenceVisiting);
    pushLimitedSample(SIM.actual.scopeSamples[scopeNode.id],{t:time,v:actualValue});
    pushLimitedSample(SIM.reference.scopeSamples[scopeNode.id],{t:time,v:referenceValue});
  });
};

const __legacyOscilloscopeGetNodePorts = getNodePorts;

getNodePorts = function(node){
  if(node?.type==='instrument_scope'){
    return {
      inputs:[
        {key:'ch1',label:'CH1',kind:'input',side:'left'},
        {key:'ch2',label:'CH2',kind:'input',side:'left'}
      ],
      outputs:[]
    };
  }
  return __legacyOscilloscopeGetNodePorts(node);
};

  __legacyOscilloscopeRenderModelNodes();
  renderScopeWindows();
};

    toast('当前没有可打开的示波器模块','w');
    return;
  }
  focusScopeWindow(SIM.activeScopeId);
  renderScopeWindows();
};

  if(!SIM.activeScopeId){return;}
  focusScopeWindow(SIM.activeScopeId);
  renderScopeWindows();
};

  if(status){return status;}
  status=document.createElement('div');
  status.id='model-package-status';
  status.className='props-help';
  const panel=document.getElementById('pd');
  if(panel){
    panel.appendChild(status);
  }else{
    document.body.appendChild(status);
  }
  return status;
}

  const status=ensureModelPackageStatusElement();
  const panel=document.getElementById('pd');
  if(panel&&status.parentElement!==panel){
    panel.appendChild(status);

  status.textContent=`当前模型包：${meta.packageName} · 执行模式：${meta.executionMode}`;
}

const __task5ApplyFlightModelPackage = window.__GZ_APPLY_FLIGHT_MODEL_PACKAGE__;
window.__GZ_APPLY_FLIGHT_MODEL_PACKAGE__ = function(pkg,prepared){

  restoreSystemModelSnapshot(restored);
  S.availableFaultModels=cloneDefaults(prepared?.faultLibrary||pkg?.faultLibrary||[]);

function ensureScopeChannelBucket(bucket,scopeId){
  const current=bucket.scopeSamples[scopeId];
  if(!current||Array.isArray(current)){
    bucket.scopeSamples[scopeId]={ch1:[],ch2:[]};
  }else{
    current.ch1=current.ch1||[];
    current.ch2=current.ch2||[];
  }
  return bucket.scopeSamples[scopeId];
}

function getScopeChannelKey(portIndex=0){
  return Number(portIndex)===1?'ch2':'ch1';
}

function getSampleValue(sample){
  if(sample&&Number.isFinite(sample.actual)){return sample.actual;}
  if(sample&&Number.isFinite(sample.v)){return sample.v;}
  return 0;
}

function formatScopeMetric(value){
  const numeric=Number(value);
  return Number.isFinite(numeric)?numeric.toFixed(2):'--';
}

function summarizeScopeChannel(samples){
  if(!samples?.length){
    return {connected:false,current:'--',min:'--',max:'--',pp:'--'};
  }
  const values=samples.map(getSampleValue);
  const min=Math.min(...values);
  const max=Math.max(...values);
  return {
    connected:true,
    current:formatScopeMetric(values.at(-1)),
    min:formatScopeMetric(min),
    max:formatScopeMetric(max),
    pp:formatScopeMetric(max-min)
  };
}

function getScopeChannelSignalName(scopeNode,channelKey){
  const targetPortIndex=channelKey==='ch2'?1:0;
  const incoming=getIncomingEdgesForNode(scopeNode.id).find(edge=>(edge.targetPortIndex||0)===targetPortIndex);
  if(!incoming){return '未连接';}
  const sourceNode=getNode(incoming.sourceNodeId);
  if(!sourceNode){return '未知信号';}
  const outputPort=getNodePorts(sourceNode).outputs[incoming.sourcePortIndex||0];
  return outputPort
    ?`${sourceNode.props?.name||'信号'} · ${outputPort.label}`
    :(sourceNode.props?.name||'信号');
}

function prepareScopeCanvas(canvas){
  const ratio=window.devicePixelRatio||1;
  const rect=canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
  const width=Math.max(Math.round(rect.width||canvas.clientWidth||300),1);
  const height=Math.max(Math.round(rect.height||canvas.clientHeight||150),1);
  canvas.width=width*ratio;
  canvas.height=height*ratio;
  const ctx=canvas.getContext('2d');
  if(ctx?.setTransform){
    ctx.setTransform(ratio,0,0,ratio,0,0);
  }
  return {ctx,width,height};
}

function drawScopeTrace(ctx,series,color,getX,getY){
  if(!ctx||!series.length){return;}
  ctx.strokeStyle=color;
  ctx.lineWidth=1.5;
  ctx.beginPath();
  series.forEach((sample,index)=>{
    const x=getX(sample.t,index,series.length);
    const y=getY(getSampleValue(sample));
    if(index===0){ctx.moveTo(x,y);}else{ctx.lineTo(x,y);}
  });
  ctx.stroke();
}

function drawScopeWindow(scopeId){
  const scopeEl=document.querySelector(`.scope-window[data-scope-id="${scopeId}"]`);
  if(!scopeEl){return;}
  const canvas=scopeEl.querySelector('[data-scope-role="wave-canvas"]');
  if(!canvas){return;}
  const {ctx,width,height}=prepareScopeCanvas(canvas);
  if(!ctx){return;}
  const scopeWindow=ensureScopeWindow(scopeId);
  const samples=ensureScopeChannelBucket(SIM.actual,scopeId);
  const ch1Series=samples.ch1.slice(-240);
  const ch2Series=samples.ch2.slice(-240);
  const visibleSeries=scopeWindow.mode==='ch1'
    ?ch1Series
    :scopeWindow.mode==='ch2'
      ?ch2Series
      :ch1Series.concat(ch2Series);
  if(!visibleSeries.length){
    drawScopeEmpty(ctx,width,height,'连接 CH1 或 CH2 后开始仿真');
    return;
  }
  drawScopeGrid(ctx,width,height);
  const values=visibleSeries.map(getSampleValue);
  let minValue=Math.min(...values);
  let maxValue=Math.max(...values);
  if(Math.abs(maxValue-minValue)<1e-6){
    maxValue+=1;
    minValue-=1;
  }else{
    const padding=(maxValue-minValue)*0.18;
    maxValue+=padding;
    minValue-=padding;
  }
  const startTime=Math.min(...visibleSeries.map(sample=>sample.t||0));
  const endTime=Math.max(...visibleSeries.map(sample=>sample.t||0),startTime+SIM.stepSize);
  const span=Math.max(endTime-startTime,SIM.stepSize,0.001);
  const getX=time=>18+((time-startTime)/span)*(width-36);
  const getY=value=>14+(maxValue-value)/(maxValue-minValue)*(height-28);
  const zeroY=getY(0);
  if(zeroY>=10&&zeroY<=height-10){
    ctx.strokeStyle='#c2d6ea';
    ctx.lineWidth=1;
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(0,zeroY);
    ctx.lineTo(width,zeroY);
    ctx.stroke();
  }
  if(scopeWindow.mode!=='ch2'){
    drawScopeTrace(ctx,ch1Series,'#1d6fbf',getX,getY);
  }
  if(scopeWindow.mode!=='ch1'){
    drawScopeTrace(ctx,ch2Series,'#16a34a',getX,getY);
  }
  ctx.fillStyle='#7a9ab8';
  ctx.font='10px JetBrains Mono,monospace';
  ctx.fillText(`${startTime.toFixed(1)}s`,6,height-6);
  ctx.fillText(`${endTime.toFixed(1)}s`,Math.max(width-44,6),height-6);
}

function setScopeDisplayMode(scopeId,mode){
  const scopeWindow=ensureScopeWindow(scopeId);
  scopeWindow.mode=mode;
  renderScopeWindows();
}

function startScopeWindowDrag(event,scopeId){
  const scopeWindow=ensureScopeWindow(scopeId);
  focusScopeWindow(scopeId);
  SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG.active=true;
  SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG.engaged=false;
  SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG.pointerId=Number.isFinite(Number(event.pointerId))?Number(event.pointerId):null;
  SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG.scopeId=scopeId;
  SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG.startX=event.clientX;
  SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG.startY=event.clientY;
  SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG.originX=scopeWindow.x;
  SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG.originY=scopeWindow.y;
  if(event.stopPropagation){event.stopPropagation();}
  if(event.preventDefault){event.preventDefault();}
}

function bindScopeWindowDragListeners(){
  if(window.__GZ_SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG_BOUND__){return;}
  window.__GZ_SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG_BOUND__=true;
  const runtimeListeners=getRuntimeListenerStore();
  runtimeListeners.scopeWindowDragPointerMove=event=>{
    if(!SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG.active){return;}
    if(SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG.pointerId!==null&&event.pointerId!==SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG.pointerId){return;}
    const scopeWindow=SIM.scopeWindows?.[SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG.scopeId];
    if(!scopeWindow){return;}
    if(!SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG.engaged){
      if(!movedBeyondPointerThreshold(SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG.startX,SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG.startY,event.clientX,event.clientY)){return;}
      SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG.engaged=true;
    }
    if(!scopeWindow){return;}
    scopeWindow.x=Math.round(SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG.originX+(event.clientX-SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG.startX));
    scopeWindow.y=Math.round(SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG.originY+(event.clientY-SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG.startY));
    clampScopeWindowPosition(scopeWindow);
    renderScopeWindows();
  };
  runtimeListeners.scopeWindowDragPointerUp=event=>{
    if(!SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG.active){return;}
    if(SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG.pointerId!==null&&event.pointerId!==SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG.pointerId){return;}
    SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG.active=false;
    SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG.engaged=false;
    SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG.pointerId=null;
    SCOPE_WINDOW_DRAG.scopeId='';
  };
  window.addEventListener('pointermove',runtimeListeners.scopeWindowDragPointerMove);
  window.addEventListener('pointerup',runtimeListeners.scopeWindowDragPointerUp);
  window.addEventListener('mousemove',runtimeListeners.scopeWindowDragPointerMove);
  window.addEventListener('mouseup',runtimeListeners.scopeWindowDragPointerUp);
  document.addEventListener('pointermove',runtimeListeners.scopeWindowDragPointerMove);
  document.addEventListener('pointerup',runtimeListeners.scopeWindowDragPointerUp);
  document.addEventListener('mousemove',runtimeListeners.scopeWindowDragPointerMove);
  document.addEventListener('mouseup',runtimeListeners.scopeWindowDragPointerUp);
}

const __dualScopeRecordScopeSamples = recordScopeSamples;
const __dualScopeGetNodePorts = getNodePorts;
const __dualScopeRenderModelNodes = renderModelNodes;
const __dualScopeRunSimulationTick = runSimulationTick;

recordScopeSamples = function(time,dt){
  const actualCache=new Map();
  const referenceCache=new Map();
  const actualVisiting=new Set();
  const referenceVisiting=new Set();
  clearAssignedMiddleValues(SIM.actual);
  clearAssignedMiddleValues(SIM.reference);
  applyMiddleAssignmentsForMode('actual',time,dt,actualCache,actualVisiting);
  applyMiddleAssignmentsForMode('reference',time,dt,referenceCache,referenceVisiting);
  getScopeNodes().forEach(scopeNode=>{
    const actualBucket=ensureScopeChannelBucket(SIM.actual,scopeNode.id);
    const referenceBucket=ensureScopeChannelBucket(SIM.reference,scopeNode.id);
    getIncomingEdgesForNode(scopeNode.id).forEach(edge=>{
      const channelKey=getScopeChannelKey(edge.targetPortIndex||0);
      const actualValue=resolveNodeOutput(edge.sourceNodeId,edge.sourcePortIndex||0,'actual',time,dt,actualCache,actualVisiting);
      const referenceValue=resolveNodeOutput(edge.sourceNodeId,edge.sourcePortIndex||0,'reference',time,dt,referenceCache,referenceVisiting);
      pushLimitedSample(actualBucket[channelKey],{t:time,actual:actualValue});
      pushLimitedSample(referenceBucket[channelKey],{t:time,actual:referenceValue});
    });
  });
  getAuxInstrumentNodes().forEach(instrumentNode=>{
    const incoming=getIncomingEdgesForNode(instrumentNode.id)[0];
    if(!incoming){return;}
    if(!SIM.actual.instrumentSamples){SIM.actual.instrumentSamples={};}
    if(!SIM.reference.instrumentSamples){SIM.reference.instrumentSamples={};}
    if(!Array.isArray(SIM.actual.instrumentSamples[instrumentNode.id])){
      SIM.actual.instrumentSamples[instrumentNode.id]=[];
    }
    if(!Array.isArray(SIM.reference.instrumentSamples[instrumentNode.id])){
      SIM.reference.instrumentSamples[instrumentNode.id]=[];
    }
    const actualValue=resolveNodeOutput(incoming.sourceNodeId,incoming.sourcePortIndex||0,'actual',time,dt,actualCache,actualVisiting);
    const referenceValue=resolveNodeOutput(incoming.sourceNodeId,incoming.sourcePortIndex||0,'reference',time,dt,referenceCache,referenceVisiting);
    pushLimitedSample(SIM.actual.instrumentSamples[instrumentNode.id],{t:time,actual:actualValue,reference:referenceValue});
    pushLimitedSample(SIM.reference.instrumentSamples[instrumentNode.id],{t:time,actual:referenceValue,reference:referenceValue});
  });
};

getNodePorts = function(node){
  if(node?.type==='instrument_scope'){
    return {
      inputs:[
        {key:'ch1',label:'CH1',kind:'input',side:'left'},
        {key:'ch2',label:'CH2',kind:'input',side:'left'}
      ],
      outputs:[]
    };
  }
  return __dualScopeGetNodePorts(node);
};

renderScopeWindows = function(){
  const host=document.getElementById('scope-window-layer');
  if(!host){return;}
  bindScopeWindowDragListeners();
  host.innerHTML=listOpenScopeWindows()
    .sort((left,right)=>left.z-right.z)
    .map(scopeWindow=>{
      clampScopeWindowPosition(scopeWindow);
      const node=getNode(scopeWindow.scopeId);
      const bucket=ensureScopeChannelBucket(SIM.actual,scopeWindow.scopeId);
      const ch1=summarizeScopeChannel(bucket.ch1);
      const ch2=summarizeScopeChannel(bucket.ch2);
      const ch1Metrics={
        current:formatScopeMetric(ch1.current),
        min:formatScopeMetric(ch1.min),
        max:formatScopeMetric(ch1.max),
        pp:formatScopeMetric(ch1.pp)
      };
      const ch2Metrics={
        current:formatScopeMetric(ch2.current),
        min:formatScopeMetric(ch2.min),
        max:formatScopeMetric(ch2.max),
        pp:formatScopeMetric(ch2.pp)
      };
      const ch1Signal=getScopeChannelSignalName(node,'ch1');
      const ch2Signal=getScopeChannelSignalName(node,'ch2');
      const ch1TagLabel=`CH1: ${ch1Signal}`;
      const ch2TagLabel=`CH2: ${ch2Signal}`;
      const mode=scopeWindow.mode||'overlay';
      return `
        <section class="scope-window" data-scope-id="${scopeWindow.scopeId}" style="left:${scopeWindow.x}px;top:${scopeWindow.y}px;z-index:${scopeWindow.z}">
          <header class="scope-window__header" data-scope-drag-handle="${scopeWindow.scopeId}">
            <div class="scope-window__header-main">
              <div class="scope-window__identity">
                <div class="scope-window__title">${escapeHtml(node?.props?.name||node?.name||'示波器')}</div>
              </div>
              <div class="scope-window__toolbar">
                <button type="button" class="scope-window__mode${mode==='overlay'?' is-active':''}" data-scope-mode="overlay" data-scope-id="${scopeWindow.scopeId}">叠加</button>
                <button type="button" class="scope-window__mode${mode==='ch1'?' is-active':''}" data-scope-mode="ch1" data-scope-id="${scopeWindow.scopeId}">CH1</button>
                <button type="button" class="scope-window__mode${mode==='ch2'?' is-active':''}" data-scope-mode="ch2" data-scope-id="${scopeWindow.scopeId}">CH2</button>
                <button type="button" class="scope-window__close" data-scope-close="${scopeWindow.scopeId}">关闭 ×</button>
              </div>
            </div>
          </header>
          <div class="scope-window__signal-band">
            <div class="scope-window__signals">
              <span class="scope-window__tag" data-scope-tag="ch1" data-connected="${ch1.connected}" title="${escapeHtml(ch1TagLabel)}">
                <span class="scope-window__tag-prefix">CH1:</span>
                <span class="scope-window__tag-text">${escapeHtml(ch1Signal)}</span>
              </span>
              <span class="scope-window__tag" data-scope-tag="ch2" data-connected="${ch2.connected}" title="${escapeHtml(ch2TagLabel)}">
                <span class="scope-window__tag-prefix">CH2:</span>
                <span class="scope-window__tag-text">${escapeHtml(ch2Signal)}</span>
              </span>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div class="scope-window__plot">
            <canvas data-scope-role="wave-canvas"></canvas>
          </div>
          <div class="scope-window__stats scope-window__stats--strip">
            <article class="scope-readout scope-readout--strip" data-scope-channel="ch1" data-connected="${ch1.connected}">
              <div class="scope-readout__title">CH1</div>
              <div class="scope-readout__metric"><span class="scope-readout__metric-label">当前</span><strong class="scope-readout__metric-value" data-field="current">${ch1Metrics.current}</strong></div>
              <div class="scope-readout__metric"><span class="scope-readout__metric-label">最小</span><strong class="scope-readout__metric-value" data-field="min">${ch1Metrics.min}</strong></div>
              <div class="scope-readout__metric"><span class="scope-readout__metric-label">最大</span><strong class="scope-readout__metric-value" data-field="max">${ch1Metrics.max}</strong></div>
              <div class="scope-readout__metric"><span class="scope-readout__metric-label">峰峰</span><strong class="scope-readout__metric-value" data-field="pp">${ch1Metrics.pp}</strong></div>
            </article>
            <article class="scope-readout scope-readout--strip" data-scope-channel="ch2" data-connected="${ch2.connected}">
              <div class="scope-readout__title">CH2</div>
              <div class="scope-readout__metric"><span class="scope-readout__metric-label">当前</span><strong class="scope-readout__metric-value" data-field="current">${ch2Metrics.current}</strong></div>
              <div class="scope-readout__metric"><span class="scope-readout__metric-label">最小</span><strong class="scope-readout__metric-value" data-field="min">${ch2Metrics.min}</strong></div>
              <div class="scope-readout__metric"><span class="scope-readout__metric-label">最大</span><strong class="scope-readout__metric-value" data-field="max">${ch2Metrics.max}</strong></div>
              <div class="scope-readout__metric"><span class="scope-readout__metric-label">峰峰</span><strong class="scope-readout__metric-value" data-field="pp">${ch2Metrics.pp}</strong></div>
            </article>
          </div>
        </section>`;
    })
    .join('');
  host.querySelectorAll('.scope-window').forEach(el=>{
    el.addEventListener('pointerdown',event=>{
      if(event.target.closest('[data-scope-close],[data-scope-mode],[data-scope-drag-handle]')){return;}
      const scopeWindow=focusScopeWindow(el.dataset.scopeId||'');
      el.style.zIndex=scopeWindow.z;
    });
  });
  host.querySelectorAll('[data-scope-drag-handle]').forEach(header=>{
    header.addEventListener('pointerdown',event=>{
      startScopeWindowDrag(event,header.dataset.scopeDragHandle||'');
    });
  });
  host.querySelectorAll('[data-scope-close]').forEach(btn=>{
    btn.addEventListener('click',event=>{
      event.stopPropagation();
      closeScopeWindow(btn.dataset.scopeClose||'');
    });
  });
  host.querySelectorAll('[data-scope-mode]').forEach(btn=>{
    btn.addEventListener('click',event=>{
      event.stopPropagation();
      setScopeDisplayMode(btn.dataset.scopeId||'',btn.dataset.scopeMode||'overlay');
    });
  });
  listOpenScopeWindows().forEach(scopeWindow=>drawScopeWindow(scopeWindow.scopeId));
};

renderModelNodes = function(){
  __dualScopeRenderModelNodes();
  renderCanvasBreadcrumbs();
  S.modelNodes.forEach(node=>{
    if(node.type!=='subsystem_block'){return;}
    ensureSubsystemCanvasNode(node);
    const el=document.getElementById('b-' + node.id);
    if(!el){return;}
    const kicker=el.querySelector('.blk-kicker');
    const sub=el.querySelector('.blk-sub');
    el.title='双击进入子画布';
    if(kicker){kicker.textContent='子系统';}
    if(sub){sub.textContent=node.targetCanvasId?'双击进入子画布':'子画布未创建';}
    if(el.dataset.subsystemNavBound!=='1'){
      el.dataset.subsystemNavBound='1';
      el.addEventListener('dblclick',event=>{
        event.stopPropagation();
        openSubsystemCanvas(node.id);
      });
    }
  });
  renderScopeWindows();
};

runSimulationTick = function(){
  const completed=__dualScopeRunSimulationTick();
  if(listOpenScopeWindows().length){
    renderScopeWindows();
  }
  return completed;
};

openScope = function(scopeId=''){
  ensureScopeSelection(scopeId||S.selBlk);
  if(!SIM.activeScopeId){
    toast('当前没有可打开的示波器模块','w');
    return;
  }
  focusScopeWindow(SIM.activeScopeId);
  renderScopeWindows();
};

focusScopeLatest = function(){
  if(!SIM.activeScopeId){return;}
  focusScopeWindow(SIM.activeScopeId);
  renderScopeWindows();
};

togCmp = function(){
  S.cmpMode=!S.cmpMode;
  const scopeId=SIM.activeScopeId||getScopeNodes()[0]?.id||'';
  if(scopeId){
    setScopeDisplayMode(scopeId,S.cmpMode?'overlay':'ch1');
  }
};

const __task3BuildNodeSubtitle = buildNodeSubtitle;
buildNodeSubtitle = function(node){
  if(!node){return '';}
  const props=node.props||{};
  const faultNote=node.injectedFault?' · 电气故障':'';
  switch(node.type){
    case 'signal_source':
      return `${props.waveType||'信号'} · 幅值 ${props.amplitude||'1'} · ${props.outputFormat||'标量'}`;
    case 'flow_block':
      return `${props.inputName||'输入'} / ${props.inputFormat||'标量'} → ${props.outputName||'输出'} / ${props.outputFormat||'标量'}${faultNote}`;
    case 'simulation_block':
      normalizeSimulationInterfaces(props);
      return `${props.inputs.length}输入 · ${props.outputs.length}输出 · ${props.middleVars.length}中间变量 · ${props.moduleType||'函数块'}${faultNote}`;
    case 'subsystem_block':{
      const intf=ensureSubsystemInterface(node);
      return `${intf.inputs.length} 输入 · ${intf.outputs.length} 输出 · 双击进入子画布`;
    }
    case 'subsystem_in_port':
      return `父层输入映射 · ${props.portType||'标量'}`;
    case 'subsystem_out_port':
      return `父层输出映射 · ${props.portType||'标量'}`;
    case 'instrument_scope':
      return `${props.instrumentType||'波形监测'} · 双击查看波形`;
    case 'instrument_spectrum':
    case 'instrument_logger':
      return `${props.instrumentType||'仪器'} · ${props.sampleRate||'-'}`;
    case 'link_normal':
    case 'link_can':
      return `${props.sourcePort||'源端口'} → ${props.targetPort||'目标端口'}`;
    default:
      return __task3BuildNodeSubtitle(node);
  }
};

const __task3GetNodePorts = getNodePorts;
getNodePorts = function(node){
  if(node?.type==='subsystem_block'){
    const intf=ensureSubsystemInterface(node);
    return {
      inputs:intf.inputs.map((item,index)=>({
        key:`subsystem-input-${item.id}`,
        label:item.name,
        kind:'input',
        side:'left',
        meta:item,
        index
      })),
      outputs:intf.outputs.map((item,index)=>({
        key:`subsystem-output-${item.id}`,
        label:item.name,
        kind:'output',
        side:'right',
        meta:item,
        index
      }))
    };
  }
  if(node?.type==='subsystem_in_port'){
    return {
      inputs:[],
      outputs:[{
        key:`boundary-out-${node.props?.interfacePortId||node.id}`,
        label:node.props?.name||'子系统输入',
        kind:'output',
        side:'right'
      }]
    };
  }
  if(node?.type==='subsystem_out_port'){
    return {
      inputs:[{
        key:`boundary-in-${node.props?.interfacePortId||node.id}`,
        label:node.props?.name||'子系统输出',
        kind:'input',
        side:'left'
      }],
      outputs:[]
    };
  }
